# Welcome to SEO Utils | SEO Utils

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/#overview)

Overview

SEO Utils is a desktop application that provides a set of essential tools and utilities for your SEO tasks, including Backlink Analytics, Traffic Analytics, Keyword Clustering, etc.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/#supported-platforms)

Supported Platforms

*   macOS High Sierra 10.13+ (Intel)
    
*   macOS Big Sur 11.0+ (Apple Silicon)
    
*   Windows 10/11 (AMD64)
    
*   Windows 10/11 (ARM64) (Working on)
    
*   Linux (Ubuntu 22.04 and above)
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/#features)

Features

Feature

Description

DataForSEO Required (\*)?

Backlinks Analytics

Provides detailed insights into the backlink profile of any website, including the number, quality, and sources of backlinks.

Yes

Traffic Analytics

Unleash your marketing potential! Uncover rivals' traffic stats, identify growth opportunities, organic keywords, and supercharge your strategy.

Yes

[Semantic Keyword Clustering](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering)

Do you often wonder if two keywords can be targeted together on a page or struggle with a large list of keywords that ChatGPT or other tools can't cluster due to token limits or cost? This tool resolves all those issues.

No

[SERP Clustering](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering)

Same as Semantic Clustering, but use SERP data to cluster keywords.

No (or Yes)

Sitemap Extractor

Extract all URLs from a sitemap

No

SERP Similarity

Quickly shows the overlap between two keywords, helping to decide if they can be targeted together on the same page.

Yes & No

SERP UULE

Check Google Search Results for different locations.

No

Keyword Explorer

Comprehensive solution for researching and analyzing keywords. It helps you discover relevant keywords, understand their search volume, competition level, and trends, and rank competitors on SERP.

Yes

Content Gap

Easily pull and bulk check all mentions of your keywords with a single click, helping you understand and enhance their ranking.

Yes

Bulk Analysis

Run backlink, traffic analysis on 1,000 URLs per time.

Yes

[Google Search Console Integration](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console)

Providing advanced features such as checking if a keyword appears in the title, headings, and body of a page.

No

Bulk Google PAA

Automatically extract information from the "People Also Ask" section by clicking through multiple layers for a large number of keywords all at once.

No

Bulk Bing/Google Autocomplete

Extract all keywords from Google/Bing Autocomplete with many keyword modifiers.

No

[Auto Indexing](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool)

Use your personal Google Service Account to automatically submit many URLs for indexing.

No

[IndexNow](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow)

Automatically submit URLs to Bing, Yandex, Naver, Seznam.cz, and Yep.

No

[Bulk SEO Metadata Optimizer](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer)

Allows you to optimize **titles, meta descriptions, and H1 headings** across multiple pages using AI models (Cloud or Local). This tool is perfect for SEOs looking to save time while enhancing metadata for better search engine visibility and click-through rates.

No

[Content Struct](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct)

Scrapes all headings, metadata, and main content from the top 20 URLs on the SERP, and allows you to generate a content outline using either cloud-based AI or local AI models.

No

Backlink Gap

Compares your website's backlink profile with those of your competitors, identifying opportunities where you can build more backlinks to improve your site's search engine ranking.

Yes

[GMB Rank Tracker](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker)

This tool lets you track your Google Business profile's ranking on Google Maps search results for specific locations. It also provides insights about your competitors, helping you develop strategies to improve your ranking.

Yes & No

[N.A.P Finder](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/n.a.p-finder)

Automates citation tracking by scanning the web for variations of a business’s name, address, and phone number, making it easy to spot inconsistent or rogue listings.

Yes & No

Content Explorer (Coming soon)

Find the ideas for your content.

Yes

[Organic Rank Tracker](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/organic-rank-tracker)

Keep track of how keywords rank on desktop, mobile, and local search results. Also, include an analysis of competitor performance.

No (or Yes)

SERP Diff (Coming soon)

Keep an eye on the search engine results page (SERP) and get notified when there are changes or when differences are spotted between two dates.

No

[NLP Text Analysis](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis)

Extract key topics and entities from text or URLs, powered by Google NLP, TextRazor, and Dandelion, supporting 20+ languages.

No

[White-labeled Client Report](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report)

Create a white-labeled client report with your logo, domain, and optional password. Share the link so clients can view their ranking data.

No

[Log File Analysis](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/log-file-analysis)

Track and optimize for these AI bots, alongside traditional search engine crawlers like Googlebot and Bingbot.

No

[LLM Rank Tracker](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/llm-rank-tracker)

Monitor your brand’s visibility, sentiment, and citations in AI search results like Google AI Overview, AI Mode, ChatGPT. Track mentions, analyze competitors, and measure trends over time.

Yes

[SEO Tests](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests)

_Time-based, URL Switch, and Split Tests_ — to run controlled experiments and see the real impact of your changes with Google Search Console data.

No

[Automations](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations)

Automate actions when rank tracking completes. When an Organic Rank Tracker or Google Business Rank Tracker snapshot finishes, you can automatically export PDFs, send emails to clients, or trigger webhook URLs.

No

[Workspace](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace)

Organize and separate your projects, clients, or different SEO campaigns. Each workspace maintains its own set of data.

No

[Embedding Database](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database)

Convert text into mathematical representations (embeddings) that capture semantic meaning

No

(\*) You are required to use your own [DataForSEO account](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/seo-data-source)
 or [rent an API Key from SEO Utils](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key)
.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/#download-links-and-license-key)

Download Links & License Key

After you [purchase a license key](https://larseo.lemonsqueezy.com/checkout/buy/630311af-3d08-47e3-9e29-9531b7ea60e0)
, you will see the download app links for all platforms and the license key on the checkout page or in your email inbox.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/#app-updates)

App Updates

One license key allows you to use the current app version indefinitely. They are also eligible for one year of free updates.

If you don't want to renew the license after one year, you can continue to use the last version of the app that you have access to.

# SEO Data Source | SEO Utils

First, you need to know that, SEO Utils is just a desktop application that provides you with a set of SEO tools including Backlinks Analytics and traffic Analytics. SEO Utils doesn't have a backlinks or keyword database.

The main database is from DataForSEO.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/seo-data-source#what-is-dataforseo)

What is DataForSEO


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[DatForSEO](https://dataforseo.com/?aff=134458)
 is a solution that provides comprehensive SEO and digital marketing data via API. Currently, DataForSEO database has over 9 billion keywords (Google + Bing) and over 2.81 trillion backlinks

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fp6euyyK2UtPlYCc5u9Rj%252FXnapper-2023-11-18-13.49.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd4cac3e-9223-4364-b81d-786b373d0cc8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c83fb1aa&sv=2)

Source: [https://dataforseo.com/our-data](https://dataforseo.com/our-data/?aff=134458)

Ahrefs boasts the most extensive backlink database in the market, while SEMrush leads with the largest collection of keywords. DataForSEO stands out for its highly competitive pricing, complemented by a database that is equally formidable.

You **don't need a subscription**. With DataForSEO, you pay only for the individual services you consume. The **pay-as-you-go** pricing model is designed to help you minimize costs, increase resource efficiency, and build operational resilience.

If you're seeking a budget-friendly alternative to Ahrefs or SEMrush, this option is ideal. Even for those already using Ahrefs or SEMrush, adding an additional data source can significantly enhance your SEO insights. A rich keyword database helps in identifying trending topics, enabling you to create content that better resonates with your audience and aligns with their interests.

**Read more:** [Backlink APIs: An In-Depth Comparison of DataForSEO, Ahrefs, and Semrush](https://dataforseo.com/blog/backlink-api-comparison-dataforseo-ahrefs-semrush/?aff=134458)

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/seo-data-source#what-are-the-roles-of-seo-utils)

What Are the Roles of SEO Utils?

You might wonder why you need SEO Utils when you can directly access data from DataForSEO. The key difference is that DataForSEO only offers data through an API, without the user-friendly interface (UI) you see in tools like Ahrefs or SEMrush. So, if you don't have coding skills or are not familiar with using APIs, SEO Utils steps in to fill this gap.

Understanding the importance of data presentation, SEO Utils provides a smart and clean UI to help you interact with the data effectively.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FHqYQbRmcm2O2KD2bYdkx%252FCleanShot%25202023-11-18%2520at%252014.37.24%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4fc594f0-672b-4e41-81c4-79fd2af5f3c0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cf07f5f1&sv=2)

SEO Utils

Also, SEO Utils adds a cache layer to help you save costs when pulling data from DataForSEO.

For example, when you check a website's backlinks, SEO Utils saves the first page's data in the cache. If you go to the second page and then come back to the first, it uses the saved data instead of making another API request. This way, you don't end up pulling the same data twice for the same page or filters, saving both time and resources.

Besides Backlinks and Traffic Analytics, SEO Utils offers more handy tools. This includes [Keyword Clustering](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering)
 for grouping a million keywords, a Sitemap Extractor to easily understand website structure, and an AI Content Writer to help you create great content quickly and easily.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/seo-data-source#how-to-connect-your-dataforseo-account-to-seo-utils)

How to Connect Your DataForSEO Account to SEO Utils?

1.  First, you need to register a DataForSEO account at: [https://app.dataforseo.com/register](https://app.dataforseo.com/register/?aff=134458)
    

If you don't have a **business email**, please use this form for registration [https://dataforseo.com/registration-request](https://dataforseo.com/registration-request/?aff=134458)

1.  Visit [https://app.dataforseo.com/api-access](https://app.dataforseo.com/api-access)
     to grab your API login & API password
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fu4HhsKqY7MF2EVVVXNIG%252FXnapper-2023-11-18-14.31.30.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d534042-d988-41ca-9e53-36470dbd43bf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=505b6b42&sv=2)

API login and API password are **NOT** the username and password you use to log in to the DataForSEO dashboard.

1.  Open SEO Utils on your computer, and click on the App dropdown in the top-left of the app.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FRqtWXBCAFolcNHPlrBlL%252FXnapper-2023-11-18-14.33.14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63831c52-375c-46f8-b0f9-2531afa92d16&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=27f281ff&sv=2)

1.  Scroll down to the DatForSEO section, and enter your login + password.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Ft2e6enAXCwX09RpzzzKX%252FXnapper-2023-11-18-14.34.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54af22cd-0fa0-4357-a80e-23507fa21df0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=987b59f3&sv=2)

1.  Start using SEO Utils to pull backlinks, traffic, and keyword data.
    

**Your API credentials will be saved locally, nothing leaves your computer.**

# Workspace | SEO Utils

Workspaces in SEO Utils allow you to organize and separate your projects, clients, or different SEO campaigns. Each workspace maintains its own set of data, making it easy to manage multiple projects without mixing information.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#what-are-workspaces)

What are Workspaces?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Workspaces act as separate containers for your SEO data. When you switch between workspaces, you're essentially switching between different databases of:

*   [Organic Rank Tracker reports](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/organic-rank-tracker)
    
*   [GMB Rank Tracker reports](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker)
    
*   [LLM Rank Tracker reports](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/llm-rank-tracker)
    
*   [Content Structs](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct)
    
*   [Google Search Console properties](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console)
    
*   And many more...
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#default-workspace)

Default Workspace

Every SEO Utils installation comes with a **Default** that cannot be deleted. This ensures you always have at least one workspace to work with.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#managing-workspaces)

Managing Workspaces


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#accessing-workspaces)

Accessing Workspaces

You can access the workspace switcher from the sidebar. The current active workspace is displayed with its logo (if set) or a default icon.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FRDqNq5Mg7rEwXhH5Ow9S%252FXnapper-2025-08-14-23.05.36.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a8e2e7a-6540-4a1b-b917-85a34b4930f3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=726573d4&sv=2)

Workspace switcher in the sidebar

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#creating-a-new-workspace)

Creating a New Workspace

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#step-1)

Step 1

Click on the workspace switcher in the sidebar to open the dropdown menu.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#step-2)

Step 2

Click on the **"Add workspace"** button at the bottom of the dropdown.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#step-3)

Step 3

Enter a **name** for your workspace and optionally add a **logo URL** to help identify it visually.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F9pwyg5wl2XfI9KpwwGuC%252FXnapper-2025-08-14-23.09.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3154862-7452-4921-964f-423fb875f5d7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db856712&sv=2)

Create workspace modal

Click **"Create"** to create the workspace, or **"Create & Switch"** to create and immediately switch to the new workspace.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#editing-a-workspace)

Editing a Workspace

To edit an existing workspace:

1.  Open the workspace dropdown
    
2.  Hover over the workspace you want to edit
    
3.  Click the **pencil icon** that appears
    
4.  Update the name or logo URL
    
5.  Click **"Save"** to apply changes
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FbXZxIxbvSjdu9Y6l1gBb%252FCleanShot%25202025-08-14%2520at%252023.10.22%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debc851f9-b413-43ed-af00-0efdf488d3fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=75f71358&sv=2)

Edit workspace by clicking the pencil icon

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#deleting-a-workspace)

Deleting a Workspace

You can only delete workspaces that contain **no data**. If a workspace has any reports, tracked keywords, or other data, you must first delete or move that data before deleting the workspace.

To delete a workspace:

1.  Open the workspace dropdown
    
2.  Hover over the workspace you want to delete
    
3.  Click the **trash icon** that appears
    
4.  Confirm the deletion in the modal
    

The **Default Workspace** cannot be deleted.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#switching-between-workspaces)

Switching Between Workspaces


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#using-the-dropdown)

Using the Dropdown

Click on any workspace in the dropdown to switch to it. The app will reload with the selected workspace's data.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#using-keyboard-shortcuts)

Using Keyboard Shortcuts

You can quickly switch between workspaces using keyboard shortcuts:

*   **Mac**: `⌘1` through `⌘9`
    
*   **Windows/Linux**: `Ctrl+1` through `Ctrl+9`
    

The number corresponds to the workspace's position in your list. For example, `⌘1` switches to the first workspace, `⌘2` to the second, and so on.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#reordering-workspaces)

Reordering Workspaces

You can reorder workspaces to customize your keyboard shortcuts:

1.  Open the workspace dropdown
    
2.  Hover over a workspace to see the **drag handle** (grip icon)
    
3.  Click and drag the workspace to your desired position
    
4.  Release to save the new order
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FxgqhMjzK9pFEaZpB24Oi%252FCleanShot%25202025-08-14%2520at%252023.10.22%25202%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da04cce77-2bf0-4b14-9695-3e23207934b2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4838ef10&sv=2)

Drag workspaces to reorder them

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#moving-data-between-workspaces)

Moving Data Between Workspaces


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can move existing data from one workspace to another using the bulk move feature:

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#moving-multiple-records)

Moving Multiple Records

1.  Select the records you want to move (using checkboxes in any data table)
    
2.  Click on **"Bulk Actions"** button
    
3.  Select **"Move to Workspace"**
    
4.  Choose the target workspace from the dropdown
    
5.  Click **"Execute"** to move the selected records
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FnfISuT310rp95V112JcM%252FXnapper-2025-08-14-23.12.54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d6cf64c-8215-4afa-b42c-464413349a3b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=51b17e5f&sv=2)

Bulk move records to another workspace

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#use-cases-for-workspaces)

Use Cases for Workspaces


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#client-management)

Client Management

Create separate workspaces for each client to keep their SEO data isolated:

*   **Client A Workspace**: Contains all rank tracking, backlinks, and reports for Client A
    
*   **Client B Workspace**: Separate data for Client B
    
*   **Personal Projects**: Your own website's SEO data
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#project-organization)

Project Organization

Organize different projects or websites:

*   **E-commerce Site**: Track product page rankings and organic traffic
    
*   **Blog Network**: Monitor multiple blog sites
    
*   **Local Business**: Track Google Business rankings and local SEO
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#team-collaboration)

Team Collaboration

Different teams or departments can have their own workspaces:

*   **Content Team**: Focus on content analysis and optimization
    
*   **Link Building Team**: Track backlink campaigns
    
*   **Technical SEO**: Monitor site health and technical metrics
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#important-notes)

Important Notes


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Each workspace maintains completely **separate data**
    
*   Switching workspaces will **refresh the current view** to show the new workspace's data
    
*   Workspace settings are **saved locally** and persist between app sessions
    
*   The active workspace is **remembered** when you close and reopen the app
    
*   All API keys and service accounts are **shared across all workspaces**
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/workspace#best-practices)

Best Practices


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Name workspaces clearly**: Use descriptive names like "Client - ABC Corp" or "Project - Summer Campaign"
    
2.  **Add logos**: Upload client logos or project icons to quickly identify workspaces visually
    
3.  **Organize by priority**: Place your most-used workspaces at the top for quick keyboard access
    
4.  **Regular cleanup**: Delete empty workspaces you no longer need to keep your list organized
    
5.  **Move data carefully**: Double-check the target workspace before moving important data

# Troubleshooting | SEO Utils

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/troubleshooting#macos)

macOS

When installing the app on macOS, if you see this kind of message:

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FlzrKaoE7ekXZpRqndSd9%252FXnapper-2024-01-24-12.27.54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc55946f7-7b31-4c57-8f11-18cbaf587be2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d5d221d&sv=2)

“SEO Utils” can’t be opened because Apple cannot check it for malicious software.

1.  Please open the **System Settings**
    
2.  Go to the **Privacy & Security** menu
    
3.  Hit the **Open Anyway** button
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F2cyq2Es71OhSW855qHmP%252FCleanShot%25202024-01-24%2520at%252012.31.18%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f4d2d51-e17f-43d1-a8f1-977adf92e6d5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=29c26ef8&sv=2)

If you cannot upgrade the app, please move the SEO Utils app to the **Applications** folder

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fy93I5n8K7cP1Rr4oeHks%252F471607863_8910071832395299_4952853912844482308_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc759c6bb-7c00-4488-8d49-34c41f4fa218&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72f44974&sv=2)

Move the SEO Utils app to the Applications to folder

And please make sure you allow SEO Utils to access your Downloads folder.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FQjpwKXREYkuX40PlLmFc%252FCleanShot%25202024-05-06%2520at%252012.13.03%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea984b74-251e-4394-a996-b9ae6f42fc71&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cb3c1918&sv=2)

Allows SEO Utils to access the Downloads folder in macOS

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/troubleshooting#windows)

Windows

If you encounter a permission error or the program exits when clustering keywords on Windows, please ensure that you run SEO Utils as an administrator. This will allow the app to write the cluster data into a CSV file on your machine.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FtB2Gl8pH0NlWOrerB62w%252F53db0b2010303a3571c40e969cd8623b.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d965feb-97e8-4669-a323-06ae812a0175&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f2efbe8f&sv=2)

Permission denied

You can do that by right-clicking on the SEO Utils shortcode, going to the **Compatibility** tab, and selecting "**Run this program as an administrator**." So, each time you run it, it will always run as an administrator.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fx3zjkkn9e69lMNalG4rS%252Fimage-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D595ea24e-4d2d-4567-bb16-9063c8f90e17&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3715603&sv=2)

Run "SEO Utils" as an administrator

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/troubleshooting#linux)

Linux

If you can't open the app and see an alert like this.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FTuryZkDBIBTbaYDiOsem%252FCleanShot%25202024-08-06%2520at%252010.51.50%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5b421ee-6334-486f-85d2-7b7d4f19c06d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=76af4513&sv=2)

# Local SERP Checker | SEO Utils

The SERP UULE tool leverages the UULE (Unicode URL-Encoded) parameter, a method Google uses to understand and simulate search results as if they were being conducted from various geographic locations. This capability is significant because Google's search results can vary greatly depending on the searcher's location, due to localization and personalization factors.

By manipulating the UULE parameter, this tool can simulate searches from different locations, providing insights into how search results appear to users in those areas.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/local-serp-checker#benefits-of-using-the-serp-uule-tool)

Benefits of Using the SERP UULE Tool

1.  **SEO Strategy Optimization:** By understanding how websites rank in different regions, SEO professionals can tailor their strategies to target specific geographic markets more effectively.
    
2.  **Competitive Analysis:** It enables businesses to see how their competitors perform in different locales, providing insights into local market competition and identifying potential areas for expansion.
    
3.  **Content Localization:** Helps in identifying what localized content performs well in certain regions, guiding content creation and marketing strategies to cater to local tastes and preferences.
    
4.  **Ad Campaigns Refinement:** By analyzing search results in different locations, marketers can refine their ad campaigns to be more relevant to local audiences, potentially increasing engagement and conversion rates.
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/local-serp-checker#how-to-check-google-search-results-for-different-locations)

**How To Check Google Search Results for Different Locations**

1.  Click the "SERP UULE" tool in the left sidebar.
    
2.  Enter a search query.
    
3.  Enter a city, state, or country that you want to view the search results for.
    
4.  Hit the "Search" button. SEO Utils will open a new tab with the SERP based on the location you selected.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FIpc5sB5YNOT8c5zpjUvH%252FCleanShot%25202024-03-04%2520at%252016.59.12%25202%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddc38b3b9-66e0-40d0-a5da-1d5debcc4075&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d124eeb7&sv=2)

SERP UULE

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/local-serp-checker#how-to-change-the-default-geo-target)

How to Change the Default Geo Target

You can change the default location by visiting the Settings menu. Then, type the default location at the **Default Geo Target** field.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F0hFTHZPFFCHSHAL0rhsu%252FXnapper-2024-03-04-17.06.10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbbde7972-9ac7-4826-bcce-b837dafe9bcd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=da41a9fc&sv=2)

Set the default geo target.

By setting the default geotarget, you won't have to type it in every search.

# Semantic Keyword Clustering | SEO Utils

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#what-are-the-differences-between-seo-utils-keyword-clustering-and-other-tools)

What Are the Differences Between SEO Utils' Keyword Clustering and Other Tools?

Here are 2 of the main differences:

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#flexible-to-switch-the-embedding-model)

Flexible to Switch the Embedding Model

Embedding models in Natural Language Processing (NLP) are designed to convert words, phrases, sentences, or entire documents into numerical vectors. These vectors represent the linguistic features of the text, allowing machines to process and analyze language in a meaningful way.

To do keyword clustering well, you need a good model that's already been trained. With AI growing fast, new models are coming out almost every day. You can visit [HuggingFace](https://huggingface.co/)
, a website, to get a free model and use it with SEO Utils to find one that's best for your type of business.

You can also take one of these models and train it more on words specific to your niche or industry. Then, use this customized model in SEO Utils for even better keyword clustering, which can improve your SEO results.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#unlimited-keywords-for-clustering)

Unlimited Keywords for Clustering

With SEO Utils, you're not restricted in the number of keywords you can cluster. This is a big advantage over other tools that limit you to clustering between 5,000 to 10,000 keywords at a time. Since SEO Utils runs on your computer, it can handle as many keywords as you need, going way beyond these limits.

There's also no credit-based system, meaning you don’t have to pay extra no matter how many keywords you cluster. This can mean big savings, especially in large niches like Gym or Fitness where you might need to cluster a million keywords.

You might think, "_Can't I just cluster keywords with ChatGPT or the OpenAI API?_" While it's true you can cluster a few hundred keywords with these tools, they hit a limit when you try more than 10,000 keywords due to token limitations. Even with GPT-4 Turbo, which allows more tokens, the quality of clustering decreases with more keywords. It often loses context, doesn't follow instructions well, and misses keywords because you cannot control the `temperature` parameter in ChatGPT. You can do it with OpenAI API, but the cost is too high.

That's where a dedicated keyword clustering tool like SEO Utils makes a big difference.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#semantic-clustering-vs-serp-clustering)

Semantic Clustering vs SERP Clustering

In my experience, SERP Clustering always gives you the best result of clustering. However, it comes with many technical issues like proxy rotation, time-consuming, server resources, etc.

Take [Larseo's SERP Clustering](http://larseo.app/)
, for example. It lets you cluster unlimited keywords, but clustering 1 million keywords takes a really long time and can cost about $2,900 (at 0.5 credit per keyword).

On the other hand, using the Semantic Clustering feature in SEO Utils is a different story. You don't have to pay extra, and you can get results as good as SERP Clustering. You can achieve this by fine-tuning your model to suit your specific needs.

SEO Utils will support fine-tuning soon!

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#how-to-download-embedding-models-and-use-it-on-seo-utils)

How to Download Embedding Models and Use It on SEO Utils?

This documentation is for Semantic Clustering v1. For a better experience and improved performance, please refer to the [documentation for Version 2](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#updated-nov-26-2024-semantic-keyword-clustering-v2)
.

Also, version 1 is not available for Linux.

SEO Utils - How to use Semantic Keyword Clustering

1.  First, you can visit this leaderboard: [https://huggingface.co/spaces/mteb/leaderboard](https://huggingface.co/spaces/mteb/leaderboard)
    
2.  Click on the "Clustering" tab, and then select the language that matches your keywords.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FwC9XUQKGuM9Y5KzHouW9%252FXnapper-2023-11-18-18.38.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54831e91-840c-4cba-a353-96eecbd042d4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b197c7e2&sv=2)

List of top embedding models

1.  You will see the top embedding models based on their clustering task performance.
    
2.  Select one model, for example, [https://huggingface.co/thenlper/gte-large](https://huggingface.co/thenlper/gte-large)
    

Only select the mode that can be used with **Sentence Transformers**.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FVachbp3x842tHl5gzApC%252FXnapper-2023-11-18-18.47.05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39ed6808-ccf7-4c6b-a184-4a49db650459&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94e70478&sv=2)

Example a model can be used with Sentence Transformers.

1.  Click on the Clone repository to download a model with GIT `git-lfs`
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FW7rmZXkHdUU1YfZBAcSP%252FXnapper-2023-11-18-18.48.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad6f147a-db89-4db2-9e0b-3a466bde4e36&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b97f292&sv=2)

Download a model

Copy

    # Make sure you have git-lfs installed (https://git-lfs.com)
    git lfs install
    git clone https://huggingface.co/thenlper/gte-large
    
    # if you want to clone without large files – just their pointers
    # prepend your git clone with the following env var:
    GIT_LFS_SKIP_SMUDGE=1

I will provide a [list of popular models on Google Drive](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#popular-models)
 so that you can easily download them.

1.  After downloading a model, open SEO Utils on your machine.
    
2.  Click on the App dropdown, and go to the Settings page.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FRqtWXBCAFolcNHPlrBlL%252FXnapper-2023-11-18-14.33.14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63831c52-375c-46f8-b0f9-2531afa92d16&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=27f281ff&sv=2)

1.  Scroll down to the **Keyword Clustering** section and enter the path to the downloaded model on your machine. Then hit the Save button.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FYSc8r7W9M8o5zn3hocIc%252FXnapper-2023-11-18-19.09.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b7ab1fa-58ed-45af-8aa6-3b0595f38c51&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bc8ff44d&sv=2)

1.  That's all. Now, you can go to the Keyword Clustering page and kick off the process.
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#popular-models)

Popular Models

English[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#english)

**thenlper/gte-large**

*   Download: [https://drive.google.com/file/d/1O4lm4hnqXoCDloqaw\_exWiz9a-Vy0ZZK/view?usp=sharing](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1O4lm4hnqXoCDloqaw_exWiz9a-Vy0ZZK/view?usp=sharing)
    
*   More info: [https://huggingface.co/thenlper/gte-large](https://huggingface.co/thenlper/gte-large)
    

**BAAI/bge-large-en-v1.5**

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#updated-nov-26-2024-semantic-keyword-clustering-v2)

Updated Nov 26, 2024: Semantic Keyword Clustering v2

With the release of [SEO Utils v1.23.2](https://help.seoutils.app/changelog#v1.23.2)
, I’ve introduced Semantic Keyword Clustering v2, which leverages a consistent [Docker environment](https://www.docker.com/)
 for running the clustering Python script. Here’s how this upgrade improves your experience:

*   **Streamlined Model Selection:** No more manual downloads from HuggingFace—simply select your model from a dropdown menu, and SEO Utils takes care of the rest.
    
*   **Faster Clustering with GPU Support:** Speed up keyword clustering with GPU support for Windows and Linux. While macOS only supports CPU, version 2 still delivers faster clustering compared to version 1!
    
*   **Polished Output:** All formatting issues in the output file have been resolved.
    
*   **Improved Reliability:** Minimize unexpected issues with a more stable setup.
    
*   **Simplified Updates:** Updating the clustering script is now easier for me, as I no longer need to build separate executable scripts for each platform.
    

**Why do I still keep version one?** Some users run SEO Utils on VPS, and not all VPS can support Docker. That’s why version 1 is still available as a backup option. If your setup supports Docker, I highly recommend using version 2!

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#how-to-install-docker)

How to Install Docker

*   Visit [https://www.docker.com/](https://www.docker.com/)
    , download it, and install it as you normally would.
    
*   Open Docker and follow the app’s instructions to start it as recommended.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FDu9xVWKili1ANkkmm7pO%252FXnapper-2024-11-26-17.53.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97c7572b-8a1e-45eb-a22b-ad18958c7c25&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b1cb1c9a&sv=2)

Docker will be run in the background

You can close Docker if you’re not using Semantic Clustering version 2 anymore.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/semantic-keyword-clustering#switch-to-version-2)

Switch to Version 2

**Step 1:** Go to Settings > Services from the left sidebar.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FPm6fLw7pjvM5JHyBA6FL%252FXnapper-2024-11-26-17.56.11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9a9ab39-3ab6-4fb1-a239-2bab2f4bcddd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f50cb993&sv=2)

Settings > Services

**Step 2:** Select **Version 2** from the dropdown and click the Save button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FKc4C3EdlZtdTxyG13G41%252FXnapper-2024-11-26-19.28.49.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63001ceb-c797-478a-b94d-8254058950bc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c46a90dc&sv=2)

Select "Version 2" option

**Step 3:** Open the Semantic Clustering tool as you normally would. You’ll notice a new field called “**Embedding Mode**l”. Simply choose a model from the dropdown based on your language to start clustering keywords.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F3t0c3cBTRZRp6eEECol3%252FXnapper-2024-11-26-19.30.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3a1cba6-edab-4b46-8626-d14786360ff3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d71b04a9&sv=2)

Select an ebmedding model from dropdown.

No more complicated setups or manual downloads! SEO Utils will automatically download the model and **cache it** for future use, so you won’t need to wait for it to re-download every time.

# Google OAuth Token | SEO Utils

SEO Utils uses Google OAuth Tokens to securely connect to your Google accounts and access Google Search Console data. This allows you to pull GSC data directly into SEO Utils for advanced analysis and reporting that the standard GSC interface doesn't provide.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#connect-your-google-account)

Connect Your Google Account


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#step-1-access-google-oauth-tokens)

Step 1: Access Google OAuth Tokens

Open the SEO Utils app on your machine, and locate the Settings menu in the left sidebar. You will see the Google OAuth Tokens menu.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F5Is9CgNnnCukZIVN3lPr%252FXnapper-2025-08-05-22.48.22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31ca83e4-d471-4e6e-b378-95fd86330289&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4ce3f6f6&sv=2)

Click on Google OAuth Tokens menu to manage your connections

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#step-2-connect-your-google-account)

Step 2: Connect Your Google Account

Click the "**Connect**" button in the top-right corner of the Google OAuth Tokens page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FV4RWVc6FAY8ywM4XVs5c%252FXnapper-2025-08-05-22.48.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddcfbb862-a186-4d28-a477-0c551a9b2fc5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=de2bbb16&sv=2)

Click the Connect button to start the authorization process

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#step-3-authorize-seo-utils)

Step 3: Authorize SEO Utils

After clicking Connect, your default web browser will open with Google's authorization page. Follow these steps:

1.  **Select your Google account** that has access to Google Search Console
    
2.  **Review the permissions** that SEO Utils is requesting
    
3.  Click "**Allow**" to grant SEO Utils access to your Google Search Console data
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F9TBLShNeq4BHXJBEkZvV%252FXnapper-2025-08-05-22.49.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d836a38-a8fb-47fe-b200-b060848a62ae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6520204a&sv=2)

Review and allow the requested permissions

SEO Utils only requests read-only access to your Google Search Console data. It cannot modify or delete any data in your GSC account.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#step-4-authorization-complete)

Step 4: Authorization Complete

Once you've authorized access, you'll see a success message in your browser. You can close the browser tab and return to SEO Utils.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FzpSdg4viY6ryCZ0vl71g%252FXnapper-2025-08-05-22.50.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc88b3c4-57b6-4757-8e09-b10735017e78&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=533ffd68&sv=2)

Authorization successful - you can close this tab

Your connected Google account will now appear in the Google OAuth Tokens list with your email address and profile picture.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FB3zLL0pkHvsxTPpcRh8R%252FXnapper-2025-08-05-22.51.09.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De891f94e-0f5b-4e44-8a64-8fe5fa0930bc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ff4c5ab5&sv=2)

Your connected Google account

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#managing-multiple-google-accounts)

Managing Multiple Google Accounts


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can connect multiple Google accounts to SEO Utils. This is useful if you manage GSC properties across different Google accounts.

Simply click the "**Connect**" button again and follow the same authorization process with a different Google account.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#remove-a-google-account)

Remove a Google Account

To disconnect a Google account:

1.  Find the account you want to remove in the list
    
2.  Click on the three-dot menu on the right side of the account row
    
3.  Select "**Delete**" from the dropdown menu
    
4.  Confirm the deletion when prompted
    

Removing a Google account will disconnect all associated Google Search Console properties from SEO Utils. You'll need to reconnect the account to access that GSC data again.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#using-google-oauth-with-gsc-integration)

Using Google OAuth with GSC Integration


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you've connected your Google accounts, you can use them with various [Google Search Console integration](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console)
 features in SEO Utils:

*   **Performance Analytics**: Complete search data with advanced regex filtering and more than 16 months of history
    
*   **Keyword Cannibalization Detection**: Identify when multiple pages compete for the same keywords, hurting your rankings
    
*   **Bulk Mentions Analysis**: Check if target keywords appear in critical SEO elements:
    
    *   Page titles and meta descriptions
        
    *   H1, H2, and other headings
        
    *   Body content and paragraphs
        
    *   Image alt text and captions
        
    
*   **Optimization Opportunities**: Data-driven insights showing:
    
    *   Pages ranking 4-10 that need small tweaks to reach top 3
        
    *   High-impression keywords missing from your content
        
    *   Title/meta description improvements for better CTR
        
    *   Quick wins based on position and mentions analysis
        
    
*   **Bulk URL Indexing**: Submit multiple URLs to Google for indexing at once
    
*   **Sitemap Management**: Monitor and manage your XML sitemaps directly
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#authorization-failed)

Authorization Failed

If the authorization process fails:

1.  Make sure you're selecting a Google account that has access to Google Search Console
    
2.  Check that you're allowing all the requested permissions
    
3.  Try clearing your browser cache and cookies, then attempt the connection again
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#account-not-showing-gsc-properties)

Account Not Showing GSC Properties

If your connected account doesn't show any GSC properties:

1.  Verify that the Google account has been added as a user in Google Search Console
    
2.  Check that the account has at least "Read" permissions for the properties (needs "Owner" permissions to check index status if using the [Auto Indexing tool](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool)
    ).
    
3.  Try disconnecting and reconnecting the account
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#token-expired)

Token Expired

Google OAuth tokens may occasionally expire. If you see errors about expired tokens:

1.  Simply delete the affected account from the list
    
2.  Click "**Connect**" to re-authorize the account
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token#privacy-and-security)

Privacy & Security


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   SEO Utils stores OAuth tokens securely on your local machine
    
*   Tokens are never transmitted to any external servers except Google's APIs
    
*   You can revoke access at any time by deleting the account from SEO Utils
    

[PreviousGoogle Service Accounts](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts)
[NextGoogle Search Console](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console)

Last updated 3 months ago

---

# My Go-To SEO Checklist with Google Search Console & GPTs | SEO Utils

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/my-go-to-seo-checklist-with-google-search-console-and-gpts#step-1-download-all-the-query-and-page-data-from-my-google-search-console-account)

Step 1: Download all the query and page data from my Google Search Console account.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/my-go-to-seo-checklist-with-google-search-console-and-gpts#step-2-go-over-each-prompt-individually-using-my-data-analyzer-gpts.-each-prompt-includes-specific-a)

Step 2: Go over each prompt individually using my [Data Analyzer GPTs](https://chat.openai.com/g/g-3uK215Gt4-seo-utils-gsc-data-analyzer)
. Each prompt includes specific actions, so you'll know exactly what to do.

Demo video on how to use Data Analyzer GPTs.

**#1. Prompt:** Find keywords that ranked on page 2 but are not mentioned in the title

**Action:** I add these keywords to the title. It's a simple tweak that can make a big difference.

* * *

**#2. Prompt:** Find keywords that ranked on page 2 but are not mentioned in the meta description **Action:** I make sure to include these keywords in the meta description for better relevance.

* * *

**#3. Prompt:** Find keywords that ranked on page 2 but are not mentioned in headings

**Action:** Adding these keywords to the headings helps in better structuring my content.

* * *

**#4. Prompt:** Find keywords that are not mentioned at all, but still ranking

**Action:** Sprinkle these keywords throughout my content to climb higher in search rankings.

* * *

**#5. Prompt:** Find keywords that have high impressions but are not mentioned.

**Action:** Ensure these keywords are mentioned in my content as Google already finds them relevant.

* * *

**#6. Prompt:** Find keywords that are getting a lot of impressions, but no or low clicks. These are potential opportunities. A high impression count means your site is showing up in search results, but a low click-through rate suggests that users are not finding your listing relevant or compelling enough to click.

**Action:** I focus on these keywords more, sometimes creating new content around them. It's all about converting views to clicks.

* * *

**#7. Prompt:** Find keywords that are ranking in position 3-11.

**Action:** Almost there, just put extra effort into these by optimizing my content and sometimes adding backlinks to boost them further.

* * *

**#8. Prompt:** Find keywords that have low average ranking positions but high CTR.

**Actions:** These keywords are already doing good in terms of CTR, just need to optimize content to get a higher rank.

* * *

**#9. Prompt:** Find keywords that have high average ranking positions but low CTR.

**Action:** Working on title or meta description to increase clicks on these well-positioned keywords.

* * *

**#10. Prompt:** Find question keywords that I can add to FAQ sections

**Action:** Add these to my FAQ section, answering popular queries directly.

* * *

**#11. Prompt:** Find keywords & pages that bring traffic to my site

**Actions:**

*   You might find variations of your current keywords or entirely new phrases that you hadn’t considered before.
    
*   Explore expanding this topic or using a similar approach (content or backlink strategy) for other topics.
    
*   Consider creating more related content or enhancing existing content around these topics.
    

* * *

**#12. Prompt:** What are the topics that all keywords are covering? This will help you understand what topics are already covered on the website

**Action:** Find the topic gap by doing reverse-engineering on competitor's websites

* * *

**#13. Prompt:** Find keyword cannibalization

**Action:**

*   First, I usually ignore the URLs that contain fragment symbols ("#"). GSC considers those URLs are pages, just make sure you have a correct canonical tag on your page.
    
*   Then, I visit the pages that are ranking the same keywords as other pages and check if they haven't had any traffic in the last 3 months, I will delete them and do a 301 redirect. if you feel the content of the deleted page is good, consider merging its content with the content of the main page.
    

* * *

**Output:** The GPTs will export the keyword list as a CSV file.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/my-go-to-seo-checklist-with-google-search-console-and-gpts#if-your-keyword-list-is-still-large-after-using-the-prompts-here-are-some-additional-tips)

🔑 If your keyword list is still large after using the prompts, here are some additional tips:

✅ Add the topic with the prompt. For example, "Find keywords that are not mentioned at all, but still ranking"

✅ Focus on long-tail keywords first. For example, "Find long-tail keywords that have high average ranking positions but low CTR"

✅ Focus on search intents. Are your users looking for information, trying to make a purchase, or seeking a specific website? Align your content with the user's intent for the keyword. "For example, Find informational keywords that are ranking in position 3-11"

**Pro Tip:** With SEO Utils, use the Mentions filter to quickly see if your keyword is in the title, headings, or body of a page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FzBxarmSfmD27TvU7sr0u%252FXnapper-2024-01-24-22.16.08.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8964b803-0d22-4e06-b35c-96ec5ba4a4a1&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=21c087b9&sv=2)

I hope these tips are useful for you. Cheers! 🎉🔥

[PreviousSEO Tests](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests)
[NextAuto-Indexing Tool](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool)

# Rent DataForSEO API Key | SEO Utils

Using DataForSEO's API has a major drawback: a required monthly fee of $100 to use their Backlinks API. SEO Utils has introduced a solution to this problem. We offer a feature where you can rent a DataForSEO API Key, eliminating the need for the monthly fee.

You simply purchase credits of $10, $20, or $50 and pay as you go. The best part? These credits never expire.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key#how-to-purchase-credits)

How to Purchase Credits?

**Step 1:** Visit [https://app.seoutils.app/register](https://app.seoutils.app/register)
 and register an account. You will need to verify your email address.

**Step 2:** After logging in, click the user dropdown in the top-right corner and select "Purchase Credits."

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F2zYx8QPksWIkcuFjfXlJ%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-16.43.22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26795994-3ad3-4f4d-bcd9-7f2150da4775&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=274cc076&sv=2)

Click Purchase Credits

**Step 3:** Select the credit package that you would like to purchase and click the "Purchase" button. You will be redirected to the checkout page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FfmAjCgqsUEGc5Oa9sduD%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-16.50.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6537f841-41db-4969-9391-ccb877407f06&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3c62afc0&sv=2)

Select a credit package

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key#how-to-access-backlinks-api-on-seo-utils-by-using-credits)

How to Access Backlinks API on SEO Utils by Using Credits?

To access the Backlinks API, you will need an SEO Utils API Key.

**Step 1:** Visit [https://app.seoutils.app/](https://app.seoutils.app/)
 and click the user dropdown in the top-right corner and select "API Tokens".

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FujfBtmK21EXKoHUqAYuE%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-16.56.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf163fb3-66a1-4d57-8a5b-7214e1ef1838&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c564488e&sv=2)

Select "API Tokens" menu item.

**Step 2:** Enter the "Token Name" and ensure that you check the "Backlink" permission so that the Token can have access to the Backlinks API.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FDiFq19c2DRs7DOEWOeW3%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-16.57.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da603596c-beac-4ba9-9d77-f1087304cd0e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=80eaba04&sv=2)

Enter Token Name

**Step 3:** Click on the "Create" button, and the system will display the API Token. Copy the token before clicking the "Close" button, as the token will never be displayed again.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FkGamdQJYr4xbwhva7fVV%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-16.59.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dead6f82a-9408-4387-a64e-f19d84339b7c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3c25df33&sv=2)

Copy the API Token

**Step 4:** Open the SEO Utils app on your machine (Ensure that it is version 1.1.0 or newer). Go to the Settings page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FKUPayXq2BpxBJGrr4nrk%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.26.48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D991c99ea-6ff0-4934-bb0f-3c50343e85e0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69814cc3&sv=2)

Go to Settings page in SEO Utils app

**Step 5:** Scroll down to the "**Renting DataForSEO API Key**" section. You will see the API Key input.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fpl1d0IWJIfc9XSzRspV6%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.19.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D458f42fa-0c95-4342-9727-6828697a305d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bff337a4&sv=2)

Enter the API Key

Paste the API token that you already copied in Step 3 into that input and make sure you check the **Backlink API** on the "**Use On**" field, so the app will know that you would like to use the API token for the Backlink API, not your DataForSEO account. Click the "Save" button.

Now you can access the Backlinks API of DataForSEO without paying the $100 monthly commitment.

You can use the API token on multiple devices, or you can create multiple API tokens for multiple devices.

You cannot use the sandbox mode when using an API token to access the Backlinks API.

You can also delete an API Token by clicking the "Delete**"** button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fb6ApkqspsmAZRPnu4MUi%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.10.11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6dc7098-fc9e-400c-890a-a606710c8a79&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ebd050d&sv=2)

Delete API Token

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key#view-credit-transactions)

View Credit Transactions

You can view all credit transactions by clicking the Transactions menu from the user dropdown menu.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FwXL0sD0DkcbegM9mlAcR%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.15.36.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D176245d9-628b-42c0-9046-023b4e836ca4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b7bbf1f&sv=2)

View All Credit Transactions

You can also [share the data](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/data-sharing-with-google-drive)
 with your teammates so that they can access the same information without incurring any extra fees.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key#why-do-i-have-to-pay-usd10.89-to-get-usd10)

Why Do I Have to Pay $10.89 to Get $10?

While building this feature, I always wanted to keep the price as low as possible, so you will have seamless access to the Backlinks API. However, I have to pay the credit fee, server cost, API maintenance fee, etc., so you have to pay a little extra. Here is the breakdown:

*   Stripe charges 2.9% + 30¢ per successful card charge.
    
*   Stripe charges 0.5% per transaction when registered to collect taxes.
    
*   SEO Utils charges 2.5% per transaction to maintain API and server.
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key#updated-dec-27-2023-added-api-endpoints-for-traffic-and-keyword-tools)

Updated Dec 27, 2023: Added API Endpoints for Traffic & Keyword Tools

Before December 27, 2023, SEO Utils only supported the Backlinks API for the renting service. However, now you can use credits from SEO Utils to pull traffic and keyword data.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F6ajP5tgmto37xYsP3QpJ%252FXnapper-2023-12-27-16.13.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e31f64b-21c2-43e8-bb72-e9dc7233cc1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebe91fec&sv=2)

Settings page

Make sure your **old API Key** has "**traffic-keyword"** permission on [https://app.seoutils.app/](https://app.seoutils.app/)
 (the new API Key will be included by default).

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FB751u4mHLHvPNgnS6xsH%252FXnapper-2023-12-27-16.10.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd780e38-a729-4a1b-b7a4-befd4608ff4b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f3e3f8b5&sv=2)

# N.A.P Finder | SEO Utils

The N.A.P Finder tool in SEO Utils streamlines local citation tracking for businesses. It automatically searches for variations of a business’s name, address, and phone number (N.A.P.) across the web, helping you find inconsistent or rogue citations indexed in search engines.

**What N.A.P Finder does for you:**

*   Discovers all your business citations with a single click
    
*   Identifies inconsistent N.A.P. information that could hurt your local rankings
    
*   Exports comprehensive citation data into easy-to-use reports
    
*   Saves hours of manual search work
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FnpB82nhJiktalc8OHz8z%252FXnapper-2024-10-21-17.31.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D111a781e-522b-4e5e-b563-e73f518a0818&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e3862f9&sv=2)

N.A.P Finder report

You can access the tool in the left sidebar under the Local SEO menu.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F7vE0OrEYXoVZ9QldjAy7%252FXnapper-2024-10-21-20.34.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b8b3fb6-b166-4898-8ae9-bbf4eb80674b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=563de221&sv=2)

Access N.A.P Finder tool

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/n.a.p-finder#manage-search-term-lists)

Manage Search Term Lists

You can click the "Manage Search Term Lists" button to see all the search term Lists.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fqp2tSzeRqmRMMZ8NoheH%252FCleanShot%25202024-10-22%2520at%252011.50.19%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0bd5b98-043a-4de2-abef-730889511ed4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b66c9c9&sv=2)

Manage Search Term Lists button

SEO Utils allows you to create a Search Term List to automatically search for N.A.P. information on Google. You can structure search terms using placeholders, which are then replaced with your actual business details like name, address, and phone number. For instance, a placeholder search term like:

Copy

    "[business]" "[address_line_1]" - "[phone]"

is transformed by SEO Utils into:

Copy

    "Monsoon Seattle" "615 19th Ave E" - "(206) 325-2111"

This makes it easy to generate precise search queries for accurate N.A.P. tracking.

By default, SEO Utils will create a **Default** list with these placeholders:

Copy

    "[business]" "[address_line_1]" - "[phone]"
    "[business]" "[phone]"
    "[business]" - "[phone]"
    "[address_line_1]" "[phone]"
    "[address_line_1]" - "[phone]"
    "[business]" "[address_line_1]"
    "[business]" - "[address_line_1]"
    "[business]" "[phone]" - "[address_line_1]"
    "[business]" "[address_line_1]" - "[phone]"
    "[address_line_1]" - "[business]"
    "[phone]" - "[business]"
    "[phone]" - "[address_line_1]"
    "[phone]" - "[address_line_1]" - "[business]"
    "[address_line_1]" - "[business]" - "[phone]"

You can create a new search term list with your custom placeholders by clicking the "Add List" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FHSJ5VBmusdI8tRif9llx%252FXnapper-2024-10-24-22.21.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddfbbe6d1-ba6f-488c-b9bd-78b116f99960&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=271f293d&sv=2)

Add a new search term list modal

Note: To search for exact data on Google, be sure to enclose your placeholders in double-quotes. For example: **"\[business\]"**. This ensures that Google retrieves precise matches for your business name.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/n.a.p-finder#how-to-start-an-n.a.p-finder-report)

How to Start an N.A.P Finder Report?

After clicking the "**Run N.A.P Finder**" button, you will see a modal like this:

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FuRaTaom3d0H25AbEafE8%252FXnapper-2024-10-24-22.22.10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D243651c2-d97f-40e4-bc39-f2bb8c316b3e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef9944be&sv=2)

Run N.A.P Finder modal.

Let’s walk through all the fields.

**Business fields**

SEO Utils replaces placeholders in your [search term list](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/n.a.p-finder#manage-search-term-lists)
 with the following business details:

*   Business Name
    
*   Address Line 1
    
*   Address Line 2 (Optional)
    
*   City
    
*   State
    
*   Postal Code
    
*   Phone Number
    

**SERP Scraping fields**

**Location / Language:** Select the location and language you are targeting.

**Geo Target:** If you’d like to specify a more precise location, such as a city or state, enter it in this field. When a Geo Target is provided, SEO Utils will prioritize it over the selection from the Location / Language field.

**Desktop Devices:** Enabling this field simulates desktop devices when scraping SERP data. If disabled, SEO Utils will simulate mobile devices.

**Search Term List:** Choose a search term list for your N.A.P. search. You can either use the default list provided by SEO Utils or create a custom list tailored to your specific needs.

**Scrape SERP With:** This field functions just like the Organic Rank Tracker tool. For detailed information on how it works, please refer to the “Scraping SERP Methods” section in the [Organic Rank Tracker guide](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/organic-rank-tracker#scraping-serp-methods)
.

**Important:** To use the SERP API, you must have your own DataForSEO account. [Renting API key services](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key)
 isn't viable because DataForSEO restricts certain endpoints that I utilized to implement the Queue mode. If multiple users rely on a rented API key from my account, it will slow down the process for everyone. For the quickest results, using your own DataForSEO account is the best approach.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/n.a.p-finder#updates-on-v1.21.0)

Updates on v1.21.0

**Excluded Domains field**

Since v121.0, SEO Utils allows you to exclude specific domains from search results by using the `-site:domain.com` operator. This feature makes it easier to filter out unwanted sites and focus on relevant citations.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FP1tnqqSzkd90ItDo6sFa%252FXnapper-2024-10-31-12.56.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4d0db62-d608-439e-a4a0-a0e23fe6daa3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3f59bb98&sv=2)

Add domains to exclude

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FK8crcA2bSKedoehmipbk%252F464525662_8537579756311177_6910741920648730533_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8136b289-47f5-4624-a8b6-cffadc800fa4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31c8ce2d&sv=2)

Exclude domain using "-site:domain.com" operator

**Multiple Phone Number Formats**

You now can enter various phone number formats in the N.A.P Finder tool. SEO Utils will use each format for more thorough search results.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FB0Cv4SYdvVJE0GTS3vrd%252FXnapper-2024-10-31-12.58.37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1aec1e51-c073-4289-a3b8-82a9c393b9c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0089714&sv=2)

Enter different phone number formats.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/n.a.p-finder#mange-your-n.a.p-finder-reports)

Mange Your N.A.P Finder Reports

After successfully running a report, you’ll see a table like the one shown.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FYCRMgRB5UbjQNvaE7hqd%252FXnapper-2024-10-22-12.06.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De115ea8e-f4db-4f65-917d-8e86cc7511c3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f9a7857&sv=2)

N.A.P Finder report

Here’s a breakdown of each column:

**Title**: Displays the title of the webpage where your N.A.P. information appears. It also includes the URL of the page, allowing you to easily access the site where the citation is found.

**Search Term**: Shows the exact search term used, with your business details (like name, address, and phone number) replacing the placeholders.

**Position**: Indicates the ranking position of the result on the search engine results pages (SERP).

You can click on the SERP button to view detailed SERP data for each result.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/n.a.p-finder#available-filters)

Available Filters

**Search Term Filter:** Allows you to filter results based on specific search terms from your list, making it easy to target certain N.A.P. variations.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FykLMgVWcSuUfELvoeMy5%252FXnapper-2024-10-22-12.12.55.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa81331f-6cf6-4910-8d11-fa5815ba072e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=25207507&sv=2)

Search term filter

**Position Filter:** This lets you narrow the results to show only those that rank within the top 10, top 30, or any position range you specify.

**Domain Filter:** Helps you filter by domain to view where your business is cited across specific websites.

Once you’re satisfied with the results, you can export the data as a CSV file for further analysis by clicking the **Export** button.
