# Google Service Accounts | SEO Utils

SEO Utils uses Google Service Accounts for multiple tasks like submitting index, checking/submitting index for URLs, or pulling data from Google Search Console (GSC) to do some advanced tasks that the GSC dashboard doesn't provide to you.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#create-a-google-service-account)

Create a Google Service Account

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#step-1)

Step 1

Visit the Google Cloud Console at [https://console.cloud.google.com/](https://console.cloud.google.com/)
 and create a Project if you don't have one.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FbRVrZN84EADKlgKIL1eb%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.42.13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69f75556-50b5-424c-a776-f7da2e68cd26&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94cb8741&sv=2)

Create a project on Google Cloud Console

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#step-2)

Step 2

In your [Google Cloud Console](https://console.cloud.google.com/)
 dashboard, search for "**Service Accounts**" and click on it.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmrOPpnyFrMmJv10a9x64%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.51.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30a4be9a-68ae-404c-8c58-012cf3800d93&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebbdd184&sv=2)

Click on "Service Accounts" from the search results

Hit the "**Create Service Account**" button, and enter a service account name. Then, hit the "**Done**" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F8BZcb1ypyh8Ad9NTSSzu%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.56.52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f9ac3c6-f892-4abe-a854-5c12d4fa7269&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90c2ee27&sv=2)

Enter service account name

**Copy the email of the service account**. You will need that email to invite the service account to your Google Search Console so it can access data from Google Search Console.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmH3imZtv2LAixBDJgEKx%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.58.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47414ef3-a8a3-42c9-96f1-f0bb45ac3621&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36bdf91f&sv=2)

Copy the email

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#step-3-create-a-google-service-account-key-file)

Step 3: Create a Google Service Account key file

Click on the **Service Account's email,** select the "**KEYS**" tab, then click the "**Create new key**" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fw7wIRfDeN0xBmZRaxb40%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.08.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddfc0a806-9d8c-4e00-8fa5-9815dd29d125&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e5d4ca5&sv=2)

Create a key for your service account

A model will pop up. Select "JSON" and click the "Create" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FJf05NYUF1BLxX1oQu33F%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.10.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0984450d-e091-4dc9-91d4-e162311e1803&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a864c6f&sv=2)

Select JSON in Key type field.

After creating the key, Google will download it to your machine. Keep that file. You will need it when adding the Google Service Account to SEO Utils.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#add-the-google-service-account-to-seo-utils)

Add the Google Service Account to SEO Utils

Open the SEO Utils app on your machine, and locate the App dropdown menu in the top-right corner. You will see the Google Service Accounts menu.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FtH7mqDwIB0X1mYVQXhMZ%252FXnapper-2024-12-12-09.45.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07fec75d-97e8-42f9-a5e6-bb55f3d33163&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d5cc94a5&sv=2)

Click on Google Service Accounts menu to create one

Hit the "Add Account" button and select the key file you downloaded in the previous step.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fm9t2DkNtekc7H3OFNzqN%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-11.54.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59f6fb77-75e4-4987-ac1c-cde8e5f81928&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5d296a2c&sv=2)

Select the downloaded key file after cliking the "Add Account" button

Congratulations! You have successfully added a Google Service Account to SEO Utils!

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#connect-to-google-search-console)

Connect to Google Search Console

After adding the service account to SEO Utils, you need to grant it access to your Google Search Console properties to pull performance data and submit indexes.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#grant-access-in-google-search-console)

Grant Access in Google Search Console

1.  **Copy the Service Account Email**: After adding the JSON file, you'll see the service account email displayed (e.g., `[[email protected]](https://help.seoutils.app/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) `)
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FX6PytwRfMb5fGjEo3Vya%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-11.55.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D663ba785-6af6-4c11-a0c4-032a720427b8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=430c6211&sv=2)

Copy the Google Service Account email

1.  **Add to Google Search Console**:
    

*   Go to your [Google Search Console Dashboard](https://search.google.com/search-console)
    
*   Select your property
    
*   Navigate to Settings → Users and permissions
    
*   Click "Add user"
    
*   Paste the service account email
    
*   Select permission level:
    
    *   **Owner**: Required for submitting indexes via Google Indexing API
        
    *   **Full**: Sufficient for pulling performance data only
        
    

**Important**: To submit indexes, the service account must have **Owner** permission in Google Search Console. Full permission is only adequate for reading performance data.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#configure-properties-for-index-submission)

Configure Properties for Index Submission

You can configure which properties each service account can submit indexes for. This setting only affects index submission, not performance data access.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#property-configuration-options)

Property Configuration Options

**All Properties (Default)**

*   When enabled, the service account can submit indexes for all properties in your SEO Utils account
    
*   This is the default setting for new service accounts
    

**Specific Properties**

*   When disabled, you can select specific properties that this service account can access
    
*   Toggle off "All Properties" to reveal a list of available properties
    
*   Check the properties you want this service account to submit indexes for
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FUI6TIWGpdQaV7l1hji4B%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-11.58.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a416b11-743b-45bd-bdaf-8fcc006fb204&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db2ef26c&sv=2)

Select specific properties for this service account to access

**Note**: This property configuration is for index submission only. The service account can still pull performance data from all properties where it has been granted access in Google Search Console.

[PreviousData Sharing with Google Drive](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/data-sharing-with-google-drive)
[NextGoogle OAuth Token](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token)

# Data Sharing with Google Drive | SEO Utils

SEO Utils has a feature that allows you to automatically upload the pulled DataForSEO data to a Google Drive folder, so your teammates can access them without paying any extra fees.

For example, if you check the backlink data of site A, SEO Utils will upload that data to Google Drive. When your teammate also checks the backlink data for that site, it will pull data from Google Drive instead of requesting the DataForSEO API.

Make sure you have upgraded your app to v1.1.0 or a newer version to access this feature.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/data-sharing-with-google-drive#step-1-enable-the-google-drive-api)

Step 1: Enable the Google Drive API

Visit the Google Cloud Console at [https://console.cloud.google.com/](https://console.cloud.google.com/)
 and create a Project.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FbRVrZN84EADKlgKIL1eb%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.42.13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69f75556-50b5-424c-a776-f7da2e68cd26&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94cb8741&sv=2)

Create a project on Google Cloud Console

In the top search bar, type "API" and select "Enabled APIs & services".

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FneP1uy7uHC7NzYPFn6rC%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.44.04.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D571f9769-1be9-4c38-8d56-5fb8672b63e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=960f56&sv=2)

Select "Enabled APIs & services"

Click "Library" on the left sidebar.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fe3DpdROFizcIOn4XbGdN%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.46.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8dfaaf4-4251-4eb8-99ef-e850a465c56c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6b79dc19&sv=2)

Select "Library"

Search for "**Google Drive API**" in the top search bar and enable it, so you can access it with your Google Service Account.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FSa82EevLY6QXO7wb9R4S%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.48.37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7da2dddd-63ac-4b7d-a33a-dcc8e61dbc06&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=366b10d4&sv=2)

Enable the Google Drive API

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/data-sharing-with-google-drive#step-2-create-a-google-service-account)

Step 2: Create a Google Service Account

In your [Google Cloud Console](https://console.cloud.google.com/)
 dashboard, search for "**Service Accounts**" and click on it.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmrOPpnyFrMmJv10a9x64%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.51.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30a4be9a-68ae-404c-8c58-012cf3800d93&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebbdd184&sv=2)

Click on "Service Accounts"

Hit the "Create Service Account" button, and enter a service account name. Then, hit the "Done" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F8BZcb1ypyh8Ad9NTSSzu%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.56.52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f9ac3c6-f892-4abe-a854-5c12d4fa7269&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90c2ee27&sv=2)

Enter service account name

Copy the email of the service account.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmH3imZtv2LAixBDJgEKx%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.58.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47414ef3-a8a3-42c9-96f1-f0bb45ac3621&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36bdf91f&sv=2)

Copy the email

Click on the Service Account's email, select the "**KEYS**" tab, then click the "**Create new key**" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fw7wIRfDeN0xBmZRaxb40%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.08.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddfc0a806-9d8c-4e00-8fa5-9815dd29d125&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e5d4ca5&sv=2)

Create a key for your service account

A model will pop up. Select "JSON" and click the "Create" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FJf05NYUF1BLxX1oQu33F%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.10.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0984450d-e091-4dc9-91d4-e162311e1803&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a864c6f&sv=2)

Select JSON in Key type field.

After creating the key, Google will download it to your machine. Keep that file. We will need it in Step 4.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/data-sharing-with-google-drive#step-3-create-a-google-drive-folder-and-share-the-permission)

Step 3: Create a Google Drive Folder & Share the Permission

Go to [https://drive.google.com/](https://drive.google.com/)
 and create a folder. I will name it as "DataForSEO".

Then, click the share button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FQqCBjka8ufSdCY2v2p7Z%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.01.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0688ff5e-d109-4a7a-a8fb-62bdb8b3fb34&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=78b3211c&sv=2)

Click the "Share" button.

Paste the Service Account's email that you copied in the previous step and hit the "Send" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FePq7z9jF2nzXxkUWiESQ%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.03.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25bcb3f1-6596-4b6f-948a-53d508b676e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9f8a76de&sv=2)

Share the Google Drive folder with the Service Account's email

So the Service Account can access the Google Drive folder as an Editor.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/data-sharing-with-google-drive#step-4-enter-your-service-account-in-the-seo-utils-app)

Step 4: Enter Your Service Account in the SEO Utils App

Open the SEO Utils app on your machine, and go to the Settings page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FKUPayXq2BpxBJGrr4nrk%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.26.48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D991c99ea-6ff0-4934-bb0f-3c50343e85e0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69814cc3&sv=2)

Go to settings page

Scroll down to the "DataForSEO" section, and click the Browse button on the "**Google Drive Service Account Path"** field.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FZkUk53Nvp5OmfXq99PHQ%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.14.30.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86a485b8-bb81-45cd-a5f9-ca70a3d856cc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=92df313&sv=2)

Select the Browse button.

Select the JSON Key file that you have downloaded in the previous step.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F4XnEtxnlg6p5gxrodbd2%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.16.01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fa38035-987c-4c76-9da1-9ebab56344aa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1a73cdb9&sv=2)

Select the JSON Key file.

Copy and paste the Google Drive Folder ID into "**Google Drive Folder ID**" field.

My ID is `1WxTqniMwajikXM4dckdYpTg8a_4bLqyV`

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FCyxHYTFO7AKt56h90mnt%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.17.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68b11d3d-9b59-4ef9-8f17-71d7a5d6a1fc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d3a31ae&sv=2)

Copy the Google Drive Folder ID

Finally, click the "Save" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FRB8cdnlB2YHTsRrMAbZ3%252FXnapper-2024-03-03-10.24.13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44f0e0a0-f562-49b2-b62c-951151a80ba0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f5bf8cc&sv=2)

Enter the Google Drive Folder ID and hit the Save button.

From now on, every time you pull data from DataForSEO, it will automatically upload the data to the Google Drive Folder.

You will need to share the JSON key file and the folder ID with your teammates, and they have to set up that information in their app so they can access that folder on Google Drive.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fx5vcue7gKMHb5NugaKlT%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.32.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a3fd0bb-efc0-416f-b38f-af8d424e30b0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3cb18b66&sv=2)

The traffic data of larseo.app was uploaded to Google Drive

The SEO Utils app will automatically delete the data in the Google Drive folder after **7 days**, so you can obtain fresh data. If you prefer to retrieve the fresh data without waiting for 7 days, you can manually delete the data file in the Google Drive folder.

If you delete the Google Service Account or the Google Drive folder, you will need to remove them from the SEO Utils app to avoid any unexpected errors.

# How to Save Costs when Using DataForSEO | SEO Utils

To save costs while using DataForSEO data on SEO Utils, consider implementing the following strategies:

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-save-costs-when-using-dataforseo#id-1.-using-google-drive-api-to-cache-data)

1\. Using Google Drive API to Cache Data

SEO Utils has a feature that allows you to automatically upload the pulled DataForSEO data to a Google Drive folder, and the data is cached for up to 7 days. Additionally, your teammates can access that data without paying any extra fees.

Read the instructions at: [How to Save Costs when Using DataForSEO](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-save-costs-when-using-dataforseo#using-google-drive-api-to-cache-data)

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-save-costs-when-using-dataforseo#id-2.-using-default-filters)

2\. Using Default Filters

Since [v1.13.0](https://help.seoutils.app/changelog#v1.13.0)
, you will be able to set default filters for each request to DataForSEO. SEO Utils will apply those filters on the initial load, helping you save costs by avoiding pulling unneeded data.

For example, I often look for keywords that get searched at least **800 times per month**, have a **Keyword Difficulty of no more than 25**, and are used for **informational purposes**. I can set the default filters as shown in the following image.

Every time I visit the **Organic Keywords** page, the same filters will be applied during the initial loading.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FZL2LuohHShVmfEJJxm0r%252F436261487_7529981993737630_4040108221033116791_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78469f6f-5860-4a1c-a0ac-5af76fd46b88&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0d66f&sv=2)

Set default filters for the tool that pulls DataForSEO data to save costs.

[PreviousBulk SEO Metadata Optimizer](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer)
[NextManage SERP Data](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/manage-serp-data)

# Topic Clusters | SEO Utils

Topic Clusters is an AI-powered feature that groups semantically related search queries together, allowing you to analyze their collective performance and identify content opportunities at scale. By leveraging the [Embedding Database](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database)
, this feature goes beyond simple keyword matching to understand the actual meaning and intent behind queries.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FtcYULN7JGdyRh6uVO0V8%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-21.55.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D921ba6ea-b362-4736-8789-d01fa166e514&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e71739a&sv=2)

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#why-use-topic-clusters)

Why Use Topic Clusters?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Traditional keyword analysis looks at queries individually, missing the bigger picture of how related searches contribute to your overall performance. Topic Clusters solves this by:

*   **Revealing Hidden Patterns**: Discover groups of queries that share semantic meaning but use different words
    
*   **Measuring Topic Performance**: See aggregated metrics (clicks, impressions) for entire topic areas
    
*   **Identifying Content Gaps**: Find clusters of queries where you're underperforming
    
*   **Streamlining Optimization**: Focus on improving entire topics rather than individual keywords
    
*   **Understanding User Intent**: Group queries by what users actually mean, not just what they type
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you can create topic clusters, you need to set up the embedding system:

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#step-1-enable-embedding-database)

Step 1: Enable Embedding Database

1.  Navigate to **Settings** → **Embedding** in the left sidebar
    
2.  Toggle on **"Enable Embeddings"** master switch
    
3.  Under **Google Search Console Queries**, ensure it's enabled
    
4.  Select an embedding model (see [Choosing the Right Model](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#how-to-choose-the-right-model)
    )
    
5.  Click **"Update settings"**
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FjmHOzRFyng6u84ukcX7X%252FXnapper-2025-08-27-21.47.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab59d79b-f42a-4c51-bee1-d73614639989&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d519f162&sv=2)

Enable embeddings for Google Search Console Queries

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#step-2-generate-query-embeddings)

Step 2: Generate Query Embeddings

1.  Go to **Google Search Console > Properties** in the left sidebar
    
2.  Select your property
    
3.  Navigate to the **Settings** tab
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F8L7Ze4xrBXy0yqSgcWs3%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-22.53.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42ffffb4-467a-440c-a74b-67291502b159&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43affc36&sv=2)

Go to Property Settings page

1.  Scroll down to the **"Query Embeddings"** section
    
2.  Click **"Generate Embeddings"** to process all your queries
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FVohPaqMtZhMPRqoCbmoD%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-22.52.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ca6e3c2-a7db-4edc-b0a9-17350893b28e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d6af3b1d&sv=2)

Generate embeddings for your search queries

**Auto-Embed New Queries**: Toggle this on to automatically generate embeddings when new search queries are synced from Google Search Console, ensuring your clusters stay up-to-date.

The embedding process runs in the background. Processing time depends on:

*   Number of queries (1,000 queries ≈ 1-2 minutes)
    
*   Selected model (local models are slower but free)
    
*   Your computer's specifications
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#creating-topic-clusters)

Creating Topic Clusters


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once embeddings are generated, you can start creating clusters:

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#step-1-access-topic-clusters)

Step 1: Access Topic Clusters

1.  Navigate to your GSC property's **Insights** page
    
2.  Scroll down to the **Topic Clusters** card
    
3.  Click **"Create Cluster"** to begin
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FIrSpxEWdRpcNa5umpl0A%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-22.55.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f4595cf-0629-4008-9122-ebeab6dfe38f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73e001e4&sv=2)

Topic Clusters card

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#step-2-search-for-related-queries)

Step 2: Search for Related Queries

1.  **Enter Topics**: Type one or more seed topics to find similar queries
    
    *   Single topic: Finds queries similar to that specific topic
        
    *   Multiple topics: Finds queries similar to the centroid (average) of all topics
        
    
2.  **Set Similarity Threshold**: Adjust the threshold to control how closely queries must match
    
    *   Higher values (0.8-0.9): Stricter matching, fewer but more relevant results
        
    *   Lower values (0.6-0.7): Broader matching, more results with varying relevance
        
    *   See [Understanding Similarity Scores](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#understanding-similarity-scores)
         for details
        
    
3.  **Click Search**: SEO Utils will return all semantically related queries
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FTHlRZXugAcKPJjGCferV%252FXnapper-2025-08-27-22.04.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9cd73700-06b6-4218-99cc-d431eaf6f5d7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e6dd8e65&sv=2)

Search for semantically similar queries using AI

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#step-3-select-queries)

Step 3: Select Queries

Review the search results and select queries to include in your cluster:

*   **Individual Selection**: Click checkboxes for specific queries
    
*   **Select All on Page**: Use the header checkbox to select visible queries
    
*   **Select All Results**: Click "Select all X queries" to include all matching queries across pages
    
*   **Review Similarity Scores**: Higher scores indicate stronger semantic relationships
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Ffz0LX8NtC5dBZrwJylgM%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-22.58.08.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f5771fb-90e7-472a-96cb-67f1a461f2a7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f09f28ec&sv=2)

Select queries to include in your cluster

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#step-4-configure-cluster-details)

Step 4: Configure Cluster Details

After selecting queries, click **"Next"** to configure your cluster:

1.  **Cluster Name**: Give your cluster a descriptive name (e.g., "SEO Best Practices", "Local Coffee Shops")
    
2.  **Description** (Optional): Add notes about what this cluster represents
    
3.  **Color**: Choose a color for visual identification in charts and reports
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FcV5wBZqWjcYDlUw9LbEW%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-22.58.55.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72050e4a-1cde-430c-bae9-105cb88499cc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31e950a7&sv=2)

Configure your topic cluster details

Click **"Create Cluster"** to save your new topic cluster.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#managing-topic-clusters)

Managing Topic Clusters


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#viewing-cluster-performance)

Viewing Cluster Performance

Once created, clusters appear in the Topic Clusters card, showing:

*   **Total Clicks**: Aggregated clicks from all queries in the cluster
    
*   **Total Impressions**: Combined visibility across all cluster queries
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#editing-clusters)

Editing Clusters

Click on any cluster to:

*   **Add/Remove Queries**: Refine your cluster by adjusting included queries
    
*   **Update Details**: Change name, description, or color
    
*   **Re-run Search**: Find new related queries with a different threshold
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#deleting-clusters)

Deleting Clusters

To remove a cluster:

1.  Click on the cluster to open edit mode
    
2.  Click the **"Delete"** button
    
3.  Confirm deletion (this only removes the cluster, not the underlying queries)
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#exporting-cluster-data)

Exporting Cluster Data

Export your clusters for further analysis:

*   **Download CSV**: Click the download button to export cluster metrics
    
*   **PDF Reports**: Clusters appear in exported PDF Insights reports
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#advanced-features)

Advanced Features


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#multi-model-flexibility)

Multi-Model Flexibility

The embedding database stores vectors from different models separately, allowing you to:

*   **Experiment with Models**: Try different embedding models to find the best for your content
    
*   **Compare Results**: See how different models group your queries
    
*   **Switch Without Loss**: Change models without losing previously generated embeddings
    

To switch models:

1.  Go to **Settings** → **Embedding**
    
2.  Select a different model for Google Search Console Queries
    
3.  Generate new embeddings with the selected model
    
4.  Create clusters using the new embeddings
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#managing-embeddings)

Managing Embeddings

Control your embedding data from the GSC Settings page:

*   **View Status**: See how many queries have embeddings
    
*   **Delete Embeddings**: Remove embeddings for a specific model to free space or start fresh
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FBXJldDNV9jgcPHAfKyjZ%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-22.59.44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddc5217f7-5ca2-421c-a3db-d608081dc4b3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69bddafe&sv=2)

Manage embedding data per model

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#best-practices)

Best Practices


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#choosing-seed-topics)

Choosing Seed Topics

*   **Be Specific**: "coffee brewing methods" works better than just "coffee"
    
*   **Use Natural Language**: Write topics as users would search
    
*   **Combine Related Terms**: Use multiple seeds to capture topic variations
    
*   **Consider Intent**: Mix informational, commercial, and navigational terms
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#setting-similarity-thresholds)

Setting Similarity Thresholds

Start with these recommended thresholds:

*   **Tight Clusters (0.85-0.95)**: For very specific topics or branded queries
    
*   **Balanced Clusters (0.75-0.85)**: Good for most content topics
    
*   **Broad Clusters (0.65-0.75)**: For exploratory analysis or finding opportunities
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#organizing-clusters)

Organizing Clusters

*   **Avoid Overlap**: Check that queries don't appear in multiple similar clusters
    
*   **Create Hierarchies**: Build parent topics with broader themes, child clusters for specifics
    
*   **Use Consistent Naming**: Develop a naming convention for easy identification
    
*   **Document Purpose**: Use descriptions to explain each cluster's optimization goal
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#use-cases)

Use Cases


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#content-gap-analysis)

Content Gap Analysis

1.  Create clusters for topics you want to rank for
    
2.  Identify clusters with high impressions but low clicks
    
3.  Analyze which queries need better content
    
4.  Develop content strategies for entire topic areas
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#competitor-comparison)

Competitor Comparison

1.  Build clusters around competitor brand terms
    
2.  Find topics where competitors are mentioned
    
3.  Identify opportunities to create comparison content
    
4.  Track performance improvements over time
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#seasonal-planning)

Seasonal Planning

1.  Create clusters for seasonal topics
    
2.  Monitor performance trends throughout the year
    
3.  Plan content calendars based on cluster seasonality
    
4.  Optimize existing content before peak seasons
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#user-intent-mapping)

User Intent Mapping

1.  Group queries by search intent (informational, transactional, navigational)
    
2.  Ensure content matches the dominant intent in each cluster
    
3.  Identify intent gaps in your content strategy
    
4.  Optimize conversion paths for each intent type
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#no-queries-found)

No Queries Found

*   **Lower the threshold**: Try 0.6-0.7 for broader matching
    
*   **Use different seed topics**: Try synonyms or related terms
    
*   **Check embeddings**: Ensure queries have been embedded with the current model
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#too-many-irrelevant-queries)

Too Many Irrelevant Queries

*   **Increase threshold**: Use 0.85+ for stricter matching
    
*   **Refine seed topics**: Be more specific with your search terms
    
*   **Manual curation**: Remove irrelevant queries after initial search
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters#embeddings-not-generating)

Embeddings Not Generating

*   **Check model configuration**: Ensure the embedding model is properly selected
    
*   **Verify API keys**: For cloud models, check API key validity
    
*   **Local model issues**: Ensure Ollama is running and the model is downloaded
    

[PreviousGoogle Search Console](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console)
[NextKeyword Metrics](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/keyword-metrics)

# Keyword Metrics | SEO Utils

The **Keyword Metrics** feature enriches your Google Search Console queries with valuable SEO data like search volume, CPC, keyword difficulty, and competition metrics. You can also analyze SERP data to understand your competition better.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FDWyCcQFkh6ix86RwULts%252FXnapper-2025-08-31-21.42.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4f997a9-d274-4ba0-a444-60424feaae87&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77e50e94&sv=2)

Keyword Metrics

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/keyword-metrics#configure-keyword-metrics-settings)

Configure Keyword Metrics Settings

Before checking metrics, you need to configure the location and language settings. Navigate to your Search Console property settings and find the "Keyword Metrics" section.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FHyMNoFCnVq468dFbElYM%252FXnapper-2025-09-01-22.14.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b0cb4b6-d255-4444-9b2a-f37bcae9bad3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2ad5dc28&sv=2)

**Required Settings:**

*   **Location/Language:** Select your target market (e.g., United States / English)
    
*   **Geo Target (Optional):** Specify a more precise location for SERP analysis
    
*   **Auto-check:** Toggle this on to automatically check metrics for new queries pulled from GSC
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fi8UQCj1cSzBmxJYB7JnX%252FXnapper-2025-09-01-22.15.01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e0c9870-3ba6-4293-84e1-c78a03407fb2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c915894&sv=2)

Configure keyword metrics settings

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/keyword-metrics#check-keyword-metrics)

Check Keyword Metrics

Once configured, click the "**Check Metrics**" button to start checking metrics for your queries.

**Cost Note:** DataForSEO won't charge for keywords without search volume data, so actual costs will be lower than the estimation. SEO Utils only checks metrics for queries with missing or outdated data.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FaYJzMz3jJvu73HE5TJAc%252FXnapper-2025-09-01-22.15.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Decd39047-44cc-4609-87bc-ce363adf1f3e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=366e8ea7&sv=2)

Review estimated cost before checking

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/keyword-metrics#view-queries-with-metrics)

View Queries with Metrics

After checking completes, visit the "Keyword Metrics" page from the main dropdown to see your enriched query data.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FIyIlNE43TrJEGhbzgH6u%252FXnapper-2025-09-01-22.16.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26a5046e-bb5b-472b-8f09-856fd43269d4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8428ea07&sv=2)

Access Keyword Metrics page

You can:

*   Sort by any column (clicks, impressions, search volume, CPC, keyword difficulty)
    
*   Filter using range filters for numeric values
    
*   Search for specific queries
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FDWyCcQFkh6ix86RwULts%252FXnapper-2025-08-31-21.42.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4f997a9-d274-4ba0-a444-60424feaae87&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77e50e94&sv=2)

Keyword metrics table with enriched data

You can click the **View** button on the table to see more columns.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/keyword-metrics#analyze-serp-data)

Analyze SERP Data

Click the "**Live SERP**" button next to any query to pull live SERP data. This shows the top-ranking pages for that keyword.

For deeper analysis, select SERP URLs and click "**Analyze SERP**" to view:

*   **DR** (Domain Rating)
    
*   **UR** (URL Rating)
    
*   **RD** (Referring Domains)
    
*   **Backlinks** count
    
*   **Traffic** estimates
    
*   **Ranked Keywords** count
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FHOAWmN6yUGRSe4mRaUOq%252FXnapper-2025-08-31-21.47.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64bc0bd6-3186-42eb-b1f9-f7acbe3d3b78&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec5e716c&sv=2)

SERP analysis showing competitor metrics

This data helps you understand the competition level and identify opportunities to improve your rankings.

# How to Use Proxies | SEO Utils

While proxies aren't necessary for SEO Utils, using them is recommended if you want to speed up scraping for "People Also Ask" (PAA), check if URLs are indexed, or avoid having your IP blocked by Google.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-use-proxies#recommended-proxy-providers)

Recommended Proxy Providers

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-use-proxies#proxy-rack)

Proxy Rack

*   Website: [https://www.proxyrack.com/](https://www.proxyrack.com/)
    
*   Proxy plans that work for Google scraping tasks:
    
    *   Premium Residential Proxies
        
    *   Private Unmetered Residential Proxies
        
    

(More coming soon...)

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-use-proxies#renting-proxies)

Renting Proxies

Residential proxies can be expensive, typically costing between $60 to $150 per month. To offer a more affordable solution, I've decided to launch a proxy rental service. Details will be released next month.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-use-proxies#how-to-connect-proxies-in-seo-utils)

How to Connect Proxies in SEO Utils

To use proxies in SEO Utils for tasks like scraping Google's "People Also Ask" or checking if URLs are indexed, go to the App dropdown in the top right corner of the app and select the "Proxies" menu item.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FJRPP9Fr8Z2NdQoFG1JVG%252FXnapper-2024-02-25-16.57.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcbbca194-ad18-4431-a09d-0b18f372aa7d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=424f8b0f&sv=2)

Proxies menu

Then, click the "**Add Proxy**" button and fill all the required fields.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FSCOd3VPUDPxaETh7yEND%252FXnapper-2024-02-25-16.58.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2088dd8-13ee-4b5b-8e7d-6e162f7df475&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1f352ef9&sv=2)

Fill all the fields to add a proxy

After you add a proxy, SEO Utils will automatically use it for tasks that require proxies.

# Migration Tools | SEO Utils

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/migration-tools#database-backup-tool)

Database Backup Tool

To access the tool, please navigate to the user dropdown and select **Backup Tools > Database**.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F2Jx2wLDRIX3sSZgXjwCw%252FXnapper-2024-11-13-20.47.25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def36be0c-5212-4531-9ba2-c62e556cecec&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=10fd2a5&sv=2)

Access Database backup tool

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/migration-tools#create-backup)

Create Backup

Simply click the **Create Backup** button, and select a folder you want to save the backup file.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F8gE4e2vPyuk3CrJg6bdp%252FXnapper-2024-11-13-20.49.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1b20ae3-0031-4a0c-a1e6-a548a51248c5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e58df43c&sv=2)

Create backup

There are some **important** things you need to note.

1.  You won't be able to use the app while the backup is being created, and all background jobs will be paused.
    
2.  Please ensure that no reports are running before starting the backup to avoid data corruption.
    

The process will take 1 to 15 minutes, depending on the size of your database. Once the backup is complete, you can click "Back to Database Backup" to return to the previous page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FfT1UIW1mtoLy3FUdKn3P%252FXnapper-2024-11-13-20.54.41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39103233-cf9e-4de7-ab4f-d9a2d2ea765d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db363a56&sv=2)

Create backup process is completed!

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/migration-tools#restore-backup)

Restore Backup

You can restore a backup on your current device or a different one. **Please note:**

1.  The version of SEO Utils on the device you’re restoring to must match the version used to create the backup file.
    
2.  Restoring a database will overwrite all current data on the device.
    

Please select a backup file and click the "Import Database" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FNKa3lAplGOnjmKCTQXtw%252FXnapper-2024-11-13-21.00.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25e123a4-ce48-4152-acbc-5e28c437e2c5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=375a3fa4&sv=2)

Restore a backup file

After the restore process is complete, please restart the app to apply the changes.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F2ngxrh61oY4mOeGfGufv%252FXnapper-2024-11-13-21.02.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c757c77-4377-471d-ae6b-aec06d538f47&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9c16f806&sv=2)

The restore process is complete.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/migration-tools#app-configurations-backup-tool)

App Configurations Backup Tool

In addition to the database, consider backing up your app configurations to save time on re-setting important settings like the [DataForSEO API](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/seo-data-source#how-to-connect-your-dataforseo-account-to-seo-utils)
, [Renting API Key](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key)
, [Google Maps API](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#setup-the-google-places-api)
, [IndexNow API](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow)
, and others.

To access the tool, please navigate to the user dropdown and select **Backup Tools > App Configurations**.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FuLcgHluBrT9glH07eR5A%252FXnapper-2024-11-13-21.07.01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c990533-be15-431d-856e-8238d0fd63c7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc20a97a&sv=2)

Access the app configurations backup tool

Just like the database backup tool, you’ll be able to create and restore a backup file for your app configuration.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fo3f9r3gWRRSlP32246uU%252FXnapper-2024-11-13-21.08.09.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9064fc58-5f96-43ca-9ae9-c820ce8a2ebe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a677aa5a&sv=2)

Create & restore app confugrations

Cloud Database

This feature is coming in January 2025.

# Google Search Console | SEO Utils

SEO Utils' Google Search Console integration provides a powerful alternative to the standard GSC interface. By connecting your GSC account, you get access to all your search data with advanced features like unlimited historical data storage, natural language filtering, bulk operations, and AI-powered insights - all while maintaining the familiar GSC functionality you already use.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FaMUL8d2kDWu8HnPCa0jw%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-21.47.11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64734b2e-7dba-47a4-bd71-6ab799fa45ac&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4dc1089d&sv=2)

See how the keyword is mentioned in your content.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#setup-the-integration)

Setup the Integration

There are two methods to connect SEO Utils to your Google Search Console data:

1.  **Google OAuth Token** (Recommended for most users)
    
2.  **Google Service Account** (Advanced option for automation)
    

* * *

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#method-1-google-oauth-token)

Method 1: Google OAuth Token


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Google OAuth Token method is the simplest way to connect your Google Search Console data to SEO Utils. This method uses your own Google account credentials.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#benefits-of-oauth-token-method)

Benefits of OAuth Token Method

*   **Quick setup** - No need to create service accounts or manage API keys
    
*   **Direct access** - Uses your existing Google account permissions
    
*   **Multiple accounts** - Easily connect multiple Google accounts
    
*   **Automatic permissions** - Access all GSC properties your account can see
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#setup-steps)

Setup Steps

1.  Open SEO Utils and navigate to **Settings menu in the left sidebar > Google OAuth Tokens**
    
2.  Click the **Connect** button
    
3.  Authorize SEO Utils to access your Google Search Console data
    
4.  Your Google account will be connected and ready to use
    

For detailed setup instructions, see the [Google OAuth Token guide](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-oauth-token)
.

The OAuth Token method is perfect for individual users and small teams who want a simple, secure way to access their GSC data.

* * *

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#method-2-google-service-account)

Method 2: Google Service Account


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Google Service Account method provides more control and is suitable for advanced users who need programmatic access or specific permission management.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#benefits-of-service-account-method)

Benefits of Service Account Method

*   **Granular control** - Manage permissions for specific properties
    
*   **Automation-ready** - Ideal for scheduled tasks and API automation
    
*   **No expiration** - Service account keys don't expire like OAuth tokens
    
*   **Team sharing** - Share service account across team without sharing personal credentials
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#setup-steps-1)

Setup Steps

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#step-1-enable-google-search-console-api)

**Step 1: Enable Google Search Console API**

Start by setting up a project and turning on the **Google Search Console API** in your Google Cloud Console dashboard.

If you're not sure how to do this, follow the [first step in this guide](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/data-sharing-with-google-drive#step-1-enable-the-google-drive-api)
. The only difference is that instead of activating the Google Drive API, you'll need to enable the Google Search Console API.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FZ6zZl23z75eiDUGLLGqG%252FXnapper-2024-01-08-21.51.21.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6ee0d19b-99bf-443c-ae12-69d05c9f8dd7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b6ced9d&sv=2)

Google Search Console API is enabled

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#step-2-create-and-add-a-google-service-account)

Step 2: Create and Add a Google Service Account

Follow the comprehensive guide to create and add a Google Service Account to SEO Utils:

1.  **Create the Service Account**: Follow [this guide](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#create-a-google-service-account)
     to create a service account and download the JSON key file
    
2.  **Add to SEO Utils**: Follow [this guide](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-service-accounts#add-the-google-service-account-to-seo-utils)
     to add the service account to SEO Utils
    
3.  **Important**: Copy the service account email address - you'll need it in the next step
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#step-3-grant-service-account-access-in-gsc)

Step 3: Grant Service Account Access in GSC

Now you need to grant the service account access to your Google Search Console properties:

1.  Go to your [Google Search Console Tool](https://search.google.com/search-console)
    
2.  Select the property you want to integrate
    
3.  Navigate to **Settings → Users and permissions**
    
4.  Click **Add user**
    
5.  Enter the **service account email** (e.g., `[[email protected]](https://help.seoutils.app/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) `)
    
6.  Select permission level:
    
    *   **Full**: For pulling performance data only
        
    *   **Owner**: Required if you want to use the [Auto-indexing tool](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool)
         to submit indexes
        
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FQKrzFWgRpLkPMja8sKFb%252FXnapper-2024-01-08-22.11.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D578e8903-7abc-430f-a957-37d46cdb33b6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=423cdda8&sv=2)

Add the service account email with appropriate permissions

**Important**: To submit indexes via the Google Indexing API, the service account must have **Owner** permission. Full permission is sufficient for reading performance data only.

Once you complete this step, the Google Service Account will gain full access to the website data in your Google Search Console. With this, you're all set to utilize this integration on SEO Utils 🎉

* * *

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#data-storage-and-retention)

Data Storage and Retention


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After connecting your properties, SEO Utils will pull all data from the Google Search Console API and store it locally on your machine.

The application automatically pulls new data every day, which means you can view and analyze data for **more than the standard 16-month limit** imposed by Google Search Console.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#key-benefits-of-local-storage)

Key Benefits of Local Storage

*   **Extended Historical Data**: While Google Search Console only provides 16 months of data, SEO Utils stores everything locally, allowing you to build an unlimited historical archive
    
*   **Daily Automatic Updates**: New data is automatically fetched every day without any manual intervention
    
*   **Offline Access**: Your data is available even without an internet connection since it's stored locally
    
*   **No API Limits**: Browse and analyze your data without worrying about API rate limits
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#available-features)

Available Features


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The SEO Utils integration contains all features from the Google Search Console dashboard, plus advanced features that GSC doesn't provide. Whatever you can do on the GSC dashboard, you can do in SEO Utils - and more.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#standard-gsc-features-available-in-seo-utils)

Standard GSC Features Available in SEO Utils

*   Performance reports with clicks, impressions, CTR, and position data
    
*   Search analytics with query and page filtering
    
*   Date range comparisons
    
*   Country, device, and search appearance filtering
    
*   Sitemap management
    
*   URL inspection and indexing status
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console#advanced-features-not-available-in-standard-gsc)

Advanced Features Not Available in Standard GSC

*   Extended data retention beyond 16 months
    
*   Filter data using Natural Language
    
*   Bulk mention checking across all content
    
*   Keyword cannibalization detection
    
*   AI-powered insights and opportunities
    
*   Bulk URL indexing submission
    
*   Complete data export without sampling limitations
    
*   Multi-account management in a single dashboard
    
*   SEO Tests: Time-based Test, URL Switch Test, Split Tests
    

Please follow the guides below to learn how to use these features:

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters)

![Cover](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FtcYULN7JGdyRh6uVO0V8%252FXnapper-2025-08-28-21.55.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D921ba6ea-b362-4736-8789-d01fa166e514&width=490&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e71739a&sv=2)

Topic Clusters

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/keyword-metrics)

![Cover](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FkoY9lMsJlEuzWoM0wK67%252FCleanShot%25202025-09-01%2520at%252022.18.29%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e8e3d8a-7739-41e8-a016-742e7216aad2&width=490&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe992360&sv=2)

Keyword Metrics

# Dashboard | SEO Utils

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard#dataforseo-organic-serp-ready-tasks)

DataForSEO Organic SERP Ready Tasks

If you see something like this, it means the queue for Organic SERP tasks from DataForSEO is stuck. DataForSEO only returns a maximum of 1,000 tasks. If the queue exceeds 1,000 tasks and you keep adding more, the [SERP Clustering Tool](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering)
 or [Organic Rank Tracker](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/organic-rank-tracker)
 will hang indefinitely because the queue operates on a first-in, first-out (FIFO) basis.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FvvV3xezZtnwqcK2nQW6Y%252FXnapper-2025-01-07-20.50.04.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e8bf433-b3db-41ce-95b0-b3ddde019a80&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db93404d&sv=2)

Organic SERP endpoint is stuck at 1,000 tasks.

To resolve this issue, please visit the **Services** menu item under **Settings**. Then select the "**Free Organic SERP Tasks**" action from the DataForSEO actions dropdown.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fof6BS2tnE9T4561qEqT8%252FCleanShot%25202025-01-07%2520at%252020.56.32%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38b2bcf7-e0d3-4e22-b00b-e743d41a487c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=47c71d73&sv=2)

Run **Free Organic SERP Tasks action.**

This process may take some time to complete, ranging from minutes to hours, depending on the number of stuck tasks. During this time, you cannot use the app.

Once all stuck tasks are cleared, SEO Utils will save the SERP data to your local database. You can then reuse this SERP data in the SERP Clustering tool by setting the “[**Use Saved SERP Data For X Days**](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#use-saved-serp-data-for-x-days)
” field to a value of 1 or higher. This approach helps you save both time and money by avoiding unnecessary SERP data re-scraping.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FFwhMUnKL3xQvFA3dkeYl%252FCleanShot%25202025-01-07%2520at%252021.02.01%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58d29fdd-8187-4a93-8548-549bd6d9e738&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=121dd4aa&sv=2)

Re-use SERP data to save money and time.

The Organic Rank Tracker tool is designed to be efficient. It intelligently checks your local database to see if SERP data for a keyword already exists for the current date. If the data is available, it skips re-scraping, saving you both time and resources.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard#dataforseo-google-maps-serp-ready-tasks)

DataForSEO Google Maps SERP Ready Tasks

Similar to the Organic SERP endpoint, the Google Maps SERP endpoint has a queue limit of 1,000 tasks. If your [GMB Rank Tracker report](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker)
 has a pending snapshot that remains in a “waiting for new tasks” status for hours, it indicates that the queue is full.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FFZOhosjqJjz8N3dGii1x%252FXnapper-2025-01-07-21.08.11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9af29adf-6996-483b-a66c-b8e53caf55e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e72e52c0&sv=2)

Google Maps SERP queue is full.

To resolve this issue, please visit the **Services** menu item under **Settings**. Then select the "**Free Stuck GMB Rank Trackers**" action from the DataForSEO actions dropdown.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F114F196Pe92pt5NTJ3l5%252FCleanShot%25202025-01-07%2520at%252021.11.11%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81927862-6f61-490f-b3d8-7550d9c3c768&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57b520a3&sv=2)

Run Free Stuck GMB Rank Trackers action

This action identifies all GMB Rank Tracker reports with pending snapshots and resolves any stuck tasks. Once completed, it updates the snapshot status from “Pending” to “Success”.

This process can take anywhere from a few minutes to several hours to complete, depending on the number of stuck tasks. Please note that the app will be unavailable for use during this time.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard#final-action-delete-dataforseo-post-tasks)

Final Action: Delete DataForSEO Post Tasks

If the issue persists after running the **Free Stuck actions** (including Google Maps and Organic SERP Data), you can try the “**Delete DataForSEO Post Tasks**” action and then **re-run the Free Stuck action** again.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fv5Bo5RrFTPBv0JQVhZws%252FXnapper-2025-03-13-11.01.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D989ccd8c-1b49-4956-abdd-fe6b9aec946d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d8325607&sv=2)

Delete DataForSEO Post Tasks action

**Warning:** This action permanently deletes all posted tasks in your local database that are older than 10 minutes. Once deleted, the data cannot be recovered, even if you have already paid for DataForSEO. Use this option only as a last resort.

[PreviousMigration Tools](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/migration-tools)
[NextOrganic Rank Tracker](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker)

# Manage SERP Data | SEO Utils

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FsPRJjYnDgWJRmnKUxsQL%252FCleanShot%25202024-10-31%2520at%252014.09.42%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f134b5c-7731-4b55-992c-b713fae2303a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a7638524&sv=2)

SERP Data

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/manage-serp-data#serp-data-exporter-importer)

SERP Data Exporter / Importer

You can export your SERP data from one computer and easily import it onto another, making it convenient to work across multiple devices. This helps reduce costs for [SERP Clustering](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering)
, [N.A.P Finder](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/n.a.p-finder)
, and [Organic Rank Tracker](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/organic-rank-tracker)
.

Additionally, SEO Utils supports importing external SERP data, making it an ideal solution when migrating your SERP data from other tools.

In the screenshot below, I uploaded over **18,000 keywords** to the SERP Clustering tool and used SERP data from the past 7 days. The cost came to just **$0.0390**, saving me **$11.2470**! SEO Utils only sent **65 keywords** to the SERP API for new data, as most of the keywords already had recent SERP data within 7 days.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fw4d5ARFO4QVfxfQMJWII%252F464919090_8563919223677230_7461303937806986891_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D782ffea3-b6ff-4b7c-9d91-843fc2b6a7e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d4b41e64&sv=2)

Save money when using old SERP data.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/manage-serp-data#delete-old-serp-data)

Delete Old SERP Data

By default, SEO Utils stores all your SERP data in a database indefinitely. However, as your database grows over years of running SERP Clustering, you may notice slower performance.

To address this, you can view your SERP database size and set a data retention period. Any SERP data older than this period will be automatically deleted at startup, helping the app run reports—like SERP Clustering and Organic Rank Tracker—more efficiently.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fel8hGi1PniyVG4XUpKVm%252FXnapper-2024-10-31-14.19.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd8ed43b-d3ca-4081-a107-3bf9b5855d5c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e9bfa93&sv=2)

SERP Database Manager

In the example above, I've set the retention period to **90 days (3 months)**, so SEO Utils will only keep SERP data from the past 90 days on my computer. You can adjust this to any timeframe you like, such as 365 days for one year, or set it to 0 to store data indefinitely.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/manage-serp-data#dataforseo-serp-data-getter)

DataForSEO SERP Data Getter

Available since v1.38.3

This feature allows you to directly import SERP data from DataForSEO by entering task IDs. This is useful when you have existing DataForSEO tasks and want to save their SERP data to your local database for use in [SERP Clustering](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering)
, [Organic Rank Tracker](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/organic-rank-tracker)
, and other tools.

![DataForSEO SERP Data Getter](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fm4GWOXg6uqIk0NFR0wyQ%252FXnapper-2025-10-05-13.07.36.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D40a1a120-a586-4b8e-8cf1-081bd87185a4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8ac04967&sv=2)

DataForSEO SERP Data Getter

**How to use:**

1.  Enter your DataForSEO task IDs (one per line) in the text area
    
2.  Select the search engine type (Organic, or AI Mode)
    
3.  Click "Fetch SERP Data"
    

The tool will automatically:

*   Fetch the SERP data from DataForSEO using the task IDs
    
*   Extract all necessary metadata (keyword, location, language, device type, etc)
    
*   Save the data to your local database
    

This is particularly helpful when:

*   You've run SERP tasks through DataForSEO's API directly
    
*   You want to import historical SERP data from DataForSEO
    
*   You're migrating data from another system that uses DataForSEO
    

[PreviousHow to Save Costs when Using DataForSEO](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-save-costs-when-using-dataforseo)
[NextMigration Tools](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/migration-tools)
