# IndexNow | SEO Utils

While the [Auto-Indexing tool](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool)
 only submits your URLs to Google, the [IndexNow](https://www.indexnow.org/index)
 tool submits your URLs to many other search engines like Bing, Yandex, Naver, Seznam.cz, and Yep with just **one submission**.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#how-to-integrate-indexnow-to-seo-utils)

How to Integrate IndexNow to SEO Utils?

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#step-1-get-an-api-key)

Step 1: Get an API Key

Visit [https://www.bing.com/indexnow/getstarted](https://www.bing.com/indexnow/getstarted)
, you will see a form like this to generate an API key.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FZq7IpZfXH33YV5bzo5WS%252FCleanShot%25202024-03-21%2520at%252016.58.01%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2de165ed-01cc-47ef-90a6-d4ab5341cca5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f117fd9&sv=2)

Generate a IndexNow API key

Click the "**Generate**" button to get an API Key, then click the "**Download**" icon to download the API Key file.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FvDRuTghe86p2XKkB0AFI%252FXnapper-2024-03-21-17.01.49.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D168db58e-73f3-4f06-8cc1-4e70123dc924&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40e4aa46&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#step-2-upload-the-key-file-to-the-root-of-your-website)

Step 2: Upload the Key File to the Root of Your Website

You will need to host your downloaded key file (Step 1) at the root of your website.

If your website domain is **tuikhoeconban.com**, then the file should be located at [https://tuikhoeconban.com/c52ff0461aee4edf836b8ff0d24c5ff8.txt](https://tuikhoeconban.com/c52ff0461aee4edf836b8ff0d24c5ff8.txt)

You can visit that URL to validate if the file is uploaded successfully.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#step-3-add-sitemap-urls-to-seo-utils)

Step 3: Add Sitemap URLs to SEO Utils

Open the SEO Utils app and click the IndexNow in the left sidebar to access the tool.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FuKstQF9pgOJRQVD0yIBC%252FCleanShot%25202024-03-21%2520at%252017.09.51%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2035be7-1bf1-43ad-b312-7d1949f6a949&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ece27853&sv=2)

IndexNow tool in SEO Utils

Click the "Import URLs" button or the "Plus" icon to add sitemap URLs.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FClLLpV1w5TgimWHnkDsT%252FXnapper-2024-03-21-19.43.56.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db573c9fa-183a-4684-9e74-136e3d961cf9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14898a2a&sv=2)

Add sitemap URLs

After adding sitemap URLs, SEO Utils will import all the URLs. You can also switch the sites by using the Site dropdown.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FwBuDPXQ84rljMBnIuDVB%252FXnapper-2024-03-21-19.45.11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74e3b0a2-570f-4972-825e-eaa3a0d560b3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f5af2638&sv=2)

Switching to a site to view URLs

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#step-4-add-indexnow-api-key-to-sites)

Step 4: Add IndexNow API Key to Sites

While selecting a site, you will see the "Cog" icon. Click on it to open the settings modal.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FAfjVzGoHK4ws6tUdtdpq%252FXnapper-2024-03-21-19.48.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd43187b5-af6a-459b-9cef-82626f20ddf2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ff0422e5&sv=2)

Open the Site Settings modal

Enter the IndexNow API Key you got from **Step 1** and hit the "Save" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F9fvMFxfEH7JaGghfnBEA%252FXnapper-2024-03-21-19.50.10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4aef9f8-2988-4310-9a61-daca5743b0b5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cd468be7&sv=2)

Enter the API Key

Now, all the setup is done. You are ready for indexing submission!

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#checking-index)

Checking Index

You can trigger a process to bulk-check the index for all URLs on your site by clicking the **Check Index** action.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmKa7doNsypA4nCVog1HI%252FXnapper-2024-03-22-10.23.55.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98ae0b3b-6eb1-4779-96fa-9ee11e999a33&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43565ef7&sv=2)

Bulk check index action

You can also check index for a single URL by clicking the vertical dots icon.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FQGRVFc3lqqhtHGUJTwMX%252FXnapper-2024-03-22-10.26.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D391ecb59-5ac5-416e-bad5-2cbd5e8ba115&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=66831e41&sv=2)

Check index for a URL

SEO Utils will search Bing and other search engines using the "site:url" operator to see if the URL is on the SERP.

You want to consider [using Proxies](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-use-proxies)
 to prevent the search engines from blocking your IP when checking thousands of URLs.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#submitting-index)

Submitting Index

Just like the "Check Index" action, you can submit either multiple URLs or just one URL for indexing.

When you bulk-submit URLs, SEO Utils will submit all URLs, regardless of their indexed or submitted status.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FKWfNjDawC7fkNuFrIkDn%252FXnapper-2024-03-22-10.40.30.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee92a85e-2c18-4e56-88aa-1f7c7ead7539&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=321f0047&sv=2)

Bulk submit index action

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#scheduled-jobs-auto-mode)

Scheduled Jobs (Auto-mode)

*   SEO Utils will pull URLs from all sitemaps daily at **5:00 AM (your local time)** to get new URLs and check if the existing URLs have content updated by using the Last Mod field from your sitemaps.
    
*   SEO Utils will auto-check index of all sites at **6:00 AM (your local time).**
    
*   SEO Utils will auto-submit your sites for indexing **every 10 minutes**.
    

SEO Utils also detects when your content has been added or updated; it will automatically resubmit the URL. Just make sure to keep the app open at all times.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#override-the-auto-mode-behavior)

Override the Auto-Mode Behavior

This is the default behavior of the Auto-mode

*   **Checking index**: If a URL is already **indexed**, it won't re-check index for that URL in the subsequent runs.
    
*   **Submitting index**: If a URL is already **submitted** or **indexed**, it won't re-submit that URL in the subsequent runs.
    

If you would like to override those behaviors, please open the Site setting modal.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F6h3WOSxhCVhUzjkfRDiH%252FXnapper-2024-04-24-21.05.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba1738e4-70c2-4df7-bf67-addab8c85faa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f5ac4c9&sv=2)

Open the setting modal.

You will see 2 fields:

*   **Auto Recheck Index After** field: You can specify the number of days to recheck the index even if the URL is already indexed.
    
*   **Auto Resubmit Index After** field: You can specify the number of days to resubmit URLs even if URLs are already submitted but not indexed.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F91wqFcuj6WcoGm6hS8z2%252FXnapper-2024-04-24-21.06.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df20aaf3b-ea22-4f65-9037-544a9fb81cda&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a9cdff89&sv=2)

Override the Auto-mode behavior

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#url-received.-indexnow-key-validation-pending)

URL received. IndexNow key validation pending

When you have just added a new API key and try to submit the index, you will see a message: "URL received. IndexNow key validation pending." This is because IndexNow needs to validate the API key with the file you uploaded to your website.

This message will disappear after a couple of minutes.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#how-to-fix-403-forbidden-error-user-is-unauthorized-to-access-the-site.-please-verify-the-site-using)

How to Fix 403 Forbidden Error: User is unauthorized to access the site. Please verify the site using the key and try again

This error occurs when IndexNow is unable to verify your site because you entered the wrong API key or the uploaded file was not located at the root of your website.

If this error keeps happening, you will need to **regenerate an API key** and complete the setup process again.

If you have any further questions, please visit the FAQs section on the IndexNow website at [https://www.indexnow.org/faq](https://www.indexnow.org/faq)

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/indexnow#two-checking-index-methods)

Two Checking Index Methods

Since version 1.17.0, SEO Utils now supports using the **Bing Webmaster Tools API** to check if a URL is indexed on Bing.com, in addition to the traditional **"site:url"** operator method.

To switch the checking index method of a site, please open the site setting modal.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FvR5Jw8PEFP5huRveG79w%252FXnapper-2024-06-25-13.55.01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64b2ee0c-3a58-4dcd-8b76-e46d81178114&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2524691e&sv=2)

Open the site setting modal.

You can select the Bing Webmaster Tools API option from the "**Checking Index Method**" field.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FCvmPchOoxHUV95353VZ0%252FXnapper-2024-06-25-13.56.32.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e0d58ea-7304-46e7-9ec4-c85902976822&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db0a3abe&sv=2)

You are required to enter a Bing Webmaster Tools API key. To get one, please visit [https://www.bing.com/webmasters/tools](https://www.bing.com/webmasters/tools)
.

Then, open the Settings panel to access the **API access** menu.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FLl1yl8JKA1vHZ7D1Ykji%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-25%2520at%252013.59.59%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c959dac-0ea1-4db7-bef5-2205e8d2c7b5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1bf6e56&sv=2)

API access from Settings panel

Select the **"API Key"** menu to continue.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FwDPWQhxeyxzgEcPzdRoM%252FXnapper-2024-06-25-14.02.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87c90cec-325e-4d68-8faa-9a210e8ad89c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9f479300&sv=2)

After creating an API Key, please copy it and paste it into the **Bing Webmaster Tools API Key** field on SEO Utils.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FXsaXnz7Yuxo681SX2X4a%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-25%2520at%252014.04.05%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82993301-c69d-4b82-90e5-040fb3dc2b8e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59eb156b&sv=2)

That's all! Now, you can check the index of URLs by using the Bing Webmaster Tools API.

# Privacy Policy | SEO Utils

**1\. Introduction**

*   This Privacy Policy applies to all information collected through our desktop application, SEO Utils ("Service"), and any related services, sales, marketing, or events.
    

**2\. Information We Collect**

*   We may collect personal information that you voluntarily provide to us when registering to use our Service, expressing an interest in obtaining information about us or our products and services, or otherwise contacting us.
    
*   The personal information we collect depends on the context of your interactions with us and the Service, the choices you make, and the features you use.
    

**3\. How We Use Your Information**

*   We use personal information collected via our Service for a variety of business purposes, such as:
    
    *   To facilitate the creation and securing of your account on our Service.
        
    *   To post testimonials with your consent.
        
    *   To enforce our terms, conditions, and policies.
        
    *   For other business purposes, such as data analysis, identifying usage trends, determining the effectiveness of our promotional campaigns, and to evaluate and improve our Service, products, marketing, and your experience.
        
    

**4\. Sharing Your Information**

*   We may share your information with our service providers, in connection with any business transfers, to comply with laws, to protect your rights, or with your consent.
    

**5\. Cookies and Similar Technologies**

*   We may use cookies and similar tracking technologies to access or store information.
    

**6\. Data Security**

*   We have implemented appropriate technical and organizational security measures designed to protect the security of any personal information we process.
    

**7\. Data Retention**

*   We will only retain your personal information for as long as necessary for the purposes set out in this Privacy Policy.
    

**8\. Privacy Rights**

*   Depending on your location, you may have rights under applicable data protection laws in relation to your personal data, such as the right to request access, correction, or deletion of your personal data.
    

**9\. Policy Updates**

*   We may update this Privacy Policy from time to time. The updated version will be indicated by an updated "Revised" date and the updated version will be effective as soon as it is accessible.
    

**10\. Contact Us**

*   If you have questions or comments about this policy, you may [email us](https://help.seoutils.app/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9ff2fadfeff7eafcf3f7b1fcf0f2)
    .

# SEO Tests | SEO Utils

SEO Utils allows you to run controlled experiments to measure the impact of your SEO changes using real [Google Search Console data](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console)
. The tool automatically tracks metrics like clicks, impressions, CTR, and rankings to help you make data-driven decisions.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fh2KohiRj6W3f9l9EIwtg%252FXnapper-2025-09-08-12.34.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2267ec9-1929-4b62-8c9d-8b265ccd3582&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b566248e&sv=2)

SEO Tests: URL Switch Test.

You can test whether your SEO changes actually improve performance before rolling them out across your entire site. The tool supports three different test types, each designed for specific testing scenarios.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#test-types)

Test Types

SEO Utils supports three types of SEO tests:

1.  **Time-based Test**: Compare performance before and after implementing a change
    
2.  **URL Switch Test**: A/B test by alternating between two versions of the pages
    
3.  **Split Test**: Run simultaneous tests on different page groups
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#how-to-create-an-seo-test)

How to Create an SEO Test

To get started, head to the SEO Tests in the left sidebar. Then, click the Create Test button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FX66g6JkibzqMsP6QuTsu%252FXnapper-2025-09-08-12.35.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd11a4e7e-65d1-4518-a594-f884397501f4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b84b258b&sv=2)

Access the SEO Tests tool in the left sidebar

The test creation process has three steps. We'll go through each step and explain the different fields for each test type.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#step-1-configure-test)

Step 1: Configure Test

First, you need to set up the basic test information.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FS2xM4SGyIvXeW7RbmGvS%252FXnapper-2025-09-08-12.37.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68edc418-31c9-451f-9d40-83c194aa871b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc086c6d&sv=2)

Configure your test settings

**Common Fields (All Test Types):**

*   **Domain**: Select the Google Search Console property you want to test
    
*   **Test Type**: Choose between Time-based, URL Switch, or Split Test
    
*   **Test Name**: Give your test a descriptive name
    
*   **Description**: Optional field to add more context about your test
    
*   **Hypothesis**: Clearly state what you expect to happen
    

**Test Type Specific Fields:**

For **Time-based Tests**:

*   **Change Implemented Date**: When the SEO change will be implemented. This date separates the "before" and "after" periods for comparison
    

For **URL Switch Tests**:

*   **Switch Interval**: How often to switch between versions (1-30 days)
    
*   **Starting Version**: Which version to show first (original or variant)
    

For **Split Tests**:

*   **Traffic Split**: Percentage of traffic for the variant group (10-90%)
    

Your hypothesis should be specific and measurable. For example: "Adding FAQ schema will increase CTR by 10%" instead of "Schema will help rankings".

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#step-2-select-pages)

Step 2: Select Pages

Next, you'll select which pages to include in your test.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FGoRRkj7i3rPgnFnaEF4E%252FXnapper-2025-09-08-13.03.25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd2cd7b8-0b94-4fd7-8e3e-418c76fdec5a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7d0df698&sv=2)

Select and validate pages for testing

**Page Selection Process:**

1.  **Add Filters**: Use filters to find pages that match your criteria
    
2.  **Date Range**: Select the date range for baseline data validation
    
    *   This ensures your selected pages have enough historical data
        
    *   Recommended: Use at least 30 days of baseline data
        
    
3.  **Find Pages**: Click to search for matching pages in your GSC data
    

**For Time-based Tests:**

*   You can select or remove pages using checkboxes
    

**For URL Switch Tests:**

*   Configure URL pairs (original vs. alternate versions)
    
*   Example: `/product` (original) vs. `/product-v2` (alternate)
    
*   The tool will automatically switch between these URLs based on your interval
    

**For Split Tests:**

*   Pages are automatically divided into Control and Variant groups
    
*   You can manually move pages between groups if needed
    
*   The tool ensures both groups have similar baseline performance
    

**Tip**: For Split Tests, SEO Utils automatically balances the groups to ensure similar baseline metrics, reducing test bias. If the current split isn't well-balanced, use the **Shuffle** button to generate a different distribution of pages between control and variant groups until you find a balanced split.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#step-3-schedule-test)

Step 3: Schedule Test

Finally, set when your test should run.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FJF2hBuyam3M7eQegeFJ2%252FXnapper-2025-09-08-13.05.15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddfa0ad2b-fee5-47ce-8d81-1bede179cb26&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=caa5419f&sv=2)

Schedule your test duration

**Scheduling Fields:**

*   **Start Date**: When to begin tracking test metrics
    
*   **End Date**: Optional - when to stop the test (leave empty for ongoing tests)
    

For **Time-based Tests** only:

*   **Change Implemented Date**: When you plan to implement (or have implemented) the SEO change
    
    *   This separates the "before" and "after" periods
        
    *   Must be between the start and end dates
        
    

Allow at least 2-4 weeks for your test to gather statistically significant data. Google Search Console data has a 2-3 day delay, so factor this into your timeline.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#when-to-use-each-test-type)

When to Use Each Test Type

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#time-based-test)

Time-based Test

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FbfblorsVXr8SrGHV9wYY%252FXnapper-2025-09-08-13.10.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e2ed992-2fa9-47db-9d59-d782dc993d18&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4bf2911&sv=2)

Time-based Test

**Use when:**

*   Making site-wide changes (like updating all title tags)
    
*   Testing changes that can't be reversed easily
    
*   You want to compare "before" and "after" performance
    
*   Historical comparison is more important than simultaneous testing
    

**Example scenarios:**

*   Adding schema markup to all product pages
    
*   Changing the URL structure site-wide
    
*   Implementing Core Web Vitals improvements
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#url-switch-test)

URL Switch Test

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fh2KohiRj6W3f9l9EIwtg%252FXnapper-2025-09-08-12.34.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2267ec9-1929-4b62-8c9d-8b265ccd3582&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b566248e&sv=2)

URL Switch Test

**Use when:**

*   You have two versions of the same page
    
*   You can programmatically switch between versions
    
*   You want to minimize the impact of external factors
    
*   Testing significant page redesigns
    

**Example scenarios:**

*   Testing two different page layouts
    
*   Comparing long-form vs. short-form content
    
*   Testing different internal linking structures
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#split-test)

Split Test

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FxKLvlj6DGTevV9y8GSeg%252FXnapper-2025-09-08-13.11.52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe5267ae-2d5d-42c0-8918-a655c9919f33&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b5589713&sv=2)

**Use when:**

*   You have many similar pages (like product or category pages)
    
*   You want to test changes on a subset before full rollout
    
*   You need results faster than sequential testing
    
*   Testing template-level changes
    

**Example scenarios:**

*   Testing new title tag templates on product pages
    
*   Adding FAQ sections to half of your blog posts
    
*   Testing different meta description formats
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#understanding-statistical-terms)

Understanding Statistical Terms

SEO Utils uses statistical analysis to ensure your test results are reliable. Here are the key terms:

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#id-1.-confidence-score-statistical-significance)

1\. Confidence Score / Statistical Significance

**What it means**: The probability that the observed difference is real and not due to random variation.

*   **95% confidence** = Only 5% chance the results are due to randomness
    
*   **99% confidence** = Only 1% chance the results are due to randomness
    

**How to use it**: Wait for at least 95% confidence before making decisions based on test results.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#id-2.-p-value)

2\. P-Value

**What it means**: The probability of seeing these results if there was actually no difference between versions.

*   **p < 0.05**: Statistically significant (less than 5% chance of random occurrence)
    
*   **p < 0.01**: Highly significant (less than 1% chance of random occurrence)
    

**How to use it**: A p-value below 0.05 indicates your results are statistically significant.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#id-3.-z-score)

3\. Z-Score

**What it means**: How many standard deviations the test results are from the mean. It measures the magnitude of difference.

*   **|z| > 1.96**: Significant at 95% confidence level
    
*   **|z| > 2.58**: Significant at 99% confidence level
    

**How to use it**: Larger absolute z-scores indicate stronger evidence of a real difference.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#id-4.-uplift)

4\. Uplift

**What it means**: The percentage change in performance between control and variant groups.

*   **Positive uplift**: Variant performs better than control
    
*   **Negative uplift**: Control performs better than variant
    

**Calculation**: `(Variant Metric - Control Metric) / Control Metric × 100`

**Important**: High uplift doesn't always mean statistical significance. Always check the confidence score before making decisions.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#interpreting-results-correctly)

Interpreting Results Correctly

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#when-to-trust-your-results)

When to Trust Your Results

✅ **Reliable results when:**

*   Statistical significance is 95% or higher
    
*   The test has run for at least 2-4 weeks
    
*   You have sufficient sample size (usually 1000+ clicks per group)
    
*   No major external events occurred during the test
    

⚠️ **Be cautious when:**

*   Significance is between 90-95%
    
*   Sample size is small (< 500 clicks)
    
*   Test duration is less than 2 weeks
    
*   Major algorithm updates occurred during testing
    

❌ **Don't trust results when:**

*   Significance is below 90%
    
*   Very small sample size (< 100 clicks)
    
*   Test ran for less than a week
    
*   Site had technical issues during the test
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#monitoring-test-progress)

Monitoring Test Progress

SEO Utils provides real-time monitoring features:

1.  **Daily Metrics Updates**: See how metrics change day by day
    
2.  **Trend Charts**: Visualize performance trends over time
    
3.  **Pause/Resume Capability**: Exclude problematic periods from analysis
    
4.  **Export Options**: Download detailed results for further analysis
    

**Pro Tip**: Check your test results weekly, but avoid making decisions too early. Early results can be misleading due to small sample sizes.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/seo-tests#best-practices)

Best Practices

1.  **Define clear hypotheses**: Be specific about what you expect to change and by how much
    
2.  **Ensure sufficient sample size**: Include enough pages and traffic for reliable results
    
3.  **Run tests for adequate duration**: At least 2-4 weeks, accounting for weekly patterns
    
4.  **Monitor external factors**: Note any algorithm updates or seasonal changes during your test
    
5.  **Document your changes**: Keep detailed records of exactly what was changed
    

SEO Tests integrate directly with your [Google Search Console data](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console)
, so there's no need for additional tracking setup. Just connect your GSC account and start testing!

[PreviousKeyword Metrics](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/keyword-metrics)
[NextMy Go-To SEO Checklist with Google Search Console & GPTs](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/my-go-to-seo-checklist-with-google-search-console-and-gpts)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Content Struct | SEO Utils

The **Content Struct** tool lets you input one or multiple seed keywords. SEO Utils will then scrape the top 20 Google SERP results for those keywords, collecting all headings, main content, and SEO metadata—including meta titles and descriptions.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FPSgRGhHeGR8KS9BzpU95%252FXnapper-2025-03-26-10.51.11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4dfd4bb-882c-446d-a2b2-4695d8b99a45&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1ab917d&sv=2)

Content Struc tool

You can export the scraped data to other tools within SEO Utils, such as [NLP Text Analysis](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis)
, to extract entities and topics from the content. Alternatively, you can use the data to manually build a comprehensive content outline—or generate one instantly with AI, all in a single click.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct#create-a-content-struct)

Create a Content Struct

To create a new Content Struct, head to the left sidebar and click on “Content Struct.” Then, simply click the “**Create Content Struct**” button to get started.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FY3OaAaHn1HwkA5CkWJml%252FXnapper-2025-03-26-10.53.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D941dd033-ef25-4617-9e8b-819db0c5dc3b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=acb5a33a&sv=2)

Access the Content Struct tool.

Next, enter your main keyword and choose the target locale you’d like to focus on.

**Excluded Domains:** If you want to skip scraping headings and metadata from certain domains (e.g., youtube.com, reddit.com), simply add them to this field.

**Scrape SERP With:** This field functions just like the Organic Rank Tracker tool. For detailed information on how it works, please refer to the “Scraping SERP Methods” section in the [Organic Rank Tracker guide](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/organic-rank-tracker#scraping-serp-methods)
.

**Important:** To use the SERP API, you must have your own DataForSEO account. [Renting API key services](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key)
 isn't viable because DataForSEO restricts certain endpoints that I utilized to implement the Queue mode. If multiple users rely on a rented API key from my account, it will slow down the process for everyone. For the quickest results, using your own DataForSEO account is the best approach.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FRUBEwqemZjcBGfCI5ucG%252FXnapper-2025-03-26-10.56.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3530775-da58-4809-87e0-e57f68a2108f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=52a84bc0&sv=2)

New Conent Struct Form

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct#bulk-mode)

Bulk Mode

You can enable Bulk Mode by toggling the switch on, allowing you to enter multiple keywords at once. When Bulk Mode is active, you can also assign a Group Name to organize your keywords. This makes it easy to identify which keywords belong to the same group, filter them accordingly, and quickly switch between them.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F0oWnS9HEXJpY429Yhiqs%252FXnapper-2025-03-27-08.28.10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D394d5760-cdea-49a9-8894-4bbdfbac24b9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=623904b7&sv=2)

Filter content structs by group

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct#content-struct-detail)

Content Struct Detail

After creating a new Content Struct, you’ll be redirected to the Content Struct detail page, which is divided into two main sections.

On the **left side**, you’ll find all the scraped data from the top 20 Google SERP results—this includes headings, metadata, and main content.

On the **right side**, you’ll see your Content Outline. You can use the “**Show/Hide My Content Outline**” button to toggle the visibility of your outline as needed.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FWJJvYxzaeYOe6nddG2kq%252FXnapper-2025-03-27-08.41.20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45b7aa0d-bd9e-48cf-9c1f-9b438c78ceaa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c383aec&sv=2)

Content Struct Detail

You can copy all headings, metadata, and main content—or add specific headings from a competitor’s URL directly to your content outline.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F90LKHYHT1UV4L6JrbuQa%252FXnapper-2025-03-27-08.49.09.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De78d4557-1610-48ed-b2fb-c93294cc7c02&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=168032f&sv=2)

Copy or add headings to your content outline

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct#manage-your-content-outline)

Manage Your Content Outline

Use the checkboxes to select headings in your content outline. You can then delete them, promote a heading (using the left arrow icon), or demote a heading (using the right arrow icon) to adjust its level.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FIRA00H95ZihV2pcZC1hU%252FXnapper-2025-03-27-08.52.00.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbfaa7ea-cc89-4c61-a19c-65990189be68&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fcf444d7&sv=2)

Manage your content outline

You can also rearrange headings by simply dragging and dropping them into your preferred order.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FCYCX9dSuXay4frC0Pwvl%252FCleanShot%25202025-03-27%2520at%252008.55.22%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D033dec37-35d3-475a-a647-545ca9895003&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3fa1ff1&sv=2)

Move headings

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct#auto-generate-content-outline-using-ai)

Auto-generate Content Outline using AI

In addition to adding headings manually, you can use AI to generate a content outline automatically. The AI-generated outline includes hierarchical headings, a meta title, and a meta description to help you get started quickly.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FPBSfls2ifvpYObpFqCPK%252FXnapper-2025-03-27-09.00.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd8628b5-7d7b-406e-ad61-7f5f3725c45e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=823844e7&sv=2)

Auto Generate Outline

Please [follow this guide](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#choose-the-ai-model)
 to set up your LLM provider API keys or connect a local LLM using Ollama.

Once your API keys are configured, click the “**Auto Generate Outline**” button. You can choose your preferred AI model and customize both the **instruction** and **prompt** sent to the LLM.

SEO Utils also provides a default setup, so you can start generating content outlines right away.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmAosi3wWZm5BWp7AdFMZ%252F486055323_9380230298712781_7484248210886069612_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc5a5eed-f396-4063-ad08-23fbf0b8ad8f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90f4770d&sv=2)

Customize prompt and instruction

**Tips**

*   Please select an AI model with a **large context window**, as SEO Utils sends detailed competitor data—including metadata and headings—to the model.
    
*   Local models with smaller parameters (_e.g., llama3.2:latest (3.2B), mistral:latest (7.2B), llama2:latest (7B)_) typically do not generate high-quality content outlines. For better results, use a larger model (e.g., **32B, 70B**) or a **cloud-based model** from providers like **OpenAI** or **Anthropic**.
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct#export-a-content-struct)

Export a Content Struct

ou can export your Content Struct as a **DOCX** file directly to **Google Drive** by clicking the **download icon** button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FgbxqoLFgYV6Gighbo4ZV%252FXnapper-2025-03-27-09.16.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d665f01-c00c-428e-8cf2-4a6412fd9bb5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8736fcf&sv=2)

Export your content sturct

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct#setup-google-drive-api-integration)

Setup Google Drive API Integration

To export to Google Drive, you’ll need to take one extra step: enable the Google Drive API. Please [follow Step 1 and Step 2 in this guide](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/data-sharing-with-google-drive#step-1-enable-the-google-drive-api)
 to activate the API and obtain your **Google Drive API key**—it’s completely free.

After obtaining your API key and copying the service account email, go to [Google Drive](https://drive.google.com/drive/u/0/)
 and create a new folder. Then, share the folder with the service account email.

Next, copy the Folder ID from the URL of your Google Drive folder. For example, if the URL is:

`https://drive.google.com/drive/u/0/folders/1GvqiPSvGEDgq2yKOC52VGtS433iZXMIv`

then the **Folder ID** is: `1GvqiPSvGEDgq2yKOC52VGtS433iZXMIv` .

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F15bSkBpiOOVANeIdQV0b%252FXnapper-2025-03-27-09.23.22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4aa77269-f526-48a5-9d34-7351c61efee8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cc0a8353&sv=2)

Create a folder on Drive and share the permission to the Google Service Account email.

Lastly, In the SEO Utils app, go to the Services page from the left sidebar.

Upload the **Google Service Account JSON Key file** you downloaded earlier, and paste the **Google Drive Folder ID** into the corresponding input field—just like shown in the screenshot below.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FZKrHaeJLwshLV8hUaKa9%252FXnapper-2025-03-27-09.33.09.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8268f78b-bc17-446c-a941-7b0c7cde3fca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2dd637bb&sv=2)

Etner all information

That’s it! You can now export your Content Struct to Google Drive. All exported files will be saved directly to the folder you created.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/content-struct#unable-to-retrieve-headings-due-to-error)

Unable to retrieve headings due to error.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FkqBpQ5GTwGzC2vEJgjg6%252FCleanShot%25202025-03-27%2520at%252009.53.57%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b212934-0914-41a8-abc4-b5fc311e575c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4ecdb834&sv=2)

Error when scraping data

Sometimes, you may see an error like the one shown in the screenshot above. This usually happens when the website blocks SEO Utils’ scraper, preventing it from retrieving the data.

To fix this, click the “**Enter HTML manually instead**” button. A modal will open, where you can click the provided link to open the URL in your browser.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FdsuQqOywsiZ9z47vhUph%252FXnapper-2025-03-27-09.57.30.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1adf9e8-78dc-4f57-bff4-bd75e3250f0b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ff7fd65d&sv=2)

Add HTML content modal

After that, right-click anywhere on the page and select “**View Page Source**” from the context menu.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FqVhbFGBdjzWnlWNlG9Lz%252FXnapper-2025-03-27-09.58.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71600786-dfc8-47ba-abc6-f010fa766246&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d85c9703&sv=2)

View page source to grab HTML

Then, copy the entire HTML content and paste it into the “**HTML Content**” field in the SEO Utils app. Click the “**Extract Data**” button, and you’ll see the headings, metadata, and main content extracted from that URL.

# Google My Business Rank Tracker | SEO Utils

This tool lets you track your Google Business profile's ranking on Google Maps search results for specific locations. It also provides insights about your competitors, helping you develop strategies to improve your ranking.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fnfwzgdt3WnT7lS0INPa7%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-06%2520at%252022.35.32%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99f71187-7bb8-44e1-9bce-75568b171288&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9f375be2&sv=2)

Google My Business Rank Tracker tool

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#setup-the-google-places-api)

Setup the Google Places API

1.  Visit [https://console.cloud.google.com/](https://console.cloud.google.com/)
    
2.  Choose an existing project or create a new one.
    
3.  Search for "**API & Services**" in the top search bar.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fxtv2H2OVsZZjBm0wPRj9%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-15.59.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba72d2ea-2379-4ee0-b3d4-109c78679987&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=216e04f6&sv=2)

Search for "API & Services"

1.  Click on the "**Library**" in the left sidebar.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Ffinf05zAIP1lSpUBHwla%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-16.02.10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D009933f1-fd31-454d-8bca-fedf150fe50d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d89a9c9&sv=2)

Select "Library" from the left sidebar.

1.  Search for "Places API" in the search bar and make sure to select **Places API (New).** Then enable it.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F7yZgVsKFSQy2mMepkkP9%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-16.09.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D53938a56-375f-429a-9b33-67b1aa06a662&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f5961b01&sv=2)

1.  Do another the search for "**Maps JavaScript API**" in the search bar and enable it.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F4xBBtio3eFcyZmB0V7La%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-22.56.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6e3d375-e88e-4ebe-b365-3391959bdffb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c00a0f&sv=2)

1.  Do another search for "**Geocoding API**" and enable it.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FB9LzNEunL8KeRVqDn57z%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-07%2520at%252023.22.31%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db53cac4a-5d22-4b02-8c1b-075344fd0219&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2cfeb412&sv=2)

1.  Visit the **Key & Credentials** from the left sidebar. Then, click the "Create Credentials" button at the top to add a new **API key**.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FvkIWJHGj8KFX0aBKajmb%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-16.08.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df572c6cd-091d-48dc-8d4c-f5b6cfb7ea88&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=163356bc&sv=2)

1.  _\[Optional\]_ After creating an API key, you can name it for easy identification. There's no need to restrict the key since it stays on your machine and remains invisible to others.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fk6fUxysM5i5cYXiAACle%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-16.12.20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8f7243d-ae81-4861-9170-f1cedcb6fc57&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=87a9daf3&sv=2)

Click the "Edit API Key" button to name your API Key.

1.  Finally, copy the API key and paste it into SEO Utils's settings page.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FP9WdiOmP9uoHUsQaCH2B%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-18.42.00.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01dc9354-d258-4fcb-befa-fa6b369a1269&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7257d6b8&sv=2)

You can access the settings page from the top-right **App dropdown** in SEO Utils app.

Google might require adding billing information because Google Places API is an enterprise API. However, they will give you $200 free credit every month, and SEO Utils only use that API to search for the location. It's not even a $1 per month fee.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#create-your-first-rank-tracking-grid)

Create Your First Rank Tracking Grid

After setting up a Google Places API key, go to the Google My Business (GMB) Rank Tracker tool in the left sidebar.

Then, click the "Create Rank Tracking Grid" button to start creating your first rank tracking grid.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FkjhUtnujPeCdzgSZEea2%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-07%2520at%252018.44.28%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f3b1164-c9ed-4f95-8d27-c3ede751c1ea&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebeb453e&sv=2)

Access the Google My Business Rank Tracker tool

You'll find a search bar at the top. Start typing the name of your target business, and it will suggest business locations using the Google Places API that you integrated in the first step.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FiEmJS21OzsYYULZQ4nZC%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-18.53.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe650cc1-6f67-4ed2-9fc1-b64b34d0803f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a3c59e6&sv=2)

Search for your target business.

**Updated June 13, 2024: Adding a business using Google Maps URL.**

Since version 1.15.3, you can add a business using a Google Maps URL. This is especially useful for adding Service Area Businesses (SAB) that don't have a physical address and therefore aren't listed in the Google Places API.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F5t3qcz6jMyjUr9WN9xht%252FSEO%2520Utils%2520-%2520Google%2520Maps%2520URL.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8dce7369-2611-4228-be03-a7c24ff5f998&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50ca557d&sv=2)

_This is an example of a Google Maps URL:_ [https://www.google.ca/maps/place/Sequoia+TreeScape+Tree+Service/@44.043951,-79.4501204,17z/data=!3m1!4b1!4m6!3m5!1s0x882ad2157062b6c3:0xe060d065957c4103!8m2!3d44.043951!4d-79.4501204!16s%2Fg%2F1hhwl0yp8?entry=ttu](https://www.google.ca/maps/place/Sequoia+TreeScape+Tree+Service/@44.043951,-79.4501204,17z/data=!3m1!4b1!4m6!3m5!1s0x882ad2157062b6c3:0xe060d065957c4103!8m2!3d44.043951!4d-79.4501204!16s%2Fg%2F1hhwl0yp8?entry=ttu)

After selecting a business, you can choose a grid size from the Gird Size dropdown.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F7xO7wUnvf0s8geE9pxxn%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-19.00.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5add24e8-1a03-455a-906a-f14139b4113a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=de9b0dfb&sv=2)

Select a grid point preset

The **"3x3" preset** creates 9 markers on the map, each with its own coordinates to track the ranking of your business.

You can click on a marker to enable or disable it. If a marker is disabled, SEO Utils won't track the ranking for that location.

To remove a marker, simply click the "X" button attached to it.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FqodVrc73loDQdXOPUk4t%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-19.05.04.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db457208b-5da5-4fd0-b65e-1aef2dad8658&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0558752&sv=2)

Disabled markers

**Tip**: To save resources, you should disable or remove markers in areas where you know nobody will be searching for keywords, such as in the sea or other irrelevant locations.

You can also add a custom marker by clicking anywhere on the map.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F3VknAD4Y0RbuP4oerL31%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-07%2520at%252019.16.54.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db27acaaf-ce7a-41e2-9a85-e6be511ac79c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=56f7b92a&sv=2)

Add custom markers

The "No preset" option provides you with a blank map, allowing you to add all markers manually.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#use-radius-field)

Use Radius Field

The “**Use Radius**” field lets you choose between two methods for defining grid spacing. When enabled, it allows you to create a grid centered on a specific point using a defined radius.

For example, if you set the radius to 2 miles and the grid size to 11x11, SEO Utils will generate a grid extending 2 miles in all directions from the center point.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FfCSBD2sEIxQDIcE6E6uu%252F468528572_8730379833697834_9126134603311656292_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c83c633-1d96-419b-97d8-e9ede8f825be&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b1c56b9d&sv=2)

Use Radius is ON & Radius = 2 miles

Alternatively, if the “**Use Radius**” field is turned off, you can directly adjust the spacing between individual grid points.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FsgqRIFAFFJ9F6RIiwkJS%252F468406281_8730380057031145_2253790820121589803_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91efd400-06c7-48a8-a5e2-304b01d5e3a2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d3c55fc6&sv=2)

Use Radius is OFF & Grid Point Spacing = 2 miles

In crowded areas, a smaller radius, like 1-1.5 miles, is typically better. In rural areas, you might want to expand the radius up to 10 miles.

You can change the "**Unit**" setting to Miles or Meters. SEO Utils automatically sets the unit to Miles if your default location is in the US; for other locations, it uses Meters.

When everything is set, click the blue "**Play**" button to continue. A modal will pop up; let's go through all the fields together to fully understand them.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FouDcUah1r4iBKTBZexJW%252FXnapper-2024-06-13-16.40.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6820c6a-8b1d-4720-8cec-fad1b358af89&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6b01c7d3&sv=2)

Create report modal

1.  **Report name:** You can set a report name in this field. Default value is your business address.
    
2.  **Location / Language:** Select the location and language relevant to where your business is situated.
    
3.  **Keywords**: Enter the list of keywords you want to track.
    
4.  You can also choose how often you want the report to be updated. There are four options:
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FAWdpd2wRfvbXEA25z2Pk%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-21.24.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca6a990e-f95f-4b2e-ad09-24a1c0c5fc57&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b4df609&sv=2)

*   **Weekly**: SEO Utils will check the ranking for all keywords every Monday.
    
*   **Twice per month**: SEO Utils will check the ranking twice per month - once during the 1st-14th period and once during the 15th-end of month period.
    
*   **Monthly**: SEO Utils will check the ranking for all keywords on the first day of each month.
    
*   **One time**: The ranking will be checked just once after you create the report, but you can rerun the report manually whenever you choose.
    

1.  If you want to schedule report runs during business hours or days for more accurate ranking results, you can set it up as shown in the following image:
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FwctRnLwqTudqKnBPULYP%252FXnapper-2024-07-03-22.34.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df64dbdc4-4dc1-417e-bfb6-2da36794aea6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c59633ac&sv=2)

Set time window and timezone.

To have SEO Utils automatically re-run the report, you will need to keep the app open.

1.  **Scrape Data With**: Select the method you want to scrape the SERP data.
    

*   **SERP API: DataForSEO**. Use SERP API from DataForSEO to scrape SERP data.
    
*   **My IP (Coming soon):** SEO Utils use your IP to scrape SERP data. This is not recommended if you have over 100 grid points to check.
    
*   **Proxies (Coming soon):** Use proxies to scrape SERP data. See how to set up a proxy [here](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-use-proxies)
    .
    

**Important:** To use the SERP API, you must have your own DataForSEO account. [Renting API key services](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key)
 isn't viable because DataForSEO restricts certain endpoints that I utilized to implement the Queue mode. If multiple users rely on a rented API key from my account, it will slow down the process for everyone. For the quickest results, using your own DataForSEO account is the best approach.

This section will also display the cost for each run, but only for the **SERP API: DataForSEO** method, as the other methods do not involve pay-as-you-go costs.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FsnbAMmHmOdZLfIlPgixQ%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-19.42.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c4d8c54-7bae-445d-9a36-b600a5759650&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a54d1eb&sv=2)

Cost for each run using **SERP API: DataForSEO** method.

After clicking the "Create Report" button, you will be redirected to the report dashboard. Here, you can view all the snapshots within that report, see the rankings for each grid point, and check the list of competitors.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#updates-on-v1.21.0)

Updates on v1.21.0

Since v121.0, you can set the grid shape to Square or Circle.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fkpltdsi7kVTot87AdpMZ%252FXnapper-2024-10-31-13.33.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D417d9008-e6fa-488a-8927-9259a642efd2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d5f3287&sv=2)

Set the shape for grid to Circle.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#how-to-use-the-report-dashboard)

How to Use the Report Dashboard

Please check out the images below to see how to navigate and use the report dashboard effectively.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fc7qTGgl7HaKk1GqM9o3R%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-07%2520at%252020.39.19%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01816e8e-abff-4314-8f73-00378fd54f2e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=573537b2&sv=2)

Report dashboard in the first view

You can select different keywords to view their respective data.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FF4Mi80d2Rc4XmzTPP8gN%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-07%2520at%252021.07.07%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8b2f2da-fa31-444d-a209-c96e750ef1c7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e27b5297&sv=2)

Statistics of the current report:

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FLUhh2c7xOcKME75im53J%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-07%2520at%252020.51.07%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D283b1260-054b-4848-b22a-473ade822cf8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=943b914b&sv=2)

View statistics of the current report in the Overview tab.

Click on a grid point to view the competitors that are ranking at that specific location.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmLeEJy1L19AyACTUEyji%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-07%2520at%252021.14.21.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D808eaa5b-86be-4127-9c34-b13dde60bc94&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1f53411e&sv=2)

Click on a grid point to view more data.

You can navigate to the "Competitors" tab to view a list of competitors who are ranking for the selected keywords.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fac9ZvCTF04y753hQMfOJ%252FXnapper-2024-06-07-21.11.45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da374f332-87bb-4d3f-95e0-0b851247b6ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4bf4c707&sv=2)

View all competitors across all grid points in the current snapshot.

You can also click on the business name to see where your competitors rank on the map, making it easy to compare with your own ranking.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FwiJU8q9ZKoEnULS7l2Ob%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-11%2520at%252023.50.51.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06506417-f638-4f88-a97f-1c063fdfa3ed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f9b9ebcd&sv=2)

Click on the Business Name to view its ranking on the map.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#marker-and-map-interactions)

Marker & Map Interactions

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#moving-markers)

Moving Markers

You can move a marker by dragging and dropping it to a new position. You can also hold the **Shift** key to select and move multiple markers simultaneously.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FBswcNuP1fOn4VNaj6sk3%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-10%2520at%252021.23.05.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D12733b03-69c9-491b-af99-e457ad64f8b5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=928e8082&sv=2)

Moving markers around

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#bulk-delete-markers)

Bulk Delete Markers

You can hold the **Shift** key to select multiple markers and press the **Delete** or **Backspace** key to delete them all at once.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#use-measuring-tool)

Use Measuring Tool

[Since v1.30.0](https://help.seoutils.app/changelog#v1.30.0)
, you can measure the distance between two or multiple points on the map using the measuring tool.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FIMoKGEzvLmfYJhKVYrJR%252FCleanShot%25202025-05-30%2520at%252009.32.58.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D061d7702-cfc2-43dd-99ef-bd4f84e6a595&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d034b5a&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#expand-map)

Expand Map

If you need more space to work on the map, you can easily adjust it by following the instructions in the image below.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FRMw9NEF3ITclsxX8pRY2%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-10%2520at%252015.42.34.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6246f0dc-fa72-4c96-8dd8-ec632dbcd537&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aeef0d87&sv=2)

Expanding the map to have more space.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#birds-eye-view)

Bird's Eye View

This view provides an overview of the ranking and rank changes for all snapshots in your campaign through color progression. It displays data not just for your business, but also for your competitors.

It is compatible with both preset and custom grids.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FBqfjCCupE6gzLpd8zvIX%252FXnapper-2024-06-28-11.20.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D254effa2-0526-4c78-9a12-cbc0b38dd22c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=80323864&sv=2)

Bird's Eye View

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#manage-keywords)

Manage Keywords

You can easily manage your keywords in the **Manage Keywords** section—enable, disable, add, or delete them as needed.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fih2jOnh6xUsQNr9nJKPF%252FXnapper-2025-03-04-14.33.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6251f2b-7c4c-4d9b-a062-2d26c8113044&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39f1939&sv=2)

Manage Keywords

Disabled keywords are **excluded** from both scheduled and manual tracking.

Need to track a single keyword? Just use the filter to quickly disable all others, allowing you to run a snapshot for the one that matters most.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FyUMw52TQqk8k9I3lVR3I%252FXnapper-2025-03-03-16.32.11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29bbc87a-9aa1-4538-b8d2-2b2f68f07a4c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=76a2ad22&sv=2)

Bulk disable/enable keywords.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#export-your-reports)

Export Your Reports

You can export the Local Grid Report in PDF or HTML format. Additionally, you can personalize the report cover with your own branding.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#how-to-use-comparison-tool)

How to Use Comparison Tool

[In v1.18.2](https://help.seoutils.app/changelog#v1.18.2)
, I've just added a comparison tool to the GMB Rank Tracker. It's flexible, allowing you to compare rankings in different ways.

You can select the same snapshot and two different businesses to compare your rankings with competitors, or you can compare the same business across two snapshots to see how rankings change over time.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FqQdIGNfsNT2jygSHRUdQ%252FXnapper-2024-08-23-22.42.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D186e5d8e-55ca-4d77-999f-1b5ae3adf6f2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7970be91&sv=2)

3.  The change applies immediately to all ranking grids
    

**Note**: The glow effect is automatically removed when exporting reports to PDF to ensure clean, professional-looking documents. HTML exports will preserve the glow effect if enabled.

Snapshots Stuck When Using DataForSEO

If you’re using DataForSEO to scrape SERP data and notice some snapshots remain stuck loading for hours, you can resolve the issue using the “**Free Stuck GMB Rank Trackers**” tool.

Here’s how:

1\. Navigate to Service Settings > DataForSEO Settings.

2\. In the DataForSEO Actions dropdown, select “Free Stuck GMB Rank Trackers”

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F6eXmeblyuKC2fDalSaLp%252FCleanShot%25202024-12-02%2520at%252018.29.09%25202%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0434a1cb-39f2-48e7-b98b-e790d05453aa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=366190b8&sv=2)

Free Stuck GMB Rank Trackers tool

The process may take some time to complete, and you won’t be able to use the app until it finishes.
