# Embedding Database | SEO Utils

The **Embedding Database** feature lets you convert text into mathematical representations (embeddings) that capture semantic meaning. SEO Utils uses these embeddings to find similar content, group related topics, and perform intelligent analysis—even when the exact words don't match.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FgdLr79xFn5yrro371ddY%252FXnapper-2025-08-27-21.47.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D494e27ff-66d5-46a9-9492-d6818161e7e4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4507d5e8&sv=2)

Embedding Settings

With embeddings, you can discover that "best coffee shops NYC" and "top cafes in New York" are semantically similar, enabling smarter content grouping and analysis.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#why-use-embeddings)

Why Use Embeddings?

Traditional keyword matching only finds exact or partial text matches. Embeddings understand **meaning**, allowing SEO Utils to:

*   Group semantically related search queries
    
*   Find content gaps and opportunities
    
*   Build topical clusters based on actual intent
    
*   Analyze content relationships beyond keywords
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#supported-providers-and-models)

Supported Providers & Models

SEO Utils supports both **paid cloud models** and **free local models**, giving you flexibility based on your needs and budget.

**Cloud Models (OpenAI)**

*   [**Text Embedding 3 Small**](https://platform.openai.com/docs/models/text-embedding-3-small)
    **:** Multilingual, highly efficient, 5x cheaper than ada-002. 1536 dimensions, 8191 max tokens ($0.02 per 1M tokens)
    
*   [**Text Embedding 3 Large**](https://platform.openai.com/docs/models/text-embedding-3-large)
    **:** Multilingual, best accuracy, 54.9% MIRACL score. 3072 dimensions, 8191 max tokens ($0.13 per 1M tokens)
    

**Local Models (Ollama - Free)**

*   [**Nomic Embed Text v1.5**](https://ollama.com/library/nomic-embed-text)
    **:** English-focused, surpasses OpenAI ada-002 & text-embedding-3-small, local & free. 768 dimensions, 8192 max tokens
    
*   [**Nomic Embed Text v2 MoE (Q6\_K)**](https://ollama.com/toshk0/nomic-embed-text-v2-moe)
    **:** Multilingual (~100 languages), MoE architecture, 65.8 MIRACL score, local & free. 768 dimensions, 512 max tokens
    
*   [**Snowflake Arctic Embed v1**](https://ollama.com/library/snowflake-arctic-embed)
    **:** English-only, 334M BERT, optimized for retrieval, local & free. 1024 dimensions, 512 max tokens
    
*   [**Snowflake Arctic Embed v2**](https://ollama.com/library/snowflake-arctic-embed2)
    **:** Multilingual, 567M BERT, beats text-embedding-3-large on MTEB, MRL compression, local & free. 1024 dimensions, 8192 max tokens
    
*   [**mxbai-embed-large**](https://ollama.com/library/mxbai-embed-large)
    **:** English-only, 334M BERT, SOTA for its size, beats text-embedding-3-large, local & free. 1024 dimensions, 512 max tokens
    
*   [**BGE-M3 (BAAI)**](https://ollama.com/library/bge-m3)
    **:** Multilingual (100+ languages), 567M XLM-RoBERTa, dense+sparse+colbert retrieval, local & free. 1024 dimensions, 8192 max tokens
    

**Understanding Dimensions**

Embedding dimensions represent the size of the vector that stores semantic information. Think of it like image resolution—higher dimensions can capture more detail, but with tradeoffs:

*   **768 dimensions**: Fast and efficient, perfect for most keyword clustering and query grouping
    
*   **1024 dimensions**: Balanced performance, better for multilingual content and complex queries
    
*   **1536-3072 dimensions**: Maximum semantic detail, but requires more storage and slower searches
    

For most SEO tasks, 768-1024 dimensions provide excellent results. Higher dimensions are only needed for highly nuanced semantic analysis or when working with very similar content that requires fine-grained distinctions.

Local models run entirely on your computer—no API costs, no data sent to external servers. Perfect for privacy-conscious users or those processing large volumes of data.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#enable-embedding-database)

Enable Embedding Database

To start using embeddings, head to the left sidebar and click on "**Settings**," then navigate to "**Embedding**".

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FTRqwUauNCAAU5oBQidlT%252FXnapper-2025-08-27-21.48.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D473930bf-22ec-4380-89e7-c374571801aa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4080ee01&sv=2)

Access Embedding Settings

Next, toggle the "**Enable Embeddings**" master switch to activate the embedding system.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FjmHOzRFyng6u84ukcX7X%252FXnapper-2025-08-27-21.47.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab59d79b-f42a-4c51-bee1-d73614639989&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d519f162&sv=2)

Enable the embedding database

Once enabled, you'll see available features that can use embeddings. Each feature can use a different model based on your requirements.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#for-cloud-models-openai)

For Cloud Models (OpenAI)

1.  Ensure you have your OpenAI API key configured in the Services page
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FN1d4iqj4WH1vcQDAPX5u%252FXnapper-2025-08-27-22.00.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79256ff9-37b4-4d80-bc83-e60d75c8ef01&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e74838e5&sv=2)

1.  Select "OpenAI" as the provider
    
2.  Choose your preferred model (Text Embedding 3 Small recommended for most use cases)
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#for-local-models-ollama)

For Local Models (Ollama)

1.  Install Ollama on your computer from [ollama.com](https://ollama.com/)
    
2.  Open Terminal and pull the model you want to use:
    
    Copy
    
        ollama pull nomic-embed-text
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FFN9TZETth8JxySRGFVpK%252FXnapper-2025-08-27-22.02.23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D425a5572-9638-48b1-96d5-1477293827fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=def75c1a&sv=2)

1.  Ensure Ollama is running (it runs in the background by default)
    
2.  Select "Ollama" as the provider
    
3.  Choose from installed models (unavailable models will be disabled)
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FB3xWqlmPkQXsQDXadTbl%252FXnapper-2025-08-27-21.50.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b47bdeb-e4f1-42cc-b445-cd1a56ede064&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e6168b5c&sv=2)

Choose embedding model for each feature

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#how-embeddings-are-stored)

How Embeddings Are Stored

SEO Utils stores all generated embeddings in your local database. Once content is embedded, it won't be re-embedded again—saving API costs, processing time, and computational resources. This means you can experiment with different similarity thresholds and search queries without regenerating embeddings each time.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#understanding-similarity-scores)

Understanding Similarity Scores

When using semantic search in most of the semantic tools, you'll work with **similarity score thresholds** that control how closely items must match:

*   **Score range**: -1 to 1 (where 1 = identical meaning, 0 = unrelated, -1 = opposite meaning)
    
*   **Finding the right threshold**: Each model and dataset combination requires different thresholds
    
*   **Ollama models**: Typically need 0.8–0.9 for good matches with SEO data
    
*   **OpenAI models**: Often work well with 0.7–0.9 (higher dimensions allow slightly lower thresholds)
    
*   **Fine-tuning tip**: Use precise decimals (0.810, 0.825, 0.835) to find the sweet spot for your specific data
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FTHlRZXugAcKPJjGCferV%252FXnapper-2025-08-27-22.04.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9cd73700-06b6-4218-99cc-d431eaf6f5d7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e6dd8e65&sv=2)

Similarity threshold is used in the Topic Cluster tool of the Google Search Console Queries.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#available-features)

Available Features

Currently, SEO Utils uses embeddings for:

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#id-1.-google-search-console-queries-topic-clusters)

**1\. Google Search Console Queries -** [**Topic Clusters**](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console/topic-clusters)
**:**

Generate embeddings for your search queries to enable semantic clustering. Group related queries by topic to analyze their collective performance.

**Coming Soon**

*   Internal Linking Suggestions
    
*   Topical Map Builder
    
*   Semantic Clustering v3
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#how-to-choose-the-right-model)

How to Choose the Right Model

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#by-budget-and-privacy)

**By Budget & Privacy:**

*   **Zero cost + Maximum privacy:** Use Ollama models (all processing stays on your computer)
    
*   **Pay-as-you-go + Fast processing**: Use OpenAI models (data sent to OpenAI servers)
    
*   **Large volume processing**: Local models save money long-term despite slower speed
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#by-language-requirements)

**By Language Requirements:**

*   **English-only content**: Nomic Embed Text v1.5 (768D) or mxbai-embed-large (1024D)
    
*   **Multilingual content**: BGE-M3 or Snowflake Arctic Embed v2 (both support 100+ languages)
    
*   **Mixed content**: Text Embedding 3 Small offers good multilingual support with cloud speed
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#by-computer-specs)

**By Computer Specs:**

*   **Limited RAM (8GB)**: Use cloud models or stick to smaller embedding models (768D requires ~150MB per model)
    
*   **Standard specs (16GB RAM)**: Can run all embedding models comfortably (1024D models need ~400MB)
    
*   **Power users (32GB+ RAM)**: Run multiple models simultaneously or process large batches locally
    
*   **Apple Silicon (M1/M2/M3/M4)**: 3-5x faster than CPU-only, with M3/M4 delivering best performance for local models
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#by-use-case-complexity)

**By Use Case Complexity:**

*   **Basic keyword clustering**: 768D models (Nomic Embed Text) are sufficient
    
*   **Topic clustering & semantic search**: 1024D models provide better accuracy
    
*   **Fine-grained content analysis**: Consider 1536D+ models for nuanced distinctions
    
*   **Large query volumes (10,000+)**: Prioritize speed—use cloud models or accept longer processing
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/embedding-database#quick-recommendations)

**Quick Recommendations:**

*   **Most users**: Start with Nomic Embed Text (free, fast, good quality)
    
*   **Agencies with client data**: Use local models for privacy compliance
    
*   **High-volume operations**: OpenAI Text Embedding 3 Small balances cost and speed
    
*   **Maximum accuracy needed**: Text Embedding 3 Large or BGE-M3

# SERP Clustering | SEO Utils

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#how-does-the-serp-clustering-tool-work)

How Does the SERP Clustering Tool Work?

SEO Utils will cluster your keywords by scraping the search engine results page (SERP). If two keywords share more than four pages in search engine results (**similar results** on SERP), it will group them into a cluster.

Of course, you can adjust the **similar results number** from 3 to 7; the larger the number, the more relevant keywords are in a cluster.

The advantage of this method is that it leverages Google's ability to discern users' search intent. If Google shows many similar pages for two keywords, it indicates that Google recognizes these keywords as having the same search intent.

The only drawback is that it can be time-consuming for large keyword lists, as scraping SERPs is a detailed and cumbersome task.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#how-to-cluster-keywords-using-serp-clustering-tool)

How to Cluster Keywords Using SERP Clustering Tool

There are two main processes when the SERP Clustering tool runs:

1.  Scraping SERP data for all keywords.
    
2.  Running the [clustering algorithm](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#clustering-algorithm)
     after scrapping all SERP data.
    

To get started, head to the SERP Clustering in the left sidebar. Then, click the Cluster Keywords button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F3q2XhT4U4C1IoxLMrMx6%252FXnapper-2024-05-17-21.23.45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c2f3627-8736-4b09-8459-6855ba4b8016&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ee9621c&sv=2)

Access the SERP Clustering tool in the left sidebar

A modal will be opened; it should look like this. We will go over each setting one by one.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FAEqlvJI9Ap6gDXFBJfSO%252FXnapper-2024-06-24-21.54.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4803bdf-c3c2-452c-a0f8-f68776f59696&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1ab3bda4&sv=2)

SERP Clustering modal

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#keyword-files)

Keyword Files

SERP Clustering tool that lets you upload multiple files. It automatically combines the keywords and removes any duplicates. No need to mess with Excel anymore. This will save you some time.

After uploading files, you need to map the columns

*   **Keyword column:** This column is required.
    
*   **Search Volume column:** This is optional. You can map your external search volume, so you don't have to re-check the search volume for your keywords.
    

To map columns, click on the Column dropdown.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FOaDpRZdA3rVMfowFYv8F%252FXnapper-2024-05-17-21.35.41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2266710-7edc-403c-b78e-8b973e77c674&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=126e1806&sv=2)

Map the keyword column

SEO Utils also automap columns if your files have a guessable column name.

**Updated:** Since version 1.6.0, you can also map CPC and search intents columns.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#location-language)

Location / Language

Select the location that you want to target and the language of your keyword lists. SEO Utils uses this field for checking keyword search volume in most cases.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#geo-target-optional)

Geo Target (Optional)

This field allows for more precise geotargeting when scraping SERP. You can type a specific location like a city, country, etc.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FM0xdTatAir6w8S08mG6D%252FXnapper-2024-05-17-21.43.37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03e1c0c5-354e-4379-9f30-3e0e717bd4f6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=846488f&sv=2)

You can type a city name like Seattle

When using this field, SEO Utils will ignore the location that you selected from the **Location / Language** field.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#desktop-devices)

Desktop Devices

SEO Utils will check search results for desktop devices. If you want to check for mobile devices, please disable this setting.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#check-keyword-metrics)

Check Keyword Metrics

SEO Utils will use DataForSEO to check keyword metrics. This helps determine the **primary keyword** for a cluster, so it's recommended to enable this setting.

However, if your uploaded files already have search volume data and you mapped the Volume or CPC column, you can turn off this setting to save money.

**Tip**: If your uploaded files don't have enough search volume data for all keywords, you can turn on the "Check Search Volume" field. SEO Utils only check the search volume for **keywords that are missing data**.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#cluster-strategy)

Cluster Strategy

When setting the primary keyword for clusters, SEO Utils will use the keyword that has the most search volume in a cluster, however, some users have mentioned that setting the primary keyword for a cluster based on Cost Per Click (CPC) provides better results when your keywords are transactional or commercial. You can now select the Cluster Strategy to use CPC instead.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FKhFIrs3kEjuyiPmIz0Z0%252FXnapper-2024-06-20-15.58.20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d956cc8-1303-4ef1-a769-d9d4d73f25a2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8688d0c1&sv=2)

Using CPC to set the primary keyword for clusters.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#clustering-algorithm)

Clustering Algorithm

Since [version 1.30.0](https://help.seoutils.app/changelog#v1.30.0)
, SEO Utils offers three different clustering algorithms to suit different needs:

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FErpkLOB72QqSi2Uu41sn%252FCleanShot%25202025-05-28%2520at%252012.01.49%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ab41193-8d04-427d-834f-c0f9e63729c7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7068a40c&sv=2)

Select the clustering algorithm that best fits your needs

**Default Algorithm**

*   Groups keywords if they share X URLs with the primary keyword (highest search volume/CPC)
    
*   Creates broader topic clusters
    
*   Best for content hubs and category planning
    
*   Fastest processing speed
    

**Strict Algorithm**

*   Groups keywords only if ALL keywords in the cluster share X URLs with each other
    
*   Creates very tight, highly relevant clusters
    
*   Best for precise content targeting
    
*   **Limitation**: May result in many single-keyword clusters due to "first-mover advantage"
    

**Balanced Strict Algorithm**

*   Solves the Strict algorithm's limitation by using progressive thresholds
    
*   Small clusters (2-5 keywords): requires 100% match (like Strict)
    
*   Medium clusters (6-10): requires 80% match
    
*   Large clusters (11+): requires 60% match
    
*   **Why it's needed**: Prevents clusters from becoming "too strict" as they grow larger
    
*   Best balance between quality and natural cluster growth
    

**Why Balanced Strict was created**: The original Strict algorithm has a "first-mover advantage" problem where early keywords easily join clusters, but later keywords struggle to match ALL members in larger clusters. This often results in many single-keyword clusters. Balanced Strict solves this by relaxing requirements as clusters grow, allowing natural expansion while maintaining quality.

**How to Choose**:

*   **Default**: When you need broad topic grouping or have 100,000+ keywords
    
*   **Strict**: When you need very precise clusters for competitive niches
    
*   **Balanced Strict**: When you want quality clusters that can still grow naturally (recommended for most users)
    

**Processing Time Comparison**

The more advanced algorithms take longer to process due to additional quality checks:

Dataset Size

Default Algorithm

Strict/Balanced Strict

Time Difference

1,000 keywords

1-2 seconds

3-5 seconds

2-3x slower

10,000 keywords

5-10 seconds

15-30 seconds

2-3x slower

50,000 keywords

1-2 minutes

5-10 minutes

3-5x slower

100,000 keywords

5-10 minutes

20-40 minutes

4-5x slower

**Performance Note**: Strict and Balanced Strict algorithms require more processing time but produce higher quality clusters. For very large datasets (100,000+ keywords), consider using the Default algorithm or breaking your keywords into smaller batches.

SEO Utils' clustering algorithm is designed to handle large-scale keyword datasets efficiently. You can cluster between 50,000 to 200,000 keywords at once—a capability not many tools on the market offer. Most other tools typically allow clustering of only 5,000 to 10,000 keywords at a time.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#similar-results-on-serps)

Similar Results on SERPs

The value range is from **3 to 7**. For example, if you set this field to 4, SEO Utils will group 2 keywords into a cluster if they have at least **4 common URLs on SERPs**. The larger the number, the more relevant keywords are in a cluster.

**Tip**: The recommended value is 4, but you are free to test a different value by using the ["Re-cluster keywords" button](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#re-cluster-keywords)
.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#use-saved-serp-data-for-x-days)

Use Saved SERP Data For X Days

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FpOJXSSdK6T4cGhL49aNo%252FXnapper-2024-05-17-22.01.13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D826124a6-e1cc-43bc-8f4a-f5348a1773de&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dbd61d7a&sv=2)

Enter the number of days you wish to use previously saved SERP data. By setting this duration, you can speed up the clustering process and save money as SEO Utils will reuse existing data without the need to re-scrape.

Choose a number that best balances freshness of data with processing speed.

Set '0' to always scrape fresh SERP data.

**Tip**: This field is a great method for testing **Similar Results on SERPs** value since you don't have to re-scrape SERP data for all keywords.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#scrape-serp-with)

Scrape SERP With

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FNMHpBYi1fgqvgtU2GLgP%252FXnapper-2024-05-17-22.03.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1412eb2a-5219-4ae0-9ed3-0306daec436e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58d8ff2c&sv=2)

Select a method to scrape SERP

There are 3 options for now:

*   **My IP:** SEO Utils use your IP to scrape SERP data. This is not recommended if you have over 100 keywords.
    
*   **Proxies:** Use proxies to scrape SERP data. See how to set up a proxy [here](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-use-proxies)
    .
    
*   **SERP API: DataForSEO:** Use SERP API from DataForSEO to scrape SERP data.
    

We will focus on Proxies & SERP API, so you can determine which method is best fit for you.

**SERP API Method**

DataForSEO provides a reliable API to scrape SERP data with 3 modes:

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmEg3rj1kVRsIvU5lIxIc%252FXnapper-2024-05-17-22.10.22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25e361fb-f888-48af-887c-2dd3cde03927&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1cb3e22e&sv=2)

3 modes

Since the Live mode is expensive, so SEO Utils doesn't support it. After selecting the SERP API method, you will able to select the mode in the **Priority** field.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fqsj698sLcQTNfze1n6Av%252FXnapper-2024-05-17-22.11.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D646004f3-1ad3-4a74-bd9f-41b5a8e17dd3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cfad7c82&sv=2)

Select a mode

I recommend using the **normal execution priority (Standard Queue)** option. I have tested to cluster 2,000 keywords, and it only took about 12 minutes to finish all processes. [See the video here](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#video-running-serp-clustering-on-2-000-keywords-with-serp-api)
.

It only costs **$0.6 to scrape SERP & cluster 1,000 keywords**. This rate is much cheaper when compared to other tools on the market, which usually cost **$7-$12 for 1,000 keywords**.

Yes, you read that right! It's 11 times cheaper✌️.

In v1.21.0, I added a cost estimation tool for the SERP API, allowing you to see the actual cost after deducting keywords that use saved SERP data. Please [click here](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#cost-estimation-tool-for-serp-api-method)
 to learn more about it.

**Important:**

To use the SERP API, you must have your own DataForSEO account. [Renting API key services](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/rent-dataforseo-api-key)
 isn't viable because DataForSEO restricts certain endpoints that I utilized to implement the Queue mode. If multiple users rely on a rented API key from my account, it will slow down the process for everyone. For the quickest results, using your own DataForSEO account is the best approach.

**Proxies Method**

If you need to cluster 1 million keywords per month, using the SERP API Method would indeed be costly, amounting to $600.

This is where the Proxies method becomes valuable. By using your own proxies, you can significantly reduce the costs associated with such large-scale keyword clustering.

You can pay about **$80-$100** per month for a rotating residential proxy and you can cluster **millions of keywords**.

However, this method has more fields to set up.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FHBpEcXPtYGNsCdr7yIUH%252FXnapper-2024-05-17-22.50.14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D439fcd43-bb2b-4c25-af39-1bf4b9d49286&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=45de1627&sv=2)

3 important fields for Proxies method

**Workers**

This is the number of concurrent requests SEO Utils will scrape SERP. You can enter from 1-50. If you have a good proxy provider, you can set it to 50 (my setting), so SEO Utils can send 50 requests in one second to scrape SERP data. This will increase the clustering process a lot.

If you are unsure about your proxy quality, go with 5-10 workers first.

**Request Delay**

Enter the number of seconds you wish to have between each request to scrape SERP data for keywords. The more delay time you set, the slower the process will be, but it will help you avoid being blocked by Google.

Set '0' to scrape SERP data without any delay.

For example, if you set **Workers** to 10 and **Request Delay** to 1 second. SEO Utils will send 10 requests and then sleep for one second before sending another 10 requests.

**Back-off Time**

Enter the number of seconds you wish to wait before retrying the failed scraping request. SEO Utils retries the request up to 3 times before skipping a keyword. The more back-off time you set, the slower the process will be, but it will help you avoid being blocked by Google.

For example, if you set **Workers** to 10, **Request Delay** to 1 second, and **Back-off Time** to 2 seconds. SEO Utils will send 10 requests and then sleep for one second before sending another 10 requests. However, while processing, if one request in 10 requests is failed, it will sleep for **2 seconds (back-off time)** before retrying the failed request.

SEO Utils will retry a maximum of **three times** before skipping scraping a keyword. That keyword will end up with no SERP data.

If you set the **Back-off Time** to '0', SEO Utils will use the default back-off time:

*   1 second for the 1st attempt
    
*   2 seconds for the 2nd attempt.
    
*   3 seconds for the 3rd attempt.
    

Feel free to experiment with different settings for your proxies and usage. When testing these settings, as long as you don't encounter a "Too Many Requests" error message, it should indicate that your setup is functioning correctly.

Since SEO Utils automatically retries each request up to three times, you might see a message like:

`Attempt 1 failed to scrape SERP for keyword 'keyword': failed to visit URL: Too Many Requests.`

Don't worry if you see this message. SEO Utils will try two more times, so everything is still fine unless you see a failure message on the third attempt.

SERP API

Proxies

Use when clustering **thousands** of keywords per month

Use when clustering **millions** of keywords per month

Less configuration and testing

More configuration and testing

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#re-cluster-keywords)

Re-cluster Keywords

After clustering keywords, you can visit the report and re-cluster keywords.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FMUCKuip3LTlbFJmhsEZr%252FXnapper-2024-05-17-23.20.37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e2c9e21-85a8-48d6-af05-2213f55c6030&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=52a7ac3e&sv=2)

Click the Re-cluster Keywords button to re-cluster all keywords in the report

You might need to re-cluster keywords in the following situations:

*   When testing the **Similar Results field on SERPs** field.
    
*   If you're adding more keywords to a report and need to cluster them with existing ones.
    
*   To monitor the clusters before and after Google Core Updates to observe any impact.
    
*   If some keywords are missing SERP data because some SERP scraping requests were failed.
    

SEO Utils will show this message if some keywords in your report are missing SERP data, so you know to re-run the clustering process.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fs1wsUY7SJI94ZCmwpjSL%252FXnapper-2024-05-17-23.28.20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd8add45-8582-42f3-94ce-ee730eb10aa8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8bbb127&sv=2)

When re-clustering keywords, make sure you use the "[**Use Saved SERP Data For X Days**](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#use-saved-serp-data-for-x-days)
" field. This ensures that SEO Utils won't re-scrape SERP data, saving time and resources.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#distribute-keywords-into-existing-clusters-available-since-v1.16.0)

Distribute Keywords into Existing Clusters (Available since v1.16.0)

When re-clustering keywords, you'll be able to distribute new and non-clustered keywords into existing clusters, rather than rebuilding all clusters from scratch.

This is particularly useful if you've already used clusters to create articles on your website and you just want to add new keywords to existing articles (clusters).

A **"New" badge** will highlight these newly added keywords, and a **"Run #" label** will indicate which clustering run they were added in.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FWmQpjuw8afnoDvuFeotu%252F448666243_7699027523499742_768845294393561290_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4eab8e5-6561-4db4-87b3-6e950f1cc3f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=79e75a7f&sv=2)

Enable the setting to distribute keywords into existing clusters

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fbnu4CucCf0Iy9UWIZfnv%252F448646536_7699027720166389_2702349076745059710_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D104a8951-f23b-49fa-880f-c4e4b47e3428&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2def203&sv=2)

The "New" badge will help you determine the latest keywords just added to a cluster.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#analyzing-serp)

Analyzing SERP

After clustering your keywords, you can analyze the SERPs of the clustered keywords to see how your competitors are performing. This analysis can show you their monthly traffic, the keywords they rank for, and how many backlinks they have.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FvpVyseDSpB48VW4vQ4SV%252FXnapper-2024-05-18-12.34.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc929d6bf-e6f3-4dcd-bd82-7d7687868632&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fd2ffeac&sv=2)

Click the vertical three dots icon to start analyzing SERP

You can choose the type of metric and specify the number of URLs on the SERP for each keyword you want to run the analysis for.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F8XZ9nP5cQn4dxhrMVlLM%252FXnapper-2024-05-18-12.38.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D465b53c9-1349-48bc-bb90-a2409c026b9e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0515837&sv=2)

Analyze SERP for selected keywords

After analysis, you can click on a keyword to view the SERP data with all metrics including traffic, backlinks, referring domains, spam score, keywords, etc for that keyword.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FneVVyowlLNJU7AVfPrXT%252FXnapper-2024-05-18-12.44.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b64207d-f05b-4ccd-bfd3-9347f0f2e5e4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bb771557&sv=2)

SERP data for the keyword "vodka cocktails," including backlinks and traffic data

The analyzed data is also included in the exported file under the second tab labeled "SERP Data."

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F9I1EPRQkH4S2tQ3OkUMv%252FXnapper-2024-05-18-12.54.08.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c16de36-720e-4fa6-a521-3a7b7225a480&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6e6f33cc&sv=2)

All backlinks & traffic data are included in the SERP data sheet

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#ranking-data)

Ranking Data

You can add a target domain to a SERP Clustering report. This will show you the ranking data of that domain across all clusters, helping you identify which clusters you are ranking well in and which ones need improvement. This feature allows you to prioritize your efforts to boost your rankings effectively.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FSB3QKu3XvJtZ5uRlFajQ%252FXnapper-2024-06-21-16.48.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D857c2482-a70f-46aa-b5dd-3f9767f6c857&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b98571da&sv=2)

Ranking data will be shown in the table after adding a target domain

When viewing the SERP of a keyword, the target domain will be marked in green color.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fvvk1iQD8Q9xwUTmEDrSq%252FXnapper-2024-06-21-16.49.10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6194897b-78c4-4f47-b483-657bb1733792&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43f9c81c&sv=2)

Target domain in SERP table

**Tip:** You can also change the target domain to a competitor's domain to see how well they are performing across different clusters. This can help you identify their strengths and areas where you might have an advantage.

SEO Utils also provides some metric cards to show you the cluster's key ranking data at a glance:

*   View and filter the number of ranking clusters.
    
*   View and filter the number of clusters without rankings.
    
*   See and filter the rank distribution across clusters.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FNCECWuX1VWZDKzo3E98x%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-23%2520at%252022.35.45%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D399a5dc6-74bc-44ba-a07b-db4d14d1f18d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88248d20&sv=2)

Metric cards and filters

You can watch the video below to see the "Ranking Data" feature in action.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#cost-estimation-tool-for-serp-api-method)

Cost Estimation Tool for SERP API Method

When using the SERP API to scrape SERP data, you can click the “Estimate Cost” button to view the actual cost. SEO Utils will read all keywords in your uploaded file, remove duplicates, and exclude keywords that already have saved SERP data, providing you with an accurate final cost.

In the screenshot below, I uploaded over **18,000 keywords** and used SERP data from the past 7 days. The cost came to just **$0.0390**, saving me **$11.2470**! SEO Utils only sent **65 keywords** to the SERP API for new data, as most of the keywords already had recent SERP data within 7 days.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fw4d5ARFO4QVfxfQMJWII%252F464919090_8563919223677230_7461303937806986891_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D782ffea3-b6ff-4b7c-9d91-843fc2b6a7e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d4b41e64&sv=2)

Cost estimation tool for SERP API.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/serp-clustering#video-running-serp-clustering-on-2-000-keywords-with-serp-api)

# Auto-Indexing Tool | SEO Utils

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#set-up-the-web-search-indexing-api-and-google-service-accounts)

Set up the Web Search Indexing API and Google Service Accounts.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#step-1-enable-the-web-search-indexing-api)

Step 1: Enable the Web Search Indexing API

Visit the Google Cloud Console at [https://console.cloud.google.com/](https://console.cloud.google.com/)
 and create a Project.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FbRVrZN84EADKlgKIL1eb%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.42.13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69f75556-50b5-424c-a776-f7da2e68cd26&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94cb8741&sv=2)

Create a project on Google Cloud Console

In the top search bar, type "API" and select "Enabled APIs & services".

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FneP1uy7uHC7NzYPFn6rC%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.44.04.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D571f9769-1be9-4c38-8d56-5fb8672b63e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=960f56&sv=2)

Select "Enabled APIs & services"

Click "Library" on the left sidebar.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fe3DpdROFizcIOn4XbGdN%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.46.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8dfaaf4-4251-4eb8-99ef-e850a465c56c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6b79dc19&sv=2)

Select "Library"

Search for "**Web Search Indexing API**" in the top search bar and enable it, so you can access it with your Google Service Account

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FijAhLeAmRZC9OUyeDVtF%252FXnapper-2024-02-21-14.34.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0f4deca-caee-4f76-822d-a5639681f0e9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=980d2ea2&sv=2)

Enable the Web Search Indexing API

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#step-2-create-a-google-service-account)

Step 2: Create a Google Service Account

In your [Google Cloud Console](https://console.cloud.google.com/)
 dashboard, search for "**Service Accounts**" and click on it.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmrOPpnyFrMmJv10a9x64%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.51.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30a4be9a-68ae-404c-8c58-012cf3800d93&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebbdd184&sv=2)

Click on "Service Accounts"

Hit the "Create Service Account" button, and enter a service account name. Then, hit the "Done" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F8BZcb1ypyh8Ad9NTSSzu%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.56.52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f9ac3c6-f892-4abe-a854-5c12d4fa7269&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90c2ee27&sv=2)

Enter service account name

Copy the email of the service account.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmH3imZtv2LAixBDJgEKx%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-17.58.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47414ef3-a8a3-42c9-96f1-f0bb45ac3621&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36bdf91f&sv=2)

Copy the email

Click on the Service Account's email, select the "**KEYS**" tab, then click the "**Create new key**" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fw7wIRfDeN0xBmZRaxb40%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.08.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddfc0a806-9d8c-4e00-8fa5-9815dd29d125&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e5d4ca5&sv=2)

Create a key for your service account

A model will pop up. Select "JSON" and click the "Create" button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FJf05NYUF1BLxX1oQu33F%252FXnapper-2023-11-30-18.10.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0984450d-e091-4dc9-91d4-e162311e1803&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a864c6f&sv=2)

Select JSON in Key type field.

After creating the key, Google will download it to your machine. Keep that file. We will need it in Step 3.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#step-3-add-the-google-search-console-to-seo-utils)

Step 3: Add the Google Search Console to SEO Utils

Access the **Google Service Accounts** menu from the App dropdown at the top-right corner.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F59wWXHJmCJyltn1QUF6b%252FXnapper-2024-02-21-14.41.52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d4954b6-8b3d-48ae-ba74-e214cd179b73&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=391cf4e7&sv=2)

Access the Google Service Accounts menu

Then, click the **Add Account** button, and select the JSON file that you downloaded in Step 2 to add a new account.

**Google Indexing API Rate Limit**

Google only allows you to submit 200 URLs per day via the Indexing API. There are 2 ways to bypass this.

1.  [Request more quota](https://developers.google.com/search/apis/indexing-api/v3/quota-pricing)
    .
    
2.  Create multiple projects and Google Service Accounts by repeating Step 1 to Step 3. Please note that you have to create a new project and then create a new Google Service Account in that new project because Google limits the API usage per project, not per Google Service Account.
    

After creating an account, please copy the Google Service Account email address.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FBzjEktv97hFoTPTjT5Xv%252FXnapper-2024-02-21-14.57.37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc37ce2d3-7aa7-4661-95f0-2df80e1e11c0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58b72061&sv=2)

Copy the Google Service Account email address

Visit your Google Search Console, select the site that you want to submit for indexing. Click on **Settings** > **Users and Permissions**.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FXpLWgcjj3av4sN5GmvYf%252FXnapper-2024-02-21-15.02.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D617993dd-6a58-4fa8-808c-fda6c70a2f37&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c6ec039d&sv=2)

Click the "**Add User**" button, then paste the Google Service Account that you copied previously. Select "Owner" permission for the new user.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FmkK4HOOi3V4PRDQdcYkf%252FXnapper-2024-02-21-15.04.49.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1031e819-837e-42cf-8349-f1602fb06c07&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8473bcd8&sv=2)

Add a new user

If you have multiple Google Service Accounts, you will need to add multiple users.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#connect-your-google-search-console-sites-and-sitemaps)

Connect your Google Search Console Sites & Sitemaps

If you haven't connected a site on your Google Search Console, please follow [this guide](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-search-console)
 to do that.

After connecting a site, SEO Utils will pull all the sitemaps that you entered on your Google Search Console.

If you haven't added a sitemap to your Google Search Console account, you can add sitemaps manually on SEO Utils

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FuagM7HbzC6gFbQxiwpWs%252FXnapper-2024-02-21-15.18.08.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D082132ff-0f0c-41ce-9a89-fb6905e5bee7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ee0b3d4a&sv=2)

Add a sitemap manually.

You can add as many sitemaps as you want.

After adding sitemaps, you can fetch all URLs from them by clicking the "**Fetch URLs From All Sitemaps**" action. SEO Utils will pull all URLs from all sitemaps and check the index of every single URL.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FuqRYhi322iqqKY2zu7n6%252FXnapper-2024-02-23-18.23.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90e4b134-ab66-497f-8be4-66264f5ef926&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=558e47dc&sv=2)

Fetch URLs From All Sitemaps

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#checking-index)

Checking Index

You can trigger a process to bulk-check the index for all URLs on your site by clicking the **Check Index** action.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FwP4CXu2DPKDC5HvVMrtB%252FXnapper-2024-02-23-18.28.56.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74b01e38-c2e9-417f-9a08-ea7fa219fd71&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=470241a3&sv=2)

Bulk-check index

You can also check index for a single URL by clicking the vertical dots icon.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FtAhtFwCmCbdcNaZWEfwk%252FXnapper-2024-02-23-18.31.16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fa28ead-6de6-4ec5-91a5-8010794fcd7f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=723d98c1&sv=2)

Check index for a URL

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#two-checking-index-methods)

Two Checking Index Methods

**#1. Using Google Search Console API (default)**

Since March 4, 2024, SEO Utils has supported checking index by using [Search Console URL Inspection API](https://developers.google.com/search/blog/2022/01/url-inspection-api)
. This method has some pros when compared to method #2 which uses the "site:url" operator.

*   Do not require proxies, so no extra cost.
    
*   Faster, can check 10 URLs per second.
    
*   Easy to set up, just need to enable the Google Search Console API.
    

However, there are some [quota limits](https://developers.google.com/webmaster-tools/limits#url-inspection)
. The quota is enforced per Search Console [website property](https://support.google.com/webmasters/answer/34592)
 (calls querying the same site):

*   2,000 queries per day
    
*   600 queries per minute
    

So if you reach the limit, you might want to switch to the #2 method.

Moreover, the Google Search Console API method also gives you [some extra information](https://developers.google.com/webmaster-tools/v1/urlInspection.index/UrlInspectionResult)
 that the second method doesn't provide like

*   Indexing State
    
*   Coverage State
    
*   Crawled Date
    

You can hover on the blue "info" icon to see that information.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FIZhZaOTbxbqJMgrspZQ4%252FXnapper-2024-03-04-15.25.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09949613-ae21-4a47-b932-f0c17a35e826&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=952fc947&sv=2)

Extra information that the first method gives you.

There is a filter for the Indexing State, so you can tell why the URL is not allowed to be indexed.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Femu4leIbwli1JL0OsWmn%252FXnapper-2024-03-04-15.30.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73846fc0-4050-4191-9563-f9dc49b9dc96&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef49e86a&sv=2)

**#2. Using the "site:url" Operator**

When using this method, SEO Utils will search Google using the "site:url" operator to see if the URL is on the SERP.

This method doesn't have a quota limit but you want to consider [using Proxies](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-use-proxies)
 to prevent Google from blocking your IP when checking thousands of URLs.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#switching-method)

Switching Method

You can click on the "cog icon" button to switch the method. The method is saved on the site scope, which means you can use method #1 for site A and method #2 for site B.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fc8JOsu8KPk74Y59MwU9c%252FXnapper-2024-03-04-15.31.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4994da48-1412-45de-823c-a606838c2727&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8865266&sv=2)

Switching checking index method.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FgyB4XVlnKgiVa7mbATra%252FXnapper-2024-03-04-15.33.56.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0ac915a-b618-4080-841c-0e67a96be547&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7f6cb3e&sv=2)

Click the "Update" button to save the settings.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#submitting-index)

Submitting Index

Just like the "Check Index" action, you can submit either multiple URLs or just one URL for indexing.

When you bulk-submit URLs, SEO Utils will submit all URLs regardless of their indexed or submitted status.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#auto-index-feature)

Auto Index Feature

SEO Utils provides an auto-pilot mode so you don't need to pull URLs from sitemaps, check & submit index manually.

To enable the Auto Index feature of a site, please ensure that you toggle the **Auto Index** field on.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FG37V8O7jvENEX5694NBs%252FXnapper-2024-02-25-09.38.00.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2eebd95d-57b0-45b8-a199-7072784f1869&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3fabb1f&sv=2)

Enable Auto Index for sites

You can also enable the Auto Index feature for specific sitemaps by visiting the Sitemaps list page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fmn9c5wULnHVM7Ptzba11%252FXnapper-2024-02-25-09.40.00.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daad21c24-c1fd-4639-aa4a-cd4ebb52516a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6beb6636&sv=2)

Enable Auto Index for all URLs of a specific sitemap

You can tell if a URL is enabled for auto-indexing if the URL is yellow like this.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FgHLr9SRmhmS0Lp0da2TX%252FXnapper-2024-02-25-09.50.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe585caa-8309-495e-aa97-6156976e7421&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca0e4704&sv=2)

URLs are disabled for auto-indexing

When URLs are disabled for auto-indexing, SEO Utils won't automatically check and submit them for indexing. However, you still can manually do that by using "**Check Index**" & "**Submit Index**" actions.

To use the Auto Index feature, you need to keep SEO Utils running on your machine or use a VPS, so you don't need to keep your computer on constantly.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#auto-pull-urls-from-sitemaps)

Auto Pull URLs From Sitemaps

SEO Utils will pull URLs from all sitemaps daily at **5:00 AM (your local time)** to get new URLs and check if the existing URLs have content updated by using the Last Mod field.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FRziTikavpVSLV8rjsDVe%252FXnapper-2024-02-25-10.00.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5cafbfc2-35f9-4cb4-9ca3-738fd805748a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=91bd62b5&sv=2)

Using Last Mod field to detect if the content of a URL is updated.

If a URL has updated content, SEO Utils will resubmit it for indexing, regardless of the submission status.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#auto-check-index)

Auto Check Index

SEO Utils will check index of all sites that enable the Auto Index feature at **6:00 AM (your local time).**

**Note:** It will skip the URLs that belong to a sitemap with the Auto-Index setting turned off.

Please consider [using Proxies](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/how-to-use-proxies)
 if you have many URLs to check index.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#auto-submit-index)

Auto Submit Index

SEO Utils will submit for indexing all sites that enable the Auto Index feature **every 10 minutes**.

**Note:**

*   It will skip the URLs that belong to a sitemap with the Auto-Index setting turned off.
    
*   The auto-pilot mode only submits URLs that have already been checked for indexing. You don't have a setting to ignore this behavior like when running the "**Submit Index**" action manually.
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#override-the-auto-mode-behavior)

Override the Auto-Mode Behavior

This is the default behavior of the Auto-mode

*   **Checking index**: If a URL is already **indexed**, it won't re-check index for that URL in the subsequent runs.
    
*   **Submitting index**: If a URL is already **submitted** or **indexed**, it won't re-submit that URL in the subsequent runs.
    

If you would like to override those behaviors, please open the Site setting modal.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FVfQm8KdDvmfMUOdUcocx%252FXnapper-2024-04-24-20.50.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d547b27-08be-4dbf-95f2-3d02eb0b6344&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f4d64388&sv=2)

Open the setting modal.

You will see 2 fields:

*   **Auto Recheck Index After** field: You can specify the number of days to recheck the index even if the URL is already indexed.
    
*   **Auto Resubmit Index After** field: You can specify the number of days to resubmit URLs even if URLs are already submitted but not indexed.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F7QhiHin1vJyHP29Euoez%252FXnapper-2024-04-24-20.54.07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35cf4580-5c4d-4a3a-bf53-d0c719860aeb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=521fcbf0&sv=2)

Override the Auto-mode behavior

Those two fields will only be shown if you **turn on the Auto mode** for the site.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#quick-tips)

Quick Tips

You can view all the logs of check and submit for indexing of each URL by clicking the log bar at the bottom.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F0zYB0eu21zxLAwlTSxfj%252FXnapper-2024-02-25-10.18.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c29b8e0-48b7-4b9d-93f9-c04e5c855d44&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=83466a4b&sv=2)

View logs

You can quickly switch between pages on a site by using the dropdown menu in the header section.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FsBFOJOlYFpCdxf6kzZou%252FXnapper-2024-02-25-10.43.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba5367d9-90e3-47db-ae10-f63b925bfbf2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=934b570b&sv=2)

Quickly move to a page

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/auto-indexing-tool#updates-on-march-22-2024)

Updates on March 22, 2024

You can now set which Google service accounts you want to use on specific sites.

For example, if you set up a Google Search Account can be used on site A. SEO Utils will only use that account to check & submit index for that site only.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FSnebLdb4hgEGvBkWtxoL%252F431388398_7260302147372284_1054525268246411615_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a68404e-77fb-4fda-b6bf-c014710a0014&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58312d4e&sv=2)

Set site scopes for each Google Service Account

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FLDQdYRhqIEwCEZHREr3I%252F431629039_7260302684038897_1728235001124597070_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4b808a3-1edf-448b-a724-fca41fc11c5c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86e5bfa7&sv=2)

Select a site where you want to use the Google Service Account.

# White-labeled Client Report | SEO Utils

This feature lets you generate a white-labeled client report. You can customize it with your company logo, domain, and even add a password for security. Simply share the link with your client so they can view their ranking data directly.

**Note:** _This is an optional feature, available in_ [v1.29.0 or above](http://help.seoutils.app/changelog#v1.29.0)
.

**Shared report demo:** [https://share.seoutils.app/gb/920d3d27-49b1-4a05-9436-b1087e633ec7/timeline](https://share.seoutils.app/gb/920d3d27-49b1-4a05-9436-b1087e633ec7/timeline)

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#how-does-it-work)

How Does It Work?

When you enable sharing on a report, SEO Utils will automatically sync it to the cloud and generate a shareable link. You can send this link to your client or [embed the report](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#embed-report)
 directly on your website or dashboard.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FoJrf0V6FBywZ5Jv9vVV1%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-10.03.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De785c505-e679-4174-83cf-437681e1e64c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4020f5ed&sv=2)

Enable sharing on a report.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#register-a-cloud-database)

Register a Cloud Database

To share reports via the cloud, you’ll need to register a cloud database. Just head over to [http://share.seoutils.app/register](http://share.seoutils.app/register)
 to create an account.

Once you’re registered, go to your [SEO Utils Share Dashboard](https://share.seoutils.app/dashboard)
 and subscribe to the “Shareable Report Link” plan to enable cloud sharing.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FnQL1mvr3SNzAfPP1d2AX%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-10.09.22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c95e088-9572-4fe2-acba-014baf692350&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58b4975f&sv=2)

Subscribe to the "Shareable Report Link" plan.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#why-is-there-an-extra-monthly-fee-for-this-feature)

**Why is there an extra monthly fee for this feature?**

This feature is completely optional. You only need it if you want to share cloud-hosted reports with your clients. Without it, you can still use SEO Utils as usual with no limitations.

The extra fee covers the cost of securely storing and delivering your reports from a cloud database. It’s the minimum amount needed to help me maintain the service and cover cloud provider costs.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#create-an-api-key)

Create an API key

To start sharing your reports, you’ll need to create an API key.

1.  Go to API Tokens from the user menu in the left sidebar, or visit: [https://share.seoutils.app/user/api-tokens](https://share.seoutils.app/user/api-tokens)
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F0nqEBDLXpXRwqQ0ahTYj%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-10.17.46.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83fa1f24-9e6a-4da8-8350-6051e1c2422a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bcab13cc&sv=2)

Visit the API Tokens page.

1.  Enter a name for your API key and click Create.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FPXK4XdcDrSJD3PeObKdd%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-10.20.58.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3a26097-053c-4cf6-b203-04786834b0ef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9727fede&sv=2)

Create an API key

1.  Copy the generated API token.
    

Next, open the **SEO Utils desktop app**:

1.  Go to the Services page in the left sidebar. Scroll down to **Shareable Report Settings**.
    
2.  Paste the API token into the field labeled “**SEO Utils Shareable API Key**”.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FJ96yQVTr4r48bMlLdtmq%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-10.23.25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2d45d3e-30b7-40d3-83a2-66e886f72c45&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0505799&sv=2)

Paste the API key in the SEO Utils app.

That’s it! 🎉 You’re now ready to share your reports with clients.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#share-gmb-rank-tracker-reports)

Share GMB Rank Tracker Reports

To share a GMB Rank Tracker report in the SEO Utils desktop app:

1.  Open the report you want to share.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FEo6EiL49DBC64mOgSVpr%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-10.30.07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31f78bae-3cc3-427f-82fb-247a8af79a04&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2ff1342e&sv=2)

Access the "Share" action.

1.  Click the Actions dropdown and select the "**Share**" action. This will open the Share Report modal:
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FD3Q7bQSJySnIkym6LPNz%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-10.37.41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5980721-f409-4217-9fcc-7c2d4bc928fd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=adab6bec&sv=2)

Share Report modal

Toggle the “**Share Report**” switch to enable or disable sharing for that specific report.

You can also set a password to protect the report. Your client will need to enter this password to view the report.

If password protection is enabled, the [embed code](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#embed-report)
 will be disabled.

That’s it! You’re all set. From now on, whenever your report is run or updated, the data will automatically sync to the cloud database.

You can also trigger a manual run by selecting the "**Sync Current Snapshot**" action. It will start the sync for the selected snapshot.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F71ehXZBg64uqPopaJp4M%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-10.44.41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd8826ad-8fc3-4963-86e4-39aa09e74aad&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d0ec99cd&sv=2)

Trigger a manual sync for the selected snapshot.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#add-google-maps-api-key)

Add Google Maps API key

To display Google Maps in your shared report, you’ll need to add a **Google Maps API key**.

**Important:** You should use a different API key from the one you use in the SEO Utils app. This key will be public, so it’s important to restrict it to prevent unauthorized use.

1.  Please follow [this guide to enable the **Maps JavaScript API**](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/google-my-business-rank-tracker#setup-the-google-places-api)
    **.** If you have already enabled it in your project, you can just create a new API key (Step 8).
    
2.  After creating a new API key, please edit it:
    
    1.  Under **Application restrictions**, select **Websites**.
        
    2.  Add `share.seoutils.app` to the list.
        
    

If you use a [custom domain](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#custom-domain)
, you want to add that domain to the list as well.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FsbHBL3k4rTVdMT6t427Y%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-11.08.01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da26d6c24-21ff-4d54-b6dd-e50af806c3d2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69baff17&sv=2)

Add website restrictions.

1.  _(Optional but recommended)_ Under **API restrictions**, allow access to only the **Maps JavaScript API**. This setup ensures your API key is safe and only used for displaying maps in shared reports.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fb5dPO2jPMXrsieeHvZ6Q%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-11.12.01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45c5010b-360f-47a7-85da-34cf6480a083&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a32bfb&sv=2)

Only allow Maps Javascript API.

Last step, visit the **Settings** page on [https://share.seoutils.app/](https://share.seoutils.app/)
 and enter the created API key under the **Google Maps** section.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FQD9DekOFsXPAxVOuVaCe%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-11.21.36.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa7c3470-0e4c-4535-bc4e-5032374329a9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5092e4bf&sv=2)

Enter the created Google Maps API key.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#share-organic-rank-tracker-reports)

Share Organic Rank Tracker Reports

Coming soon...

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#embed-report)

Embed Report

To get the embed code:

1.  Visit [https://share.seoutils.app/](https://share.seoutils.app/)
     and edit the report you want to embed.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F2K2dVs1M43FVQQ9Dx6OR%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-10.49.56.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5146771f-71d0-40d2-bed2-abe4f2084a3d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46441ed9&sv=2)

Get the report embed code.

1.  _Optional:_ Choose the snapshot and keyword you’d like to display by default on initial load.
    
2.  Copy the generated embed code and paste it anywhere—your website, dashboard, or client portal.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FB4hQxS1nbpTzQIFWkuxp%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-10.51.04.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4487b7b1-38c1-4e61-8d44-3dd0c64af500&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5badf9a&sv=2)

Copy the embed code.

The embed code doesn't work if you enable the password protection for the report.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#add-your-custom-logo-and-company-website)

Add Your Custom Logo & Company Website

You can personalize your shared reports by adding your company logo and website. Just head over to the **Company Settings** page on [https://share.seoutils.app/](https://share.seoutils.app/)

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FujeRw97BlHgcoiB7ItFS%252FXnapper-2025-04-24-11.28.14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5c4327eb-aaf3-4619-8f97-5e7427063a7b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97dd09ef&sv=2)

Add your own logo and website URL.

SEO Utils will use your company logo and website URL for all shared reports by default. If you’d like to **customize the logo and website URL for a specific report**, simply edit that report and upload a custom logo or enter a different website URL.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/white-labeled-client-report#custom-domain)

Custom Domain
