# SMTP Credentials | SEO Utils

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#what-are-smtp-credentials)

What Are SMTP Credentials?

SMTP credentials allow SEO Utils to send automated emails through your email server. This is essential for automating report delivery to clients and team members.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#setting-up-smtp-credentials)

Setting Up SMTP Credentials

To configure email sending capabilities, navigate to **SMTP** in the left sidebar and click **Add Credential**.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FWb1VZ6TFPg6yPEIyP5MC%252FXnapper-2025-09-17-22.44.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe20851e-af2a-443f-9359-5a20815dc314&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=93215a1e&sv=2)

SMTP Credentials management interface

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#configuration-fields)

Configuration Fields

Fill in the following settings based on your email provider:

**Basic Settings:**

*   **Credential Name**: A friendly name to identify this configuration (e.g., "Main Gmail Account")
    
*   **Default Credential**: Toggle on to use this as the default for all email automations
    

**Server Settings:**

*   **SMTP Host**: Your email server address (see provider settings below)
    
*   **Port**: Usually `587` for TLS or `465` for SSL
    
*   **Encryption**: Select TLS/STARTTLS (recommended) or SSL
    

**Authentication:**

*   **Username**: Your email address or username
    
*   **Password**: Your email password or app-specific password
    

**Gmail Users**: You must use an [App Password](https://support.google.com/accounts/answer/185833)
 instead of your regular password. Enable 2-factor authentication first, then generate an app password.

**Sender Information:**

*   **From Email**: The email address that appears as sender
    
*   **From Name**: Optional display name (e.g., "SEO Reports")
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#testing-your-configuration)

Testing Your Configuration

Before saving, always test your SMTP settings:

1.  Enter a **Test Email Address** where you can receive mail
    
2.  Click **Send Test Email**
    
3.  Check your inbox for the test message
    
4.  If successful, click **Create Credential**
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FpJ0xnjdit7Ln7nytuIsS%252FXnapper-2025-09-17-22.51.23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9f01a72-51af-46bc-8af9-bcd6b8415ffa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c0375c27&sv=2)

Test your SMTP configuration before saving

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#common-email-provider-settings)

Common Email Provider Settings

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#gmail)

Gmail

*   Host: `smtp.gmail.com`
    
*   Port: `587`
    
*   Encryption: `TLS`
    
*   Username: Your Gmail address
    
*   Password: [App Password](https://myaccount.google.com/apppasswords)
     (not regular password)
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#microsoft-365-outlook)

Microsoft 365/Outlook

*   Host: `smtp.office365.com`
    
*   Port: `587`
    
*   Encryption: `TLS`
    
*   Username: Your email address
    
*   Password: Your password
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#sendgrid)

SendGrid

*   Host: `smtp.sendgrid.net`
    
*   Port: `587` (or `465` for SSL, `2525` as alternative)
    
*   Encryption: `TLS`
    
*   Username: `apikey` (literal string, not your username)
    
*   Password: Your SendGrid API key
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#mailgun)

Mailgun

*   Host: `smtp.mailgun.org`
    
*   Port: `587` (or `2525` as alternative)
    
*   Encryption: `TLS`
    
*   Username: Your Mailgun email address
    
*   Password: Your Mailgun API key
    

**Tip**: Port `2525` is an alternative port offered by SendGrid and Mailgun if your ISP blocks standard ports. It works identically to port 587 with TLS encryption.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#custom-business-email)

Custom/Business Email

Contact your IT administrator or hosting provider for:

*   SMTP server address
    
*   Port number
    
*   Authentication requirements
    
*   Encryption method
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#using-smtp-in-automations)

Using SMTP in Automations

Once configured, your SMTP credentials are automatically available in the Automations tool. When creating an email action, simply:

1.  Select **Send Email** as the action type
    
2.  The system will use your default SMTP credential
    
3.  Configure recipient, subject, and message content
    
4.  Add attachments using variables like `{{pdf_export_path}}`
    

See the [Automations guide](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations)
 for detailed examples of email automation workflows.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

**Test email fails:**

*   Verify your username and password are correct
    
*   For Gmail, ensure you're using an App Password
    
*   For SendGrid, use `apikey` as username (not your email)
    
*   Check if your email provider requires specific security settings
    
*   Try alternative ports (2525 for Mailgun/SendGrid if 587 is blocked)
    

**Emails not sending in automations:**

*   Confirm the SMTP credential is marked as default
    
*   Check automation execution logs for specific error messages
    
*   Verify recipient email addresses are valid
    

**Connection timeout:**

*   Your firewall or ISP may be blocking the SMTP port
    
*   Try port 2525 as an alternative for SendGrid/Mailgun
    
*   Try using port 465 with SSL encryption instead of 587/TLS
    

[PreviousAutomations](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations)
[NextPrivacy Policy](https://help.seoutils.app/legal/privacy-policy)

# Automations | SEO Utils

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#how-does-the-automations-tool-work)

How Does the Automations Tool Work?

SEO Utils allows you to automate actions when rank tracking completes. When an Organic Rank Tracker or Google Business Rank Tracker snapshot finishes, you can automatically export PDFs, send emails to clients, or trigger webhook URLs.

The automation system processes actions sequentially. If one action fails, subsequent actions that don't depend on its output will still run. Only actions requiring output from failed actions will be skipped.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#how-to-create-an-automation)

How to Create an Automation

To get started, head to Automations in the left sidebar. Then, click the Add Automation button.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FJ15Fpons5Q9miqTRpOal%252FXnapper-2025-09-18-10.53.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f5cb84c-6c3e-4151-a01b-f2afa1857a91&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=efada81c&sv=2)

Access the Automations tool in the left sidebar

The automation form has three steps:

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#step-1-basic-information)

Step 1: Basic Information

*   **Name**: Give your automation a descriptive name like "Send GMB Report to Client"
    
*   **Description**: Optional notes about what this automation does
    
*   **Active Status**: Toggle whether the automation should run
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#step-2-configure-trigger)

Step 2: Configure Trigger

Select when the automation should run:

*   **Trigger Type**: Choose between Organic Rank Tracker or GMB Rank Tracker completion
    
*   **Run On**: Select "All Reports" or choose specific reports
    
*   **Run Once**: Enable this to run the automation only once per report, preventing duplicate actions like sending multiple emails when re-running the tracker
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FMZTYlbmGo9Y0JBI8DDuG%252FXnapper-2025-09-18-10.53.52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D385dc845-7c6d-4c0e-ac01-dec277c4947c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ebaa4c2&sv=2)

Configure the trigger

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#step-3-define-actions)

Step 3: Define Actions

Add one or more actions that execute in sequence. Each action type has specific configuration options.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#using-variables-in-actions)

Using Variables in Actions

Variables allow you to use dynamic data from your rank tracking reports. Variables are wrapped in double curly braces `{{variable_name}}`.

Click the **Variables** button in any text field to search and insert variables quickly. You can search by typing keywords like "action 1" or "email" to find relevant variables.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FUk2GQvDhtMBrF7mzdVFl%252FXnapper-2025-09-18-10.54.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1876d6ac-5843-4d89-9d94-ec48d03dc219&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a13007de&sv=2)

Use Varaibles Selector button to quickly find and insert variables

**GMB Rank Tracker Trigger Variables:**

*   `{{trigger.reportID}}` - ID of the GMB rank tracker report
    
*   `{{trigger.reportType}}` - Type of report (google-business-rank-tracker)
    
*   `{{trigger.fromDate}}` - Date of the comparison snapshot (based on automation's comparison days setting)
    
*   `{{trigger.toDate}}` - Date of the current snapshot that triggered this automation
    
*   `{{trigger.ranOn}}` - Date when the snapshot was created
    
*   `{{trigger.snapshotID}}` - ID of the current snapshot
    
*   `{{trigger.businessName}}` - Business name being tracked
    
*   `{{trigger.address}}` - Business address
    
*   `{{trigger.comparisonDays}}` - Number of days between snapshots
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#example-gmb-report-email-automation)

Example: GMB Report Email Automation

Here's a practical template for automatically sending GMB ranking reports to clients:

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#action-1-export-pdf)

Action 1: Export PDF

*   **Action Type**: Export PDF
    
*   **Export Folder**: `/Users/yourname/Downloads` (or your preferred folder)
    

**Output Variables** (automatically available for next actions):

*   `exportDate` - Date when the file was exported
    
*   `exportTime` - Full timestamp of export
    
*   `fileName` - Name of the PDF file
    
*   `filePath` - Full path to the exported PDF file
    
*   `fileSize` - Size of the file in bytes
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#action-2-send-email)

Action 2: Send Email

*   **Action Type**: Send Email
    
*   **SMTP Credential**: Select your configured credential or leave empty for default
    
*   **Recipients**: `[[email protected]](https://help.seoutils.app/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) `
    
*   **CC Recipients**: _(optional)_
    
*   **Email Subject**: `GMB Rankings Report - {{trigger.businessName}} - {{trigger.ranOn}}`
    
*   **Email Body**:
    

Copy

    Hi,
    
    Your Google Business ranking report for {{trigger.businessName}} is ready.
    
    Comparison Period: {{trigger.fromDate}} to {{trigger.toDate}}
    Location: {{trigger.address}}
    
    The detailed report is attached to this email.
    
    Best regards,
    Your SEO Team

*   **Attachments**: Use the Variables button to insert the file path from Action 1. It will look like: `{{action.act_[actionId].filePath}}`
    

**Tip**: The action ID (like `act_1757983518769_inus10vs5`) is automatically generated when you create the action. Use the Variables button to easily insert the correct reference without typing it manually.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fgu2PD77Tz6bkY4NdTeG0%252FXnapper-2025-09-18-21.55.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8533e9d-57fe-41b0-b75d-1bb1b637e558&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8e97ac33&sv=2)

Configure multiple actions to run in sequence

**Important**: To send emails, you must first configure SMTP credentials. See [SMTP Credentials](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials)
 Setup for instructions.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#monitoring-automation-history)

Monitoring Automation History

The Automation detail page shows comprehensive execution history:

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#execution-statistics)

Execution Statistics

*   **Total Runs**: How many times the automation has triggered
    
*   **Successful/Failed/Partial**: Breakdown of execution results
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#execution-history-tab)

Execution History Tab

View each automation run with:

*   **Status**: Completed, Failed, or Partial (some actions failed)
    
*   **Duration**: How long the automation took
    
*   **Actions**: Number of actions executed
    
*   **Trigger Data**: The snapshot or report that triggered it
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FEwcO8swM2mxYwBysH2ix%252FXnapper-2025-09-18-21.56.23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e9afac6-c34c-4ffb-b09a-808969487a1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=455e41ba&sv=2)

Monitor automation execution history and retry failed actions

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#retrying-failed-automations)

Retrying Failed Automations

When an automation fails or partially completes, you have two retry options:

1.  Click the **vertical three dots** next to the execution
    
2.  Choose your retry method:
    
    *   **Retry All Actions**: Runs the entire automation from the beginning
        
    *   **Retry Failed & Cancelled Actions**: Only retries actions that failed or were cancelled
        
    
3.  The system will:
    
    *   For "Retry All": Execute all actions from the start
        
    *   For "Retry Failed & Cancelled": Skip completed actions and only retry failed/cancelled ones
        
    *   Use the **original trigger data** (not current automation settings)
        
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#execution-and-action-status-types)

Execution & Action Status Types

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#automation-execution-status)

Automation Execution Status

*   **Running**: Automation is currently executing
    
*   **Success**: All actions completed successfully
    
*   **Failed**: All actions failed
    
*   **Partial**: Some actions succeeded, others failed or cancelled
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/automations#individual-action-status)

Individual Action Status

*   **Running**: Action is currently executing
    
*   **Completed**: Action executed successfully
    
*   **Failed**: Action encountered an error
    
*   **Cancelled**: Action was stopped before completion

[NextSMTP Credentials](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/smtp-credentials)

# NLP Text Analysis | SEO Utils

Whether optimizing content for SEO, performing competitive research, uncovering hidden trends, or finding gaps in topics and entities, NLP Text Analysis provides the clarity and precision your workflow demands. Boost your efficiency and elevate your strategy with deep semantic insights at your fingertips.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis#supported-api-drivers)

Supported API Drivers

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis#id-1.-text-razor)

1\. Text Razor

Register for an account at [TextRazor](https://www.textrazor.com/signup)
.

TextRazor offers a free plan with up to 500 requests per day. The free tier includes full access to all features, allowing you to extract entities and topics effectively.

If you need more than 500 requests per day, please consider a paid plan at [TextRazor Plans](https://www.textrazor.com/plans)
.

After registering an account, you can obtain your API key at your [TextRazor Console](https://www.textrazor.com/console)
.

To enter the API key to SEO Utils, please visit the **Services** > **Natural Language Processing** page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FFstJ72LKtXAqdPrjwqcZ%252FXnapper-2025-03-12-09.49.14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee2f3bd8-2f92-4c52-8a58-e6551c7c5877&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a10aff2a&sv=2)

Add TextRazor API Key to SEO Utils

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis#id-2.-google-nlp)

2\. Google NLP

To use Google NLP, you must first enable the "**Cloud Natural Language API**" in your project.

Google NLP offers a free tier providing **5,000 units per month**, where each unit represents 1,000 characters processed. Additional usage beyond the free tier incurs minimal charges based on character count. For complete pricing details and calculations, visit [Google NLP Pricing](https://cloud.google.com/natural-language/pricing)
.

Visit [Google Cloud Console](https://console.cloud.google.com/)
 and search for "Cloud Natural Language API" in the top search bar.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FtT5polo4cC14nMeQV8os%252FXnapper-2025-03-12-10.06.21.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc40ad3a-d056-4347-8c50-3970c04a8e9e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b1f919e&sv=2)

Find the Cloud Natural Language API.

After enabling the API, go to the Credentials tab from the left sidebar. Click on the "Create Credentials" button and select "API Key."

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FfdHac6HMX5prTjTzBXn1%252FXnapper-2025-03-12-09.58.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D723ab457-2c12-4fc9-a20a-81db9c09cdca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=80216596&sv=2)

Create an API key.

If you already have an existing API key, you can use that instead.

Copy the API key from the pop-up window.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FgL8rRagC4Bc46GFSapAk%252FXnapper-2025-03-12-09.59.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d7051f5-4153-4e59-9b5a-8f20bed686e1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3ea9bfc2&sv=2)

Copy the API key.

You can edit the API key to add a name and restrict access. It is recommended to restrict the key to only allow access to the Cloud Natural Language API.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F3IfEdE36OuGUiRBeB6QJ%252FXnapper-2025-03-12-10.00.55.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07786ac7-2bec-42b9-ae14-96ddf86b129a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f1eebf55&sv=2)

Restrict API key.

To enter the API key to SEO Utils, please visit the **Services** > **Natural Language Processing** page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FZUY0lz3Cx7KljpWqaaBb%252FXnapper-2025-03-12-09.50.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3d4e478-0979-4e57-b462-3ff3ecb90dfe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cb795569&sv=2)

Enter the Google NLP API Key.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis#id-3.-dandelion)

3\. Dandelion

Register for an account at [Dandelion](https://dandelion.eu/accounts/register/)
.

Dandelion offers a free tier allowing up to 1,000 requests per day, approximately 30,000 requests per month.

Obtain your API key by visiting your [Dandelion Dashboard](https://dandelion.eu/profile/dashboard/)
.

For additional requests beyond the free tier, consider upgrading to a paid plan at [Dandelion Pricing](https://dandelion.eu/profile/plans-and-pricing/)
.

To enter the API key to SEO Utils, please visit the **Services** > **Natural Language Processing** page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F9pisLq8d2dQbQAG606hi%252FXnapper-2025-03-12-09.49.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2dbd4e4-70cd-43f1-b314-d8f3a28114bc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67de6d24&sv=2)

Enter Dandelion API Key to SEO Utils.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis#how-to-use-the-nlp-text-analysis-tool)

How to Use the NLP Text Analysis Tool

To access the NLP Text Analysis tool, navigate to **NLP > Text Analysis** in the left sidebar. Hit the "Run" button to perform a new analysis.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FsEfWgkyffsnQjI1FqN8P%252FXnapper-2025-03-12-10.26.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a502f2a-5f5d-475e-9ef3-b4aaf0e0da24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=74e25a42&sv=2)

Text Analysis tool

You can enter raw text, HTML, or multiple URLs into the provided input area.

Next, select your preferred API Driver and the language for analysis from the dropdown menus.

After the analysis process is finished, SEO Utils will provide three report pages: **Text Analysis**, **Entities**, **Topics**.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis#id-1.-text-analysis-tab)

1\. Text Analysis Tab

The **Text Analysis** tab breaks your content down sentence by sentence and highlights all detected entities. Simply hover over an entity to view its details!

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FYoR88oaKtVbjVE0nNGyk%252F482116189_9295668087169003_4889640696323789957_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D017f5e72-da0e-4fb6-a1ea-0a32529beecd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e190910&sv=2)

Text Analysis tab

Instead of scanning through large blocks of text, you get a clear, digestible view of the key topics, terms, and important concepts in every sentence. This makes it incredibly easy to refine your content, optimize for SEO, and ensure that your messaging is precise and impactful.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis#id-2.-entities-tab)

2\. Entities Tab

An **entity** is a meaningful word or phrase that represents a real-world concept, such as a person, place, object, event, or idea. Unlike simple keywords, entities have deeper meanings and are linked to other related concepts. This helps you understand not just what words appear in your content, but what they actually represent.

For example, if your text mentions “**New York**”, SEO Utils doesn’t just recognize it as a word but understands it as a city, which belongs to a larger category of locations. This deeper understanding helps you structure content better, and ensure search engines correctly interpret your topics. By detecting and categorizing entities, you can fine-tune your content, focus on the most important subjects, and make it more relevant to your audience.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F3Z7L4i5L6tOfZR8MoKHM%252FXnapper-2025-03-12-11.19.04.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98a0aa28-6cd2-48aa-a1c7-9a1765786261&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5852b378&sv=2)

Entities Tab

*   **Relevance Score:** Measures how strongly an entity relates to your content. A high score means the entity is central to the text.
    
*   **Confidence Score:** Measures how confident the API Driver is that the detected entity is correct. A higher score means the detection is more reliable.
    
*   **Mention Count:** Tracks how many times an entity appears in your content. A high count means the entity is frequently referenced.
    
*   **Types**: Categorizes entities based on their meaning, such as **Software**, **Person**, or **Location**. This helps you quickly understand what kind of concepts appear in your content.
    

Key difference between Relevance Score and Confidence Score:

Feature

Relevance Score

Confidence Score

Definition

Measures how relevant an entity is to the input text.

Measures how confident the API Driver is that the detected entity is correct.

What it Evaluates

Contextual similarity between the entity and the source text.

Probability that the detected entity is correct, based on multiple signals.

Use Case

Helps rank entities by importance in the text.

Helps filter out incorrect or uncertain entity detections.

Supported API Driver

[TextRazor](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis#id-1.-text-razor)
 only.

All API Drivers.

**Using Mention Count Toggle Button**

You can see how many times each entity appears in your content by clicking the toggle button on each entity row in the table.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FBVHVD1seE6FCgnq09uek%252F482348105_9301755739893571_7965608977519722321_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7aeeab75-58b8-4564-9a68-0aae463b8bb8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=18b20a2a&sv=2)

Mention Count Toggle Button

**Using Filters for Entity List**

1.  **Filter by Relevance Score** – Focus on the most important topics in your content.
    

*   **Use Case:** If you want to analyze core topics for SEO or research, filtering by high Relevance Score ensures you see only the most relevant entities. For example, if your article is about “_coffee brewing_”, terms like “_espresso_” and “_French press_” will have high relevance, while broader terms like “_beverages_” might be excluded.
    

1.  **Filter by Confidence Score** – Remove incorrect or uncertain entity detections.
    

*   **Use Case:** If you are analyzing a large text and need high-accuracy results, filtering by high Confidence Score ensures that only correctly detected entities are included. For example, if “_Apple_” appears in a tech article, a high confidence score ensures it refers to the company rather than the fruit.
    

1.  **Filter by Mention Count** – Identify the most frequently used entities.
    

*   **Use Case:** If you want to track dominant topics in your content, filtering by mentionCount helps you find terms that appear most often. This is useful for content structuring and topic clustering. For example, if “_climate change_” is mentioned 20 times in an article, but “_global warming_” only appears twice, you might focus on emphasizing “climate change” in your SEO strategy.
    

By adjusting these filters, you can fine-tune your entity analysis, whether you need **precise topic identification** (high relevance), **accurate entity detection** (high confidence), or **frequently mentioned topics** (high mention count). 🚀

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis#id-3.-topics-tab)

3\. Topics Tab

Only [TextRazor](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/nlp-text-analysis#id-1.-text-razor)
 supports topic extraction, so you can only see the Topics tab when using that API driver.

A **topic** is a broad subject or theme that your content discusses. Topics provide a high-level understanding of what your text is about, grouping related concepts under general categories like Business, Science, or Technology. Unlike entities, which represent specific names or objects, topics capture the overall theme of your content, helping you see its main focus at a glance.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FH0MweMvk6hqgDNVUkyBW%252FXnapper-2025-03-12-11.52.37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3dac7f8e-d090-4a91-9caf-cb65bb039e2f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=53ccc4d8&sv=2)

Topics Tab

*   **Score:** Measures how relevant a topic is to the input text. The higher the score, the more relevant the topic is. Score ranges from 0 to 1.
    
*   **Coarse Topics:** General categories.
    

**Key Differences Between Topics and Entities**

Feature

Topics

Entities

Definition

General themes or subject categories

Specific real-world objects, names, or concepts

Purpose

Helps categorize content and understand its broad focus

Identifies key terms and their semantic meaning

Examples

_Business, Science, Mathematics_

_New York, Tesla, Python (programming language)_

Granularity

High-level classification

Detailed and specific references

While **entities tell you exactly what appears in the text, topics help you see the bigger picture**, making it easier to categorize, summarize, and optimize your content for relevance and clarity.

**Key Differences Between Topics and Coarse Topics**

Feature

Topics (Fine-grained)

Coarse Topics (Broad)

Granularity

More specific topics

General categories

Example

Google Search

Technology

Use Case

Detailed topic extraction

Broad text classification

**Use Cases for the Topics Tab**

1.  **Content Categorization & Relevance**
    

*   Use Case: Ensure your content aligns with your target niche.
    
*   Example: If you’re writing about “_eCommerce trends_,” but the detected topics are **Business** and **Marketing**, it confirms your content is on track. However, if unrelated topics like **Mathematics** or **Arts** appear, you might need to adjust your content focus.
    

1.  **Topic Gap Analysis**
    

*   Use Case: Compare your content topics against competitor content to find missing areas.
    
*   Example: If competitors covering “_email marketing_” are categorized under **Digital Marketing**, but your article only shows **Business**, you may need to add more relevant details to strengthen topic alignment.
    

1.  **Improving Search Intent Matching**
    

*   Use Case: Make sure your content aligns with what search engines expect for a given keyword.
    
*   Example: If you’re targeting “_AI in healthcare_,” but your topics only show **Technology**, adding more medical references can help trigger **Health & Medicine** topics for better search relevance.
    

1.  **Optimizing Internal Linking & Topic Clusters**
    

*   Use Case: Identify content clusters for better internal linking.
    
*   Example: If multiple articles on your site are categorized under **Web Development**, you can interlink them to create a **stronger topical authority** on that subject.
    

1.  **Structuring Content for Featured Snippets**
    

*   Use Case: Improve content structure by ensuring clear topic coverage.
    
*   Example: If your article about “_Best SEO Practices_” is categorized under **Business** but lacks SEO or **Digital Marketing**, adding a structured section with on-page, off-page, and technical SEO could improve your chances of ranking in Google’s featured snippets.
    

By leveraging topic detection, you can ensure **better content alignment, improve topical authority, and optimize your content for higher rankings in search results**. 🚀

# Bulk SEO Metadata Optimizer | SEO Utils

The **Bulk SEO Metadata Optimizer** in SEO Utils allows you to optimize **titles, meta descriptions, and H1 headings** across multiple pages using AI. This tool is perfect for SEOs looking to save time while enhancing metadata for better search engine visibility and click-through rates.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fujpl4k5lG0ELiS8MVlt8%252FXnapper-2024-12-15-22.25.10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da96b02ce-e04d-40eb-953a-820f578c8309&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=32f3e174&sv=2)

Bulk SEO Metadata Optimizer tool

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#start-your-first-run-with-the-bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer)

Start Your First Run with the Bulk SEO Metadata Optimizer

To get started, open SEO Utils. On the left-hand sidebar, navigate to the **Utilities** section and click on **Bulk Metadata Optimizer**. This will open the dashboard where you can manage your previous reports or create a new one.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FI1loSb0jVTtXsnCvHoft%252FXnapper-2024-12-15-22.26.00.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e9aea79-b2fc-4bb9-b40b-fec011490173&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=982edac0&sv=2)

The tool is under Ultiltes menu

To create a new optimization report, click the **Run** button located at the top-right corner of the screen. This will open the **Run Form**, where you can configure your optimization settings.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F1oWwNpBKmkS1DIMhU17Y%252FXnapper-2024-12-15-22.28.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e1b2096-c3a5-46ed-a0f2-c7cbc1df0270&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=45f6a3f3&sv=2)

Click the "Run" button to start a new run.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#add-urls-for-optimization)

**Add URLs for Optimization**

In the **Run Form**, you’ll see a text box labeled **Enter URLs (one per line)**. Here, you can paste the list of pages you want to optimize. Each URL must be on a separate line.

If you want to optimize all pages under a specific path, you can use the **wildcard (\*)** character. For example:

*   Entering `https://example.com/blog/*` will scrape and optimize all pages under the `/blog/` path.
    
*   Entering `https://example.com/category/content/*` will target every page under `/category/content/`.
    
*   If you enter a specific page like `https://example.com/page-1`, only that exact page will be optimized.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FpLngDKKyGvuNtXZ9qaeO%252F470205909_8818212598247890_4358969561379193977_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddac662de-9f39-44db-afdb-e14c6b39dd68&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e1294115&sv=2)

Use wilcard (\*) to quickly import URLs

The wildcard feature is extremely useful for bulk optimization, saving you the hassle of manually adding every single URL.

You must **install Google Chrome** on your computer to use the wildcard feature.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#choose-the-ai-model)

**Choose the AI Model**

The next step is to select the AI model that will generate the optimized metadata. SEO Utils supports multiple AI providers, so you can choose the one that best suits your needs.

*   **OpenAI:** You can choose models like GPT-4o, GPT-4o Mini, and more. Get an API key at [https://platform.openai.com/settings/organization/api-keys](https://platform.openai.com/settings/organization/api-keys)
    
*   **Anthropic**: You can use Claude models like Claude 3.5 Sonnet or Claude 3 Ocpus by getting your API key at [https://console.anthropic.com/dashboard](https://console.anthropic.com/dashboard)
    
*   **OpenRouter**: This platform gives you access to around 281 different AI models, providing plenty of options. Register an account at [https://openrouter.ai/](https://openrouter.ai/)
    

You can access the list of models from OpenRouter at [https://openrouter.ai/models](https://openrouter.ai/models)

Once you have the API keys, go to the Services settings to enter them. You don’t need to enter all the keys—just input the one for the provider you want to use.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FVIExd7JB8Fbqn7iUDbJJ%252FXnapper-2024-12-15-22.42.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ae5db3c-4221-4efc-88a0-5803e2b7b6eb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b59974ce&sv=2)

Enter LLM Provider API keys

*   **Local Models via Ollama**: If you prefer not to rely on **cloud APIs**, you can use local models like _Mistral_ for **FREE**. To set up Ollama:
    
    1.  Download and install Ollama from [https://ollama.com](https://ollama.com/)
        .
        
    2.  Open the **Terminal** app on your computer and run the command `ollama pull mistral` to download the model. Ensure your PC meets the requirements specified for the model. For example, Mistral requires at least 16GB of RAM.
        
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252Fzi7ScKYMDqLmPKDkj1q7%252FCleanShot%25202024-12-15%2520at%252022.36.09%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02db8797-4425-47d7-b759-747487aec6a7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=219985fe&sv=2)

Run the command from your Terminal app to download Ollama models.

You don’t need an API key to use local models from Ollma. Just keep the Ollama app open, and SEO Utils will find and display all the downloaded models in the dropdown.

Using local models is cost-effective, but keep in mind they require strong hardware to run efficiently. You can access the list of models at [https://ollama.com/search](https://ollama.com/search)

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#customize-advanced-settings)

**Customize Advanced Settings**

Below the AI model selection, there is an option to **Toggle Advanced Settings**. Clicking this will reveal additional customization options to fine-tune the optimization process.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FTHCOOM2hzVOKxbxhHosl%252FXnapper-2024-12-15-22.58.52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc821be2e-c3b5-4493-9f2e-37570b057e45&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=da94de34&sv=2)

Advance settings

In the **Instruction** field, you can provide a clear instruction for the AI to follow. For example, you might write:

> "You are an SEO expert tasked with improving metadata. Write engaging meta titles, descriptions, and headings that include target keywords and improve click-through rates."

The **Prompt** field is where you can provide SEO metadata that you want to improve using placeholders.

Placeholders are special tags that SEO Utils will automatically replace with the actual content when scraping data from each URL. Here is a breakdown of available placeholders:

*   `[title]`: This will be replaced with the page title scraped from the URL.
    
*   `[meta_description]`: This will be replaced with the meta description found on the page.
    
*   `[heading_1]`: This will be replaced with the main H1 heading of the page.
    
*   `[content:50]`: This will include the first 50 words of the page content, and you can edit the number to include any amount of words you prefer, such as 100 or 200 words.
    

For example, you can define the prompt as follows:

Copy

    Title: [title]
    Meta Description: [meta_description]
    Heading 1: [heading_1]
    Content Preview: [content:50]

With this setup, SEO Utils will scrape the page content for each URL, replace the placeholders with the corresponding values, and send them to the AI for optimization.

Keep the **Instruction** and **Prompt** fields empty if you want to use the default value that SEO Utils provides.

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#start-the-optimization)

**Start the Optimization**

Once you’ve entered your URLs, selected the AI model, and customized the advanced settings, you’re ready to start the optimization process. Click the **Optimize SEO Metadata** button at the bottom of the form.

SEO Utils will process all the URLs and send the scraped data to the selected AI model. Depending on the number of URLs and the model chosen, the optimization may take a few moments to complete.

After the optimization is complete, you will be redirected to the **Report Detail Page** where you can review the results.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#review-the-results)

Review the Results

The Report Detail Page provides a clear view of the optimized metadata generated for each URL. For every URL, you can see the **original version** alongside the **improved version** generated by the AI.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FIS2O5udPEPEJcjh9JmZl%252FCleanShot%25202024-12-15%2520at%252023.01.11%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d0b498a-ff37-4d16-9bab-6df58169d949&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2726a314&sv=2)

Preview changes of each URL

Changes are highlighted for easy comparison:

*   **Green**: New content that has been added.
    
*   **Red**: Content that has been removed.
    

If you want to make manual adjustments to any metadata, simply click the **pencil icon** beside the corresponding field. This will allow you to edit the title, meta description, or H1 heading directly.

To modify additional aspects of the optimization, switch to the **Main Content** tab. Here, you can edit the extracted content from the page. If you need to adjust the AI instructions or prompt message for a specific URL, switch to the **Messages** tab. This lets you refine the instructions or prompt to better suit your needs, and placeholders can still be used here for consistency.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FEmJO42zUpTubURdHvbAR%252FXnapper-2024-12-15-23.02.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D945dfb98-acdf-43b2-8284-c709a48d0f00&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b03d776d&sv=2)

Edit data if needed

After making changes, you can re-optimize the URL by selecting it and clicking the **Re-optimize** button.

**Tip:** You can make small edits to the **Improved version** before [publishing changes](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#publish-changes-to-your-website)
 by clicking the pencil icon next to it.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#publish-changes-to-your-website)

Publish Changes to Your Website

SEO Utils makes it easy to publish the optimized metadata directly to your website through **Site Integrations**.

SEO Utils currently support integration with WordPress. More integrations, such as Shopify, Webflow, and custom platforms, will be added gradually soon.

To connect your website:

1.  Go to the **Settings** section in the sidebar and select **Site Integrations**.
    
2.  Click **Add Integration** and enter the following details:
    
    *   **Site URL**: The URL of your WordPress site.
        
    *   **Platform**: Select WordPress.
        
    *   **Username** and **App Password**: These can be generated in WordPress.
        
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FRc2sqJKNbzL8AivscLtp%252FXnapper-2024-12-15-23.13.54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22d6605d-4b3b-41fc-8c00-2a1a31a08261&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=827618b9&sv=2)

Access Site Integrations

To generate an App Password in WordPress:

1.  Go to your WordPress dashboard.
    
2.  Navigate to **Users > Profile**.
    
3.  Edit a user who has permission to edit posts or pages. If you're unsure, just choose the admin user.
    
4.  Scroll down to the **Application Passwords** section.
    
5.  Generate a new password and copy it.
    
6.  Paste the application password & username into the SEO Utils integration form.
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FnQjDLf8Mz7MD9RIKERzZ%252FCleanShot%25202024-12-17%2520at%252013.04.22%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bac6503-f752-4a4b-9e1e-78c4fc048710&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=74f8aa0c&sv=2)

Make sure you copy the correct username.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FH4Cbq4phoF0iHpYutns8%252FXnapper-2024-12-15-23.19.22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5ad95da-73d2-4f0c-bf0a-5737d69984b1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba5c1d95&sv=2)

Create an app password

SEO Utils will use this application password to change metadata on your website using the SEO Utils WordPress plugin (please install it below).

This application password is **NOT the same as the password** you use to log into your WordPress dashboard, and you can revoke it anytime you need.

**Install SEO Utils WordPress plugin**

This plugin will provide a REST API endpoint that lets the SEO Utils app send a request to your website to update metadata.

Please [download it](https://larseov2.s3.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/seo-utils/site-integrations/seo-utils.zip)
 and install it as a normal WordPress plugin.

**Note**: To update metadata, ensure you have one of the following SEO plugins installed on your WordPress site:

*   Yoast SEO
    
*   Rank Math
    
*   All-in-One SEO Pack
    
*   SEOPress
    
*   Slim SEO
    
*   Squirrly SEO
    

If these plugins are not installed, only the H1 heading can be updated, as it is part of the WordPress core content.

After connecting your site, return to the [**Report Detail Page**](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#review-the-results)
. Click the pencil icon, and you will see a dropdown to select your connected site.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FrC2LkL9Qd7wG9hM5iAYw%252FCleanShot%25202024-12-15%2520at%252023.27.23%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc703e8ac-b945-4614-adda-1b27f1ae53bc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef404057&sv=2)

Edit the report to select the added site integration from the previous step.

Once the site is selected, a **Publish** button will appear.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FqSFlYDhMbDMCFV5EBnMg%252FXnapper-2024-12-15-23.28.35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De67cd9b1-536b-41d0-8f64-b9e911f01fc9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=257b9e00&sv=2)

The "Publish" button appears after connecting to your site.

You can publish the following fields:

*   Meta Title
    
*   Meta Description
    
*   H1 Heading
    

Before publishing, always back up your data to avoid any unintended changes.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#bulk-actions)

Bulk Actions

You can select multiple URLs and bulk publish or re-optimize them at once.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FFQwlIFSvHEfD9Get0MBl%252FXnapper-2024-12-15-23.35.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc341a5c6-aa7e-4908-9478-ffb131d2772a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a0d6c709&sv=2)

Bulk Publish URLs

While the bulk action is running, you can view the log in the Log Panel at the bottom of the page.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#export-the-report)

Export the Report

If you need to save the results for further analysis or reporting, SEO Utils allows you to export the optimized metadata. On the [Report Detail Page](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/bulk-seo-metadata-optimizer#review-the-results)
, click the **Export** button at the top-right corner.

# Organic Rank Tracker | SEO Utils

The Organic Rank Tracker Dashboard provides a centralized view of all your rank tracking reports, allowing you to monitor performance across multiple domains, devices, and locations from a single screen.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FNmfuFGvHxiGA0oNLAsBz%252F502698006_9868867933182346_6566893985095021518_n.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44bdce71-3c6b-4ec7-b3ef-116097f3af5a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a4cb3472&sv=2)

Organic Rank Tracker Dashboard

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#accessing-the-dashboard)

Accessing the Dashboard


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#via-the-left-sidebar-menu)

Via the Left Sidebar Menu

1.  Look for the **Dashboard** section in the left sidebar
    
2.  Click on **Organic Rank Tracker** under the Dashboard menu
    
3.  The dashboard will load showing all your rank tracking reports
    

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FjXop7xogoNyoe1WQtnve%252FXnapper-2025-05-30-10.27.25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe9addd1-9bc7-4f1f-8235-3c7fd6863adc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3bb35b8&sv=2)

Access the Organic Rank Tracker Dashboard from the left sidebar

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#via-the-reports-page)

Via the Reports Page

You can also access the dashboard from the [Organic Rank Tracker Reports](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/organic-rank-tracker)
 page by clicking the **Dashboard** button in the top right corner.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#understanding-the-dashboard-layout)

Understanding the Dashboard Layout


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#date-range-filter)

Date Range Filter

At the top of the dashboard, you'll find the date range filter. This filter controls the time period for all data displayed on the page.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FVNFaXucuUPToXRk1pmZl%252FXnapper-2025-05-30-10.29.15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4568dfb6-4fc4-4117-baa2-d52f25e4c21c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7d534937&sv=2)

Date range filter with preset options

**Preset Options Available:**

*   Past 2 days
    
*   Past 7 days
    
*   Past 30 days
    
*   Past 60 days
    
*   Past 90 days
    
*   Previous Month
    
*   All Time
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#average-position-chart)

Average Position Chart

The chart displays average position trends for all your tracked domains. This powerful visualization helps you spot trends across your entire portfolio at a glance.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FABBpPmQfcOsvIIKwhqLF%252FCleanShot%25202025-05-30%2520at%252010.29.56%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47e61b3c-9961-42aa-bd58-79db2c1ac17a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=deb1ba6f&sv=2)

Average position trends consolidated by domain

**How the Chart Works:**

*   **Each line represents one domain** - If you track the same domain across multiple locations or devices, they're combined into a single line
    
*   **Automatic averaging** - When you have multiple reports for one domain (e.g., tracking in US, UK, and Canada), the chart shows the average position across all locations
    
*   **Lower is better** - The Y-axis shows positions, where position 1 is the best
    
*   **Interactive tooltips** - Hover over any point to see exact positions and dates
    

**Example**: If you track "example.com" in 3 different cities, the chart shows one line representing the average performance across all 3 locations, giving you a unified view of your domain's performance.

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#reports-by-domain)

Reports by Domain

The dashboard intelligently groups your reports by domain, making it easy to monitor performance across different configurations.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FsnonxwZwvRNkVzj90H7t%252FXnapper-2025-05-30-10.31.20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb50752c-749a-4b7c-8f3b-e724ff572501&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fdd64c46&sv=2)

Reports grouped by domain for easy comparison

**Benefits of Domain Grouping:**

*   **Compare device performance** - See how your mobile vs desktop rankings differ
    
*   **Monitor multiple locations** - Track performance across different countries or cities
    
*   **Unified domain view** - All reports for a domain are visually grouped together
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#domain-search)

Domain Search

Quickly find specific domains using the search bar. This is especially helpful when managing many domains.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FtaWvDjpJ2wqeuwg4xN8h%252FXnapper-2025-05-30-10.33.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D915c050c-8c81-428b-b3f1-2c647d859bed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8e6db65&sv=2)

Filter reports by domain name

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#understanding-report-cards)

Understanding Report Cards


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each report is displayed as a card containing comprehensive ranking data and metrics.

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252F5bI6TFtNZyIAYRz8owCn%252FXnapper-2025-05-30-10.35.00.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33319d79-d509-4cf6-9269-e9022e07716f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2957f4df&sv=2)

Report card

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#card-header)

Card Header

The card header displays:

*   **Domain name** (e.g., laravel.com)
    
*   **Actual comparison dates** (e.g., Feb 20, 2025 → May 29, 2025)
    
*   **Report configuration**: Device type, search engine, location, and language
    
*   **View Report button** to access the full report details
    

**Important: Closest Available Dates**

The dates shown in the card header (next to the View Report button) are the actual dates being compared, which may differ from your selected date range. The system automatically finds the closest available snapshot dates for each report.

For example:

*   You select: May 25-29, 2025
    
*   Report only has data for: Feb 20 and May 29, 2025
    
*   Dashboard shows: Feb 20 → May 29 comparison
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#metrics-section-left-side)

Metrics Section (Left Side)

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FCAGFN29UjknGF3VgoAQj%252FXnapper-2025-05-30-10.35.48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05deeb58-9a64-411b-8c61-265c0ff52e1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ac3cccc5&sv=2)

Metric section

The left side of each card displays position distribution metrics:

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#position-rankings)

Position Rankings

*   **Top 3**: Keywords ranking in positions 1-3
    
*   **Top 10**: Keywords ranking in positions 1-10
    
*   **Top 20**: Keywords ranking in positions 1-20
    
*   **Top 100**: Keywords ranking in positions 1-100
    

Each metric shows:

*   Previous count → Current count
    
*   Change indicator (↑ increase, ↓ decrease)
    
*   Net change value in parentheses
    

#### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#overall-changes)

Overall Changes

Below the position rankings, you'll find the overall change summary:

*   🟢 **New**: Keywords that started ranking (weren't ranking before)
    
*   🔵 **Improved**: Keywords that improved their positions
    
*   🔴 **Lost**: Keywords that stopped ranking (were ranking before)
    
*   🟠 **Declined**: Keywords that dropped in positions
    
*   ⚪ **Unchanged**: Keywords that maintained their positions
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#keywords-table-right-side)

Keywords Table (Right Side)

![](https://help.seoutils.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1176579443-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2DwV6sJBiKjUHMDggb4d%252Fuploads%252FDmev13Loxv20DOPwtZug%252FXnapper-2025-05-30-10.35.58.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfded02e1-e9a6-4396-9890-d2781795e50e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1efb5d84&sv=2)

Top 10 performing keywords

The right side displays the top 10 performing keywords with:

*   **Keyword**: The tracked keyword
    
*   **Position columns**: Shows positions for both comparison dates
    
*   **Diff**: Position change (positive = improvement, negative = decline)
    
*   **Volume**: Monthly search volume
    
*   **KD**: Keyword difficulty score
    
*   **CPC**: Cost per click value
    

**Keyword Sorting**

Keywords are sorted by best current position, with search volume as a secondary sort to ensure consistent ordering when multiple keywords have the same position.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#important-notes)

Important Notes


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#understanding-domain-grouping)

Understanding Domain Grouping

The dashboard makes it easy to manage multiple reports for the same domain:

*   **Visual grouping** - All reports for a domain appear together under a domain header
    
*   **Separate cards** - Each configuration (device/location) gets its own card for detailed analysis
    
*   **Combined chart data** - The average position chart intelligently combines all reports for a domain into one line
    

**Perfect for Multi-Location Tracking**: If you track "mysite.com" for New York, Los Angeles, and Chicago, you'll see:

*   3 separate cards showing detailed metrics for each city
    
*   1 line in the chart showing the overall average performance
    
*   All 3 cards grouped together under "mysite.com" for easy comparison
    

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#common-use-cases)

Common Use Cases


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**1\. Quick Performance Overview** Use the dashboard to get a bird's-eye view of how all your tracked domains are performing without opening individual reports.

**2\. Identify Trends** The average position chart helps you spot overall trends across your portfolio of tracked domains.

**3\. Spot Issues Quickly** The change metrics (New, Improved, Lost, Declined) help you quickly identify domains that need attention.

**4\. Compare Time Periods** Use the date filter to compare different time periods and understand how your rankings have evolved.

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#tips-for-best-results)

Tips for Best Results


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#monitoring-multiple-locations)

Monitoring Multiple Locations

When tracking the same domain across different locations:

*   Each location gets its own detailed card
    
*   The chart combines all locations to show overall trend
    
*   Use this to identify which locations perform best
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#device-comparison)

Device Comparison

Track both mobile and desktop for comprehensive insights:

*   Quickly spot mobile vs desktop ranking differences
    
*   Identify device-specific SEO opportunities
    
*   All device data for a domain stays grouped together
    

### 

[](https://help.seoutils.app/guide/dashboard/organic-rank-tracker#using-date-comparisons)

Using Date Comparisons

The dates shown next to "View Report" button are the actual dates being compared:

*   These may differ from your selected range if exact dates aren't available
    
*   The system automatically finds the closest available data
    
*   All metrics in the card use these same dates for accuracy
    

**No data showing?** Check if the report has tracking data within your selected date range. The system needs at least two different dates with data to show comparisons.
